
-----title
山东 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='453a071fe2f6450a8e6d0890c2716698_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("453a071fe2f6450a8e6d0890c2716698");'><span id='453a071fe2f6450a8e6d0890c2716698_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1098')">1083-1098年</a>，1-16岁</div><div id='453a071fe2f6450a8e6d0890c2716698' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　是年出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1091')">1084-1091年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　居乡，颖迈，已能作诗属文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1098')">1093-1098年</a><br /></div>

-----title
开封（祥符）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b24427c6ced54a24a7b1d95e246d8bdc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b24427c6ced54a24a7b1d95e246d8bdc");'><span id='b24427c6ced54a24a7b1d95e246d8bdc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1118')">1117-1118年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='b24427c6ced54a24a7b1d95e246d8bdc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　是年冬，赴京应礼部试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在汴京，上舍释褐，有文，调淄州淄县簿。作品：《及第谢乡郡守倅启》<div id='poem_1229699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>及第谢乡郡守倅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229699")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229699'>逐队而趋，愧匪处囊之颖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229699_comment'></div>缀行以出，亦陪入彀之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229699_comment'></div>仰被恩荣，伏深战惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229699_comment'></div>惟圣世之先务，以得人为最难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229699_comment'></div>素养弗加，成材斯寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229699_comment'></div>委楩楠而莫植，孰观在沚之菁菁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229699_comment'></div>舍騄骥而不闲，讵睹食场之皎皎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229699_comment'></div>道有升降，时因盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229699_comment'></div>泮水不歌，子衿是作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229699_comment'></div>遂使成周之里选，流为近世之科名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229699_comment'></div>天佑斯文，运开列考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229699_comment'></div>本六经而造士，建三舍以成能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229699_comment'></div>训迪一新，尽黜雕虫之陋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229699_comment'></div>指归有在，谁誇绣帨之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229699_comment'></div>渊源既纯，器质咸美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229699_comment'></div>顾今日庙堂之老，皆当时庠序之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229699_comment'></div>迨嗣圣之膺图，伏先猷而燕翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229699_comment'></div>丕崇子构，有隆不拔之基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229699_comment'></div>恢广文声，增耀无前之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229699_comment'></div>干戈载戢，礼乐并兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229699_comment'></div>爰更取士之科，大阐育材之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229699_comment'></div>扫千年之弊习，追三代之宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229699_comment'></div>简秀彦于一乡，采芹在泮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229699_comment'></div>收英豪于万国，振鹭飞雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229699_comment'></div>神化诞孚，士风丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229699_comment'></div>耆龆胥劝，弦诵相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229699_comment'></div>贤关来鼓箧之游，农野无带经之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229699_comment'></div>云汉每瞻于圣作，范模兼得于师儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229699_comment'></div>五尺之童，羞道桓文之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229699_comment'></div>一介之贱，愿归尧舜之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229699_comment'></div>既由学以化民，可因言而顾行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229699_comment'></div>文皆尔雅，孰非体要之辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229699_comment'></div>仕必慕君，自许功名之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229699_comment'></div>翘翘竞秀，蔼蔼争驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229699_comment'></div>仰繄乐育之风，克底美成之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229699_comment'></div>属三年之大比，率多士以同升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229699_comment'></div>宾兴已尽于贤能，辩论更先于俊造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229699_comment'></div>虽人人抱玉，未免于遗珍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229699_comment'></div>而一一吹竽，岂容于滥奏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229699_comment'></div>顾此誉髦之选，宜登杰异之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229699_comment'></div>如某者，学术不优，性质甚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229699_comment'></div>徒守箕裘之业，仅闻诗礼之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229699_comment'></div>幸遘昌期，久濡善教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229699_comment'></div>三充方贡，两冠贤书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229699_comment'></div>倦翼何堪，望绝一飞之便；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229699_comment'></div>曲材无取，谁为万乘之容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229699_comment'></div>方蹑屩以观光，遂操觚而试艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229699_comment'></div>中非尔力，命岂人为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229699_comment'></div>偶叨兰省之奏篇，获与枫宸之赐策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229699_comment'></div>宸章深灏，迈典诰之遗文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229699_comment'></div>圣问渊微，究天人之妙蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229699_comment'></div>岂彼腐儒之论，可当睿鉴之求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229699_comment'></div>显黜是虞，明扬忽逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229699_comment'></div>簉鸳鹭而并进，罗凫鹜以前趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229699_comment'></div>交戟森森，恍再游于帝所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229699_comment'></div>睟容穆穆，惊并近于天光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229699_comment'></div>传丹陛以宣恩，曳青纶而拜命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229699_comment'></div>名联帝子，共誇金榜之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229699_comment'></div>喜动亲颜，更乐萱堂之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229699_comment'></div>布韦歆艳，闾巷咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229699_comment'></div>夫何千载之逢，有此一时之幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229699_comment'></div>静言侥冒，厥有夤缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229699_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官黼黻帝庭，甄陶士类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229699_comment'></div>不屑之教，曲尽于平时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229699_comment'></div>有味之言，阴为于道地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229699_comment'></div>俯怜衰踬，力赐提携。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229699_comment'></div>会因乡党之同推，更与郡侯而劝驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229699_comment'></div>遂容蹇步，亦陟亨途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229699_comment'></div>某谨当恪守士规，寖娴吏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229699_comment'></div>幸保一经之遗子，更希三釜之及亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229699_comment'></div>学于田野之间，粗知为政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229699_comment'></div>服在缙绅之后，敢怠修身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229699_comment'></div>勉效古人，用酬知己。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1229699_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='de0a6ee699b540b9bf92e6ff02228fd9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("de0a6ee699b540b9bf92e6ff02228fd9");'><span id='de0a6ee699b540b9bf92e6ff02228fd9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1124')">1121-1124年</a>，39-42岁</div><div id='de0a6ee699b540b9bf92e6ff02228fd9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在汴京，行太学正。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在汴京，次女出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在汴京，有文。作品：《代宰执贺顺州进枸杞表》<div id='poem_1229635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰执贺顺州进枸杞表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229635")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229635'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229635'>灵根夜吠，变异质于千年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229635_comment'></div>驿骑朝驰，荐圣人之万寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229635_comment'></div>眷荒裔沉藏之久，实王师恢复之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229635_comment'></div>物岂无知，时如有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229635_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>臣闻神仙不可以学得，至道不可以情求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229635_comment'></div>访云海之三山，殆为虚语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229635_comment'></div>候金丹之九转，安睹成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229635_comment'></div>与其捕影以徒劳，孰若清心而自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229635_comment'></div>惟养生之上药，著却老之嘉名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229635_comment'></div>夙标农帝之书，杂见道家之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229635_comment'></div>验西河之遗法，盖推服饵之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229635_comment'></div>询南丘之故封，厥有延长之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229635_comment'></div>能致飞仙之变化，更传伏狗之精英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229635_comment'></div>方士搜奇，叹穷年而未遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229635_comment'></div>边臣效异，得具体以来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229635_comment'></div>疑彼舐鼎之留形，宛若结刍而取象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229635_comment'></div>天心垂佑，上符所属之辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229635_comment'></div>地宝储休，下见始开之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229635_comment'></div>帝龄兆永，国祚增隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229635_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下体妙希夷，凝神昭旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229635_comment'></div>四海觌亨嘉之会，群生跻仁寿之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229635_comment'></div>城彼朔方，允合天人之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229635_comment'></div>震于珍物，是兴草木之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229635_comment'></div>式彰辟国之符，益衍后天之算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229635_comment'></div>遗一丸而生羽翼，笑魏君誇诞之词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229635_comment'></div>名百物而垂衣裳，协帝祖神灵之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229635_comment'></div>事光简策，欢动搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229635_comment'></div>臣等佐治无功，逢辰有幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229635_comment'></div>数北州之贡，既观寿物之奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229635_comment'></div>占南极之躔，伫奏老人之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229635_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1229635_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年8月1日</a>　在汴京，八月一日有文。作品：《代宰执贺八月一日阴云不见日食表》<div id='poem_1229644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰执贺八月一日阴云不见日蚀表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229644")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229644'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229644'>太史献占，日在当亏之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229644_comment'></div>圣人修德，天垂纯祐之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229644_comment'></div>有来云物之祥，莫睹阳精之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229644_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>窃以天神相远，匪声臭之能求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229644_comment'></div>历象有明，乃躔离之可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229644_comment'></div>维盈缩或违其常度，则推占因著于繁文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229644_comment'></div>虽日有食之，何系灾祥之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229644_comment'></div>而分同道也，初非次舍之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229644_comment'></div>赫彼众阳之宗，炳为群目之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229644_comment'></div>拂扶桑而出旸谷，岂阴慝之能干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229644_comment'></div>坐明堂而正天纲，知圣功之默运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229644_comment'></div>交居朔日，时当仲秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229644_comment'></div>仰大明之方升，蔼微阴之徐覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229644_comment'></div>霞舒雾集，讵观如月之初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229644_comment'></div>气霁烟销，还照普天之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229644_comment'></div>事光载籍，喜溢寰区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229644_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下道并尧明，功高汤圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229644_comment'></div>在璿玑而齐七政，调玉烛而行四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229644_comment'></div>德上昭天，允格太和之应；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229644_comment'></div>日不食朔，是谓太平之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229644_comment'></div>亶兹难致之休，若有固然之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229644_comment'></div>神心不测，妙用孰窥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229644_comment'></div>臣等叨备近司，获逢盛旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229644_comment'></div>修六官之治，顾敢怠于钦承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229644_comment'></div>扬五色之辉，尚继瞻于庆瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229644_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1229644_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年8月</a>　在汴京，八月初，除太学正。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年8月19日</a>　在汴京，八月十九日，除太学博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年4月</a>　在汴京，四月，有文。作品：《代李邦彦谢起复表》<div id='poem_1229633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李邦彦谢起复表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229633")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229633'>倚庐梓里，方深何怙之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229633_comment'></div>出綍枫宸，遽复频虚之促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229633_comment'></div>以仅存之残息，而使之陪国论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229633_comment'></div>以已试之空官，而责其赞治功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229633_comment'></div>恳避无从，兢惶罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229633_comment'></div>臣伏念奋身疏逖，逢时休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229633_comment'></div>亲膺睿圣特达之知，服在左右畴咨之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229633_comment'></div>俯殚末技，顾玩岁愒日以无闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229633_comment'></div>仰跂清光，惟奉令承教之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229633_comment'></div>知力微而胜重，果福过以灾生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229633_comment'></div>虽保全允赖于皇慈，而祸衅难逃于天罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229633_comment'></div>未究循陔之养，忽缠陟岵之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229633_comment'></div>曲轸宸心，特优恤典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229633_comment'></div>冠隆名于五阁，肆推蜜印之褒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229633_comment'></div>庀襄事于九原，仍厚轺车之委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229633_comment'></div>松楸改色，闾里生辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229633_comment'></div>不忘孤苦之身，每示记存之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229633_comment'></div>夺情以起，捐日以需。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229633_comment'></div>甫终哭踊之期，申命维纲之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229633_comment'></div>哀情累上，天听莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229633_comment'></div>夫何待尽之微生，乃冒非常之异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229633_comment'></div>洒宝章而关天运，载纡紫诏之温；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229633_comment'></div>颁驲骑以冀星驰，荐枉皇华之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229633_comment'></div>扶力前趋于严召，疏恩亟对于便朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229633_comment'></div>玉色赐怜，德音甚渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229633_comment'></div>谕以显亲之大，勉其许国之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229633_comment'></div>履地戴天，奚胜跼蹐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229633_comment'></div>摩顶至踵，尽出生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229633_comment'></div>矧兹筦辖之司，实佐钧衡之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229633_comment'></div>念龊龊备员之久，已愧罔功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229633_comment'></div>岂皇皇衔恤之中，敢云善职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229633_comment'></div>兹荷龙光之渥，更惭鼠技之穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229633_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下礼以使臣，道无弃物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229633_comment'></div>深顾邦家之计，聿严辅翼之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229633_comment'></div>矧制服以情，当致三年之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229633_comment'></div>然断恩以义，宁逃二事之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229633_comment'></div>爰俾从权，靡容退处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229633_comment'></div>宠灵横被，感涕交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229633_comment'></div>臣敢不恭体殊私，益坚素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229633_comment'></div>收思虑于摧裂荒迷之后，劳筋骸于忧伤毁瘠之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229633_comment'></div>贪禄何心，忍死但从于王事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229633_comment'></div>教忠在耳，捐生期报于君恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229633_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1229633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年11月8日</a>　在汴京，十一月八日，改宣教郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年11月</a>　在汴京，十一月，除秘书省正字，未及施用，以内艰去。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f22d3f5afcd843d09c4e42ea0336aca4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f22d3f5afcd843d09c4e42ea0336aca4");'><span id='f22d3f5afcd843d09c4e42ea0336aca4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>，44岁</div><div id='f22d3f5afcd843d09c4e42ea0336aca4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年1月</a>　在汴京，有文。作品：《代郑望之谢除户部侍郎表》<div id='poem_1229626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑望之谢除户部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229626")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229626'>备台中之郎属，姑试冗曹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229626_comment'></div>庀左户之贰卿，遽升要任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229626_comment'></div>饬兼衣而出笥，束宝带以华身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229626_comment'></div>拜命非常，抚躬罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229626_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以冢宰制国用而出纳，归有司之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229626_comment'></div>司徒掌邦赋而度支，专左曹之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229626_comment'></div>故在平时，最称剧部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229626_comment'></div>矧此多虞之际，岂惟经费之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229626_comment'></div>由边防失御狄之机，肆京甸萃勤王之旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229626_comment'></div>饵戎车之众，金缯殆竭于赢馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229626_comment'></div>给貔虎之师，刍粟方劳于飞挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229626_comment'></div>必有裕民之长策，乃为足食之良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229626_comment'></div>如臣者风力不彊，材资甚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229626_comment'></div>教忠有训，期黾勉以承家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229626_comment'></div>见义当为，敢逡巡而避事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229626_comment'></div>骇战尘之侵轶，逼都邑以震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229626_comment'></div>和议初陈，敌情叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229626_comment'></div>寇至君谁与守，彼忍偷安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229626_comment'></div>兵交使在其间，臣奚恤死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229626_comment'></div>赖真人之嗣极，致大敌之革心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229626_comment'></div>惟肆贪求，卒归成好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229626_comment'></div>繄圣神之所格，在臣子以何功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229626_comment'></div>宜即严诛，顾叨异宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229626_comment'></div>歘自散郎之列，径跻法从之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229626_comment'></div>虽世服厥官，获继先臣之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229626_comment'></div>而朝容幸位，惧尘初政之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229626_comment'></div>忧深徒切于循墙，令出终难于反汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229626_comment'></div>夫何孤远，乃尔遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229626_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下躬大禹之俭勤，负成汤之勇智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229626_comment'></div>无为而用天下，自销偷侈之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229626_comment'></div>不战而屈人兵，阴夺寇攘之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229626_comment'></div>属此纂图之始，遘兹猾夏之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229626_comment'></div>德务好生，嘉与兆民之康乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229626_comment'></div>仁宁屈己，姑从一切之权宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229626_comment'></div>欲就远图，岂难小忍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229626_comment'></div>共识人君之度，曾何使命之劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229626_comment'></div>犹录妄庸，遽令超躐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229626_comment'></div>而臣比缘计议，数对威光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229626_comment'></div>仰英断之无前，知睿谋之有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229626_comment'></div>侧身尝胆，愿无忘今日之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229626_comment'></div>报国捐躯，顾敢爱他时之力！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229626_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1229626_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

淄博（淄川县）
