-----title
杭州（钱塘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='09b5203a524c43bca99e68ab87049561_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("09b5203a524c43bca99e68ab87049561");'><span id='09b5203a524c43bca99e68ab87049561_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，47岁</div><div id='09b5203a524c43bca99e68ab87049561' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月23日</a>　二月二十三日，随高宗驻跸钱塘。在显宁寺处理公务。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月</a>　在钱塘，三月，有文。作品：《代李邴辞免翰林学士奏状》《代郑瑴谢除御史中丞表》<div id='poem_1229677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李邴辞免翰林学士奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229677")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229677'>闻命震惊，抚躬踧踖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229677_comment'></div>伏念臣顷由简拔，尝直禁严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229677_comment'></div>典文章翰墨之司，粗陈薄技；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229677_comment'></div>输献纳论思之益，莫见微劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229677_comment'></div>遽抵谴诃，久从流落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229677_comment'></div>志虑耗于积忧之后，筋骸疲于多病之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229677_comment'></div>清故里之烟尘，觊获耦耕于南亩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229677_comment'></div>瞻中天之日月，敢期重入于修门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229677_comment'></div>矧今国步尚艰，民情未辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229677_comment'></div>军书狎至，正赖于谋谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229677_comment'></div>王命时行，尤资于辞令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229677_comment'></div>兼任斯责，实惟此官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229677_comment'></div>筹幄居中，将以收仁声之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229677_comment'></div>诏音布外，必能感武夫之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229677_comment'></div>要须任才，乃可称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229677_comment'></div>如臣已试，惟众所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229677_comment'></div>顾有未补于平时，况可冒居于今日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229677_comment'></div>仰祈睿断，追寝误恩，俾更就于閒官，庶无妨于贤路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229677_comment'></div>臣无任祈天俟命、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229677_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1229677_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑瑴谢除御史中丞表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229630")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229630'>备七人之上列，久尸谏省之员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229630_comment'></div>总三院之大纲，伏忝宪台之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229630_comment'></div>超踰已甚，忧责弥深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229630_comment'></div>避宠命以无从，抚危躬而增惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229630_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣器难受大，才不及中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229630_comment'></div>由管库之卑微，预朝廷之任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229630_comment'></div>滥当言责，属此艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229630_comment'></div>奉白简以抨弹，徒有怨仇之积；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229630_comment'></div>伏青蒲而规劝，愧无献替之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229630_comment'></div>罪已著于丘山，功靡陈于毫发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229630_comment'></div>宜从谴斥，更误褒升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229630_comment'></div>方今国步未夷，皇家多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229630_comment'></div>敌王所忾，外虽倚于爪牙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229630_comment'></div>诘国之奸，内实资于耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229630_comment'></div>必得力能厌难，名可折冲，不吐刚而茹柔，俾绳愆而纠谬，庶张国法，先振主威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229630_comment'></div>曾何妄庸，乃堪抡选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229630_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下绍登大宝，光御丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229630_comment'></div>乃圣乃神，固有生知之性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229630_comment'></div>克岐克嶷，共瞻天纵之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229630_comment'></div>奉慈训于东朝，布英才于言路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229630_comment'></div>过收旧物，使率乃僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229630_comment'></div>臣敢不祗服训辞，激昂懦守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229630_comment'></div>见无礼者必击，期少举于颓纲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229630_comment'></div>知有命而不回，誓益坚于晚节。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1229630_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='200c97863ff84405a17b9aec9dac8f1d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("200c97863ff84405a17b9aec9dac8f1d");'><span id='200c97863ff84405a17b9aec9dac8f1d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1134')">1132-1134年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='200c97863ff84405a17b9aec9dac8f1d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月1日</a>　在钱塘，二月一日，有斋文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后几筵前寒食节水陆道埸斋文》<div id='poem_1229828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后几筵前寒食节水陆道场斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229828")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229828'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子二月朔日，皇帝为寒食节，使僧二十一人，于昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水陆道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229828_comment'></div>伏以稽山东望，再逢拜扫之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229828_comment'></div>鹫岭西来，固有追修之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229828_comment'></div>怆园陵之莫展，奉几席以犹新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229828_comment'></div>式当寒食之辰，大启法筵之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229828_comment'></div>阴功有托，具存保祐之慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229828_comment'></div>觉力可依，用荐超升之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229828_comment'></div>更推圣利，普及含灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229828_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月5日</a>　在钱塘，二月五日，经吕颐浩举荐，叔厚试吏部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月10日</a>　在钱塘，二月十日，除吏部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月</a>　在钱塘，二月，以吏部侍郎兼权直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月1日</a>　在钱塘，三月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月2日</a>　在钱塘，三月二日，言颜博文撰伪楚赦书，公议不允收叙。朝廷从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月3日</a>　在钱塘，三月三日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月8日</a>　在钱塘，三月八日，草占城国王杨卜麻叠制词。作品：《除占城国王杨卜麻叠特授依前检校太傅使持节琳州诸军事琳州刺史充怀远军节度使琳州管内观察处置等使兼御史大夫占城国王加食邑食实封散官勋如故制》<div id='poem_1229381' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229381' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229381?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除占城国王杨卜麻叠特授依前检校太傅使持节琳州诸军事琳州刺史充怀远军节度使琳州管内观察处置等使兼御史大夫占城国王加食邑食实封散官勋如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229381")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229381_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229381'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229381'>门下：朕采汶上之仪，因省方而飨帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229381_comment'></div>授泰元之策，斯敛福以锡民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229381_comment'></div>欢欣既洽于群臣，庆施远周于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229381_comment'></div>载颁显命，以逮殊邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229381_comment'></div>怀远军节度使、琳州管内观察处置等使、琳州刺史、上柱国、占城国王、食邑六千户、食实封二千五百户杨卜麻叠，气禀纯和，性资忠壹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229381_comment'></div>介南溟而有国，世蒙零露之多濡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229381_comment'></div>谨北面以称藩，蚤识烈风之不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229381_comment'></div>庭琛屡贡，爵典荐加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229381_comment'></div>建大将之高牙，视三公之极位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229381_comment'></div>王灵滋至，侯度益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229381_comment'></div>属展采于宗祈，既成釐事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229381_comment'></div>顾广恩于祭泽，可废彝章？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229381_comment'></div>乃增衍于爰田，并倍敦于真食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229381_comment'></div>以侈精禋之贶，以昭顺节之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229381_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229381_comment'></div>崇德报功，朕则靡遐遗之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229381_comment'></div>向风慕义，尔其坚内附之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229381_comment'></div>往对庞禧，永绥厚禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229381_comment'></div>可依前检校太傅、使持节琳州诸军事、琳州刺史、充怀远军节度使、琳州管内观察处置等使、兼御史大夫、占城国王，加食邑五百户、食实封二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229381_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1229381_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月8日</a>　在钱塘，三月八日，草阇婆国王悉里地茶兰固野制词。作品：《除阇婆国王悉里地茶兰固野特授依前检校司徒使持节琳州诸军事琳州刺史充怀远军节度使琳州管内观察处置等使兼御史大夫阇婆国王加食邑食实封散官勋如故制》<div id='poem_1229382' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229382' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229382?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除阇婆国王悉里地茶兰固野特授依前检校司徒使持节琳州诸军事琳州刺史充怀远军节度使琳州管内观察处置等使兼御史大夫阇婆国王加食邑食实封散官勋如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229382")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229382_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229382'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229382'>门下：朕省方近国，适当三岁之亲祠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229382_comment'></div>展采合宫，咸仿九筵之往制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229382_comment'></div>玉帛交荐，笾豆骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229382_comment'></div>辑旷礼以涓成，委鸿休而来假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229382_comment'></div>肆推庆施，用轶绵区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229382_comment'></div>怀远军节度使、琳州管内观察处置等使、金紫光禄大夫、检校司徒、使持节琳州诸军事、琳州刺史、兼御史大夫、上柱国、阇婆国王、食邑三千四百户、食实封一千四百户悉里地茶兰固野，性质温恭，天资诚顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229382_comment'></div>宅海邦而有众，自矜乐土之饶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229382_comment'></div>向天阙以观光，夙起华风之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229382_comment'></div>束帛屡至，爵服载颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229382_comment'></div>地虽隔于域中，心每倾于日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229382_comment'></div>属修元祀，普洽湛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229382_comment'></div>维显相之劳，尝已加于群后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229382_comment'></div>念来臣之旧，泽岂间于遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229382_comment'></div>即六纛之前仪，仍三槐之故秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229382_comment'></div>衍之多户，倍以真封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229382_comment'></div>并为裔土之光，式广昊穹之祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229382_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229382_comment'></div>宠均列辟，曾无内外之殊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229382_comment'></div>居限重溟，宜识朝宗之谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229382_comment'></div>往绥蕃祉，以永令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229382_comment'></div>可特授依前检校司徒、使持节琳州诸军事、琳州刺史、充怀远军节度使、琳州管内观察处置等使、兼御史大夫、阇婆国王、加食邑五百户、食实封二百户，散官、勋如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229382_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1229382_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月10日</a>　在钱塘，三月十日，有斋文。作品：《御前寒食节于昭慈献烈皇后几筵前建水陆道场斋文》《昭慈献烈皇后寒食节道场斋文》<div id='poem_1229829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御前寒食节于昭慈献烈皇后几筵前建水陆道场斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229829")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229829'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子三月壬辰朔，十日辛丑，御前为寒食节，使僧二十一人就昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水路道场一昼夜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229829_comment'></div>伏以盛德难忘，想慈颜之如在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229829_comment'></div>孝心欲报，惟象教之可凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229829_comment'></div>岁华甫觌于清明，民俗争先于拜扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229829_comment'></div>莫展柏城之域，但瞻玉几之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229829_comment'></div>爰集缁流，广陈法会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229829_comment'></div>合幽冥而普供，宣秘密之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229829_comment'></div>庶仗殊因，获资圣地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229829_comment'></div>觉乘是證，哀愿不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229829_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229829_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后寒食节道场斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229827")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229827'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子三月壬辰朔，十日辛丑，皇帝为寒食节，于临安府净慈寺使僧二十一人，昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水陆道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229827_comment'></div>伏以墦祭届期，重起园陵之慕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229827_comment'></div>玉衣留御，空瞻几席之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229827_comment'></div>恭即祗园，大兴法会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229827_comment'></div>普祫冥阳之供，用资先圣之缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229827_comment'></div>榆燧既更，感孝思而曷已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229827_comment'></div>具文可质，超慧果以何疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229827_comment'></div>更仗圣功，永扶皇祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229827_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月11日</a>　在钱塘，三月十一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月15日</a>　在钱塘，三月十五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月1日</a>　在钱塘，四月一日，有祈晴文。作品：《临安府上天竺寺开启祈晴文》<div id='poem_1229841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安府上天竺寺开启祈晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229841")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229841'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子四月辛酉朔日，皇帝遣入内内侍省东头供奉官、睿思殿掌书管簿杨立本，使僧四七人于临安府上天竺寺开启祈晴道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229841_comment'></div>伏以民勤终岁，人力待时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229841_comment'></div>凡兹衣食之原，视彼雨旸之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229841_comment'></div>愿念霖霪之久，适当长养之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229841_comment'></div>既蚕月之妨功，且麦秋之告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229841_comment'></div>饥寒之虑，宵旰是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229841_comment'></div>爰叩佛乘，庶从人愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229841_comment'></div>亟扫积阴之沴，尽还慧日之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229841_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月1日</a>　在钱塘，四月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月14日</a>　在钱塘，四月十四日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月15日</a>　在钱塘，四月十五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline'
