id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月27日</a>　在钱塘，四月二十七日，草吕颐浩制词。作品：《除吕颐浩特授依前尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事都督江淮两浙荆湖诸军事》<div id='poem_1229376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除吕颐浩特授依前尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事都督江淮两浙荆湖诸军事<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229376")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229376'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229376'>门下：承天子而裁万化，入则断国论于一堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229376_comment'></div>位冢宰而总六师，出则折遐冲于诸夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229376_comment'></div>欲并注安危之两意，顾莫先文武之兼资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229376_comment'></div>虽三公在朝，协济经邦之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229376_comment'></div>而一相处内，宜存分陕之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229376_comment'></div>属我元臣，诞扬丕号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229376_comment'></div>特进、尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事、文安郡开国侯、食邑五千五百户、食实封一千八百户吕颐浩，高明而笃实，刚毅而恢闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229376_comment'></div>学推齐鲁之英，气禀山河之粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229376_comment'></div>达于权而知变，更剧易之百为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229376_comment'></div>勇于义以奋忠，挺险夷之一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229376_comment'></div>慷慨而安神器，勤劳而乂王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229376_comment'></div>名动华戎，勋高庙社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229376_comment'></div>自再登于揆路，实首执于事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229376_comment'></div>房、杜同功，每推权而不吝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229376_comment'></div>苏、宋共政，盖相得以甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229376_comment'></div>方内治之交修，顾外夷之孰御，深轸纳沟之虑，备陈多垒之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229376_comment'></div>谓玩岁苟安，非拯溺救焚之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229376_comment'></div>且待时自定，岂兴衰拨乱之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229376_comment'></div>请以身先，愿为众倡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229376_comment'></div>朕念国步迍邅之滋久，邦基臲卼而靡宁，警跸屡迁，藩篱莫固，徒得君重，果为朕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229376_comment'></div>矧黄裳佐唐，专决用兵之算；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229376_comment'></div>而王导辅晋，尝兼都督之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229376_comment'></div>是用独委戎旃，并提相印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229376_comment'></div>董师干于八路，仍魁柄于中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229376_comment'></div>尽长江表里之封，悉归经略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229376_comment'></div>举宿将王侯之贵，咸听指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229376_comment'></div>庶宣畅于威灵，用拊宁于方域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229376_comment'></div>陪敦邑赋，昭示眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229376_comment'></div>鼎铉不移，式系苍生之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229376_comment'></div>旌旄所向，正需元老之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229376_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229376_comment'></div>内惟张仲之贤，吉甫之行何远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229376_comment'></div>上若宪宗之断，裴度之功乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229376_comment'></div>朕固披勿贰之衷，汝亦有同心之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229376_comment'></div>艰虞攸托，中外实均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229376_comment'></div>往扬厉于天声，伫恢隆于宰业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229376_comment'></div>惟我耆德，岂烦训词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229376_comment'></div>可特授依前尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事、都督江淮两浙荆湖诸军事，加食邑一千户、食实封四百户，封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229376_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1229376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月28日</a>　在钱塘，四月二十八日，奏奏新及第人差注事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月1日</a>　在钱塘，闰四月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月13日</a>　在钱塘，闰四月十三日，有奏劄。作品：《乞申饬百官札子》<div id='poem_1229648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞申饬百官劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年闰四月十三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229648")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229648'>臣伏观周宣王之《小雅》，于《车攻》则曰内修政事，外攘夷狄，复文武之境土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229648_comment'></div>于《吉日》则曰能慎微接下，无不自尽，以奉其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229648_comment'></div>然则中兴之效，本于修政事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229648_comment'></div>而政事之修，亦在夫小大之臣无不自尽而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229648_comment'></div>今朝廷播迁，庶事草创，外备彊敌，内锄群盗，日不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229648_comment'></div>而百司庶府，小大之臣，类多苟且偷安，不务举职，姑息胥吏，阔略细务，累资养誉，犹袭承平之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229648_comment'></div>其间亦有孜孜奉公，疚心职事，则众必非笑，指以为迂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229648_comment'></div>至摘其事而靳之曰：「了得其事，便足以胜夷狄否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229648_comment'></div>臣切怪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229648_comment'></div>且国家大体，辅弼大臣任之，所谓百司庶府之臣，知治其一官一职而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229648_comment'></div>夫使一官一职而皆治焉，则事将无所不治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229648_comment'></div>传曰：「嫠不恤其纬，而忧宗周之陨为将及焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229648_comment'></div>彼忧之诚是也，盍亦图其所忧而效于上欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229648_comment'></div>傥无所陈其智谋，以裨国论之万一，乃徒私忧过计，空废实务，亦奚救于危乱哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229648_comment'></div>今不及其暇时修起庶政，顾以细务为不足省，则大事亦将委靡，而纪纲弛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229648_comment'></div>纪纲既弛，而欲驾驭豪杰，以兴衰拨乱，不亦难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229648_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣断，深察兹弊，申饬百执事之臣各扬其职，无以空言忧国而妨实务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229648_comment'></div>庶几细大毕举，纪律设张，则内治外攘，无所不可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229648_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1229648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月15日</a>　在钱塘，闰四月十五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月28日</a>　在钱塘，闰四月二十八日，草刘光世制词。作品：《除刘光世特起复宁武军节度使开府仪同三司依前充两浙西路安抚大使马步军都总管兼知镇江军府事淮南东路宣抚使兼营田使食邑食实封如故制》<div id='poem_1229366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除刘光世特起复宁武军节度使开府仪同三司依前充两浙西路安抚大使马步军都总管兼知镇江军府事淮南东路宣抚使兼营田使食邑食实封如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229366")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229366'>门下：忠之所移者孝，顾孰先父子之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229366_comment'></div>礼之有变者权，盖宜徇国家之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229366_comment'></div>嗟予良翰，宅彼大忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229366_comment'></div>虽苴麻之慕方深，然金革之虞可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229366_comment'></div>式颁明命，敷告治朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229366_comment'></div>持服前宁武军节度使、开府仪同三司、充两浙西路安抚大使、马步军都总管、兼知镇江军府事、淮南东路宣抚使兼营田使、彭城郡开国公、食邑四千三百户、食实封一千八百户刘光世，智勇无前，恭勤不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229366_comment'></div>南征北讨，名夙播于华夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229366_comment'></div>入卫出藩，任兼隆于将相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229366_comment'></div>自镇临于京口，且绥定于淮壖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229366_comment'></div>休士卒以屯田，方讲营平之策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229366_comment'></div>拊流亡而复业，寖观渤海之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229366_comment'></div>威望既彰，敌情原屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229366_comment'></div>正赖折冲之效，遽兴陟岵之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229366_comment'></div>维乃先臣，为时宿将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229366_comment'></div>联勋盟府，得教子之义方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229366_comment'></div>从乃穹庐，卒陨身于名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229366_comment'></div>念尔家雠之未雪，属兹戎事之犹繁，义不戴天，应厉枕戈之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229366_comment'></div>忠当许国，难从释位之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229366_comment'></div>即命衮之上仪，仍斋坛之旧节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229366_comment'></div>其还所治，用讫尔庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229366_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229366_comment'></div>丧以礼成，固欲尽三年之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229366_comment'></div>恩由义断，亦奚拘贰事之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229366_comment'></div>期两报于君亲，盍并图于家国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229366_comment'></div>尚抑茹荼之痛，毋忘尝胆之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229366_comment'></div>可特起复宁武军节度使、开府仪同三司，依前充两浙西路安抚大使、马步军都总管、兼知镇江军府事、淮南东路宣抚使兼营田使，食邑、食实封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229366_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1229366_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年4月</a>　在钱塘，四月，草黄叔敖诏。作品：《赐新除户部侍郎黄叔敖辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除户部侍郎黄叔敖辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229479")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229479'>敕叔敖：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229479_comment'></div>卿文学行义，深得家传，而吏能心计，特闻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229479_comment'></div>服勤仕版，踰四十年，名蔼搢绅，达于朕听，擢居琐闼，兼侍经帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229479_comment'></div>议论之长，见闻之洽，初不自表，阅试乃详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229479_comment'></div>老成可亲，朕益自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229479_comment'></div>念时方多故，而财用为急，更图往效，进贰地官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229479_comment'></div>夫转输调度之宜，卿固优为之矣，亟安乃职，毋事谦撝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229479_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229479_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月1日</a>　在钱塘，五月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月1日</a>　在钱塘，五月一日，内中讲筵殿开设祈晴道场，叔厚有文。作品：《内中讲筵殿祈晴文》<div id='poem_1229845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内中讲筵殿祈晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229845")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229845'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子五月朔日，嗣天子臣，命道士二十人就内中讲筵殿开建祈晴道场，谨上启元始天尊、太上道君、太上老君混元上德皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229845_comment'></div>伏以农夫望岁，苦雨逾旬，岂惟行路之兴嗟，并与力田而告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229845_comment'></div>敢伸精祷，冀格至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229845_comment'></div>虽政事或乖，时乃眇躬之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229845_comment'></div>而粢盛有阙，恐贻上帝之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229845_comment'></div>愿驱宿沴之灾，还廓大明之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229845_comment'></div>臣无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229845_comment'></div>谨词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229845_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月1日</a>　在钱塘，五月一日，祈晴道场罢散，叔厚有文。作品：《内中讲筵殿祈晴道场罢散文》<div id='poem_1229846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内中讲筵殿祈晴道场罢散文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229846")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229846'>臣言：伏为祈晴道场设醮一座，三百六十分位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229846_comment'></div>伏以积阴作沴，久雨为淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229846_comment'></div>百祀是供，惧有粢盛之害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229846_comment'></div>六师在戍，尤怀馈饷之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229846_comment'></div>仰觊天心，俯矜民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229846_comment'></div>趣扶桑之晨照，收屏翳之馀威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229846_comment'></div>庶使三农，荐蒙一稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229846_comment'></div>臣无任精虔激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229846_comment'></div>谨告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月1日</a>　在钱塘，五月一日，雨霁，有谢晴道场散罢表。作品：《内中讲筵殿改作谢晴道场散罢表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月5日</a>　在钱塘，五月五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月15日</a>　在钱塘，五月十五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月15日</a>　在钱塘，五月十七日，草权邦彦生日诏。作品：《赐签书枢密院权邦彦生日诏》<div id='poem_1229394' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229394' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229394?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐签书枢密院权邦彦生日诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月十七日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229394")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229394_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229394'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229394'>储神骏岳，列辅鸿枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229394_comment'></div>方资借箸之谋，适庆垂弧之旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229394_comment'></div>宜加宠锡，用介禧祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229394_comment'></div>今赐卿生日羊酒米面等，具如别录，至可领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229394_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北海集》卷八。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229394_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229394'>五月十七日：原无，据翰林院本补。</div><div
