id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月</a>　在钱塘，五月，草权邦彦诏。作品：《赐新除端明殿学士签书枢密院事权邦彦辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229488' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229488?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除端明殿学士签书枢密院事权邦彦辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229488")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229488_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229488'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229488'>敕邦彦：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229488_comment'></div>朕以军国大政分畀辅臣，顾尚右武之时，尤重本兵之任，久虚厥次，盖难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229488_comment'></div>卿悃愊无华，靖共有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229488_comment'></div>临危徇节，忠尝至于毁家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229488_comment'></div>遭变苦心，虑宜深于谋国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229488_comment'></div>延登廊庙，参与枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229488_comment'></div>佥言允谐，朕志素定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229488_comment'></div>方需闳议，叶济多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229488_comment'></div>胡为逡巡，犹乃逊避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229488_comment'></div>往励匪躬之操，共伸尝胆之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229488_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229488_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229488_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月</a>　在钱塘，五月，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐新除提举万寿观兼侍读朱胜非辞免恩命乞改授一外任宫祠不允诏》<div id='poem_1229420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除提举万寿观兼侍读朱胜非辞免恩命乞改授一外任宫祠不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229420")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229420'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏辞免恩命，乞改除一外任宫祠，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229420_comment'></div>朕怀思旧臣，欲以自近，肆初召卿于外，盖期入侍燕闲，以补眇躬之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229420_comment'></div>属会稽谋帅，辍卿以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229420_comment'></div>未曾煖席，而以军国大计，起为八路之督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229420_comment'></div>卿既露恳固辞，而远临戎事，论者亦谓兹非处卿者，遽复中格，俾还旧治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229420_comment'></div>顾卿未谕厥旨，遂求閒便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229420_comment'></div>继阅来奏，良用怃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229420_comment'></div>式遄其归，申颁前命，庶几奉祠琳馆，进读金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229420_comment'></div>且无职事之烦，而得话言之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229420_comment'></div>朕之初意若此，卿尚何云？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229420_comment'></div>所请宜不允，仍不得再行陈请，日下起发前来赴行在供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229420_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229420_comment'></div>秋凉，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229420_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229420_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月1日</a>　在钱塘，六月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月15日</a>　在钱塘，六月十五日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月</a>　在钱塘，六月，草吕颐浩诏。作品：《赐特进尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事都督江淮荆淛路诸军事吕颐浩辞免长男承议郎抗次男宣教郎摭除职名赐章服恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐特进尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事都督江淮荆浙路诸军事吕颐浩辞免长男承议郎抗次男宣教郎摭除职名赐章服恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229498")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229498'>敕颐浩：省所上劄子奏，辞免男抗、摭除职名、赐章服恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229498_comment'></div>卿再登元辅，尝立大勋，比总六师，往督诸道，忠勤诚至，不惮暑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229498_comment'></div>而于其所私，曾弗内顾，在朕其可忘之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229498_comment'></div>矧方倚卿以图邦国再造之功，而卿之息则未录，岂其礼哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229498_comment'></div>肆推茂恩，断自朕志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229498_comment'></div>今卿乃以异时侥倖者为戒，引谊力辞，殊失厥旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229498_comment'></div>宜识兹意，勿复重陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229498_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229498_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229498_comment'></div>夏热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229498_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月</a>　在钱塘，六月，草张守诏。作品：《赐资政殿学士左中大夫知绍兴府张守辞免提举万寿观兼侍读恩命并乞外任宫观一次不允诏》<div id='poem_1229478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐资政殿学士左中大夫知绍兴府张守辞免提举万寿观兼侍读恩命并乞外任宫观一次不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229478")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229478'>敕张守：省所奏劄子，辞免恩命并乞外任宫观一次，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229478_comment'></div>卿顷辞近辅，继领便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229478_comment'></div>虽政化之优，流闻甚迩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229478_comment'></div>而话言之益，渴想于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229478_comment'></div>蔽之朕心，召以自近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229478_comment'></div>方需昼接，乃以疾陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229478_comment'></div>矧琳馆奉祠，无吏文之拘迫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229478_comment'></div>而经帷进读，得燕语之从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229478_comment'></div>宜深念于多艰，以来裨于不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229478_comment'></div>退閒之语，非朕所期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229478_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229478_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229478_comment'></div>夏热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229478_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月</a>　在钱塘，六月，草折彦质诏。作品：《赐新除龙图阁直学士折彦质辞免恩命并召赴行在乞除在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除龙图阁直学士折彦质辞免恩命并召赴行在乞除在外宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229446")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229446'>敕彦质：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229446_comment'></div>卿蚤由才谞，尝缀近严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229446_comment'></div>擅边境之功，世高将阀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229446_comment'></div>服诗书之教，名在儒科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229446_comment'></div>岂伊一眚之为尤，乃与远图而并弃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229446_comment'></div>肆还近职，趣赴行朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229446_comment'></div>尽涤前辜，将观后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229446_comment'></div>缅惟忠谊，宜自激昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229446_comment'></div>忽披来谂之诚，殊失所期之素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229446_comment'></div>矧湖湘谋帅，已继锡于赞书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229446_comment'></div>则江海就闲，可辄安于祠馆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229446_comment'></div>往祗朕命，毋费乃辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229446_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229446_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月1日</a>　在钱塘，七月一日，有青词。作品：《温州景灵宫奉安圣祖天尊大帝圣像奏告青词》<div id='poem_1229802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温州景灵宫奉安圣祖天尊大帝圣像奏告青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229802")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229802'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子，七月朔日，嗣天子臣伏为于温州景灵宫奉安圣像，遣某官奏告，谨上启圣祖上灵高道九天司命保生天尊大帝、元天大圣后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229802_comment'></div>伏以降延恩之秘殿，尝觌飙游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229802_comment'></div>敞万寿之殊庭，久严像设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229802_comment'></div>属有风尘之警，乃迁山海之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229802_comment'></div>馆御未宁，夙兴是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229802_comment'></div>姑从原庙，祗奉睟容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229802_comment'></div>香火弗亲，敢怠寅恭之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229802_comment'></div>干戈庶定，更延祚嗣之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229802_comment'></div>臣无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229802_comment'></div>谨词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229802'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229802_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月1日</a>　在钱塘，七月一日，有斋文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后昭慈献烈皇后筵几前中元节道场斋文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月1日</a>　在钱塘，七月一日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814'>伏以并土旧传，已举藏烟之令，稽山新卜，甫临上冢之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229814_comment'></div>拜扫不亲，瞻思徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后扶持神器，拥佑眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229814_comment'></div>未伸孝养之诚，忽叹仙游之邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229814_comment'></div>敢忘时荐，仰答慈恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（寒食节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814'>伏以谷雨初濡，见农功之毕务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229814_comment'></div>公桑载绿，感蚕事之方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道盛母仪，德侔坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229814_comment'></div>望仙游之何所，瞻遗范以空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229814_comment'></div>韶景易阑，孝思曷已<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814'>伏以候应清和，未改春生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229814_comment'></div>身离供养，还悲夏凊之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后化洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229814_comment'></div>望音容之如在，嗟晦朔之俄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229814_comment'></div>岁月有穷，哀思无既<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814'>伏以宫衣忽掩，惊月魄之沦辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229814_comment'></div>燧火俄更，叹星缠之周次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229814_comment'></div>隙驹难驻，仙驭奚攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德被眇躬，力扶大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229814_comment'></div>方承颜而尽养，乃厌世以登遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229814_comment'></div>及兹奉讳之辰，弥切怀思之念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月十四日忌辰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814'>伏以金徽戢响，悲维夏之初薰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229814_comment'></div>露麦飞芒，感有秋之新荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229814_comment'></div>慈颜在慕，孝养已违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后母道无前，阴功有衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229814_comment'></div>即帘帷而再御，安鼎祚以重新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229814_comment'></div>遗训敢忘，哀诚难写<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814'>伏以叶换阶蓂，未变清和之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229814_comment'></div>阴敷宰木，重兴感慕之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德盛四朝，功存万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229814_comment'></div>不返乘云之驭，已踰改火之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229814_comment'></div>夏凊永违，时思徒切<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814'>伏以气馀当闰，寝惊历候之还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月2日</a>　在钱塘，七月二日，奏破格差注县丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月7日</a>　在钱塘，七月七日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕欑宫旦望节序表本》<div id='poem_1229814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后祔庙毕攒宫旦望节序表本</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229814")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814'>伏以参伏星缠，叹隙驹之易失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229814_comment'></div>草薰辇路，怅羽驾以何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后德洽宫闱，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229814_comment'></div>望佳城之永闭，履芳节以时思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229814_comment'></div>哀绪难任，徽音无尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（三月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814'>伏以曲水传觞，感流年于景物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229814_comment'></div>遗衣在寝，追懿范于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后躬履艰难，志存慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229814_comment'></div>及芳辰之可乐，嗟大养之已违，但惊时序之迁，空结园陵之恋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上巳）</span>。<div
