id='poem_sentence_41_1229814_comment'></div>月满正中，载感母仪之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后圣明超古，慈俭自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229814_comment'></div>功高彤管之书，德盛练衣之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229814_comment'></div>岁时易失，思慕难忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（闰四月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814'>伏以星火方中，遂正南讹之候；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229814_comment'></div>陵园永闭，奚胜东望之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后坤载无私，母仪有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229814_comment'></div>未极孝心之报，忽惊仙驭之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229814_comment'></div>急景频迁，长哀莫既<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814'>伏以楚俗良时，甫届浴兰之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229814_comment'></div>越山佳气，遥瞻拱木之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后盛德无名，至仁有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229814_comment'></div>折大奸于指顾，避兵安事于灵符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229814_comment'></div>损上寿于忧勤，续命空悲于䌽缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229814_comment'></div>载追懿范，第极哀悰<span class='inlineComment2'>（重五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814'>伏以长夜难晨，痛泉扃之昼掩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229814_comment'></div>流年易老，感木槿之朝荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229814_comment'></div>炎序载中，慈颜永隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后仁同长养，道极高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229814_comment'></div>繄社稷之再安，岂帘帷之得已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229814_comment'></div>空馀女史，能播母仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814'>伏以庆集猗兰，载纪眇生之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229814_comment'></div>悲缠长乐，已嗟大养之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后保佑深恩，慈仁德盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229814_comment'></div>骤隔家人之礼，但瞻陵柏之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229814_comment'></div>感慕增怀，追攀劳望<span class='inlineComment2'>（圣节）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814'>伏以火晔方升，金微初伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229814_comment'></div>仰天时之迭运，感人意以增悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后早正坤元，晚安鼎器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229814_comment'></div>甫致东朝之养，遽从先后之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229814_comment'></div>庙室犹新，始奉麦瓜之荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229814_comment'></div>园林甚迩，渐惊松槚之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229814_comment'></div>缅想徽音，难胜哀绪<span class='inlineComment2'>（初伏）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814'>伏以日回东井，知溽暑之方隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229814_comment'></div>地近南溟，觉炎蒸之弥异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后业贻万世，慈化六宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229814_comment'></div>陵木已阴，徒感追凉之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229814_comment'></div>寝闱既寂，空馀欲清之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229814_comment'></div>盛德难名，悲悰奚叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814'>伏以月满柏城，始见飞萤之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229814_comment'></div>尘昏椒壁，还闻促织之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229814_comment'></div>夏景将阑，时思曷已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功高汉邓，德迈周任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229814_comment'></div>大养已违，空感《南陔》之咏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229814_comment'></div>遗芬无尽，永传《彤管》之书<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月望）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814'>伏以大火西流，骤减故宫之暑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229814_comment'></div>凉风朝至，还悲拱木之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后俪德乾元，齐功坤载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229814_comment'></div>年华晼晚，嗟供养之永违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229814_comment'></div>懿烈芬芳，但怀思而无斁<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月旦）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814'>伏以殿阒承华，讵睹班龙之驾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229814_comment'></div>山遥缑氏，应同白鹤之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229814_comment'></div>怆仙驭之难追，感母仪之增慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229814_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后道高往后，功冠本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229814_comment'></div>想神灵之在天，望星河而霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229814_comment'></div>空馀懿烈，永播鸿名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1229814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229814'><span class='label'>按：</span>七夕。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229814_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月12日</a>　在钱塘，七月十二日，奏奖酬当立约束。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月24日</a>　在钱塘，七月二十四日，草陈规奖谕诏。作品：《赐左中奉大夫徽猷阁待制徳安府复州汉阳军镇抚使马歩军都总管兼知徳安府陈规奖谕诏》<div id='poem_1229406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐左中奉大夫徽猷阁待制德安府复州汉阳军镇抚使马步军都总管兼知德安府陈规奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229406")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229406'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229406'>敕陈规：卿体国尽忠，守藩称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229406_comment'></div>当中原之未定，念南亩之多荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229406_comment'></div>兵食未充，农功盖少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229406_comment'></div>乃别营屯之制，用兴稼穑之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229406_comment'></div>军民不杂，而无争畔之辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229406_comment'></div>官吏不增，而无加廪之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229406_comment'></div>得鲁侯之重谷，同汉相之留田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229406_comment'></div>东作西成，居有安生之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229406_comment'></div>缓耕急战，人怀赴敌之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229406_comment'></div>条理不烦，设施可法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229406_comment'></div>载观绩效，深用叹嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229406_comment'></div>故兹奖谕，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229406_comment'></div>秋热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229406_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月28日</a>　在钱塘，七月二十八日，移兵部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，有奏状。作品：《固守利害奏状》<div id='poem_1229686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论进讨固守利害劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229686")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229686'>臣伏奉亲笔处分，召至都堂，令条具进讨及固守利害者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229686_comment'></div>臣伏见金人自靖康以来，无岁无兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229686_comment'></div>及乘舆南渡，己酉之冬，直寇江浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229686_comment'></div>逮其归师龃龉，谓可以休矣，乃且移兵，以寇关陕，乘我富平之败，遂窥巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229686_comment'></div>幸吴玠一胜，稍挫其锋，然其图我，盖未忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229686_comment'></div>今侦谍所传，皆言敌人并兵以趣川陕，可以知其情矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229686_comment'></div>盖以向来江表用兵，非敌形势之便，故二三岁来，悉力窥蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229686_comment'></div>其意以谓蜀若不守，江浙自摇，故必图之不置，非特报前一败而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229686_comment'></div>则是今日利害，在吾蜀兵之胜负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229686_comment'></div>吾兵若胜，而敌不得近蜀，则必气索而众离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229686_comment'></div>若乘其败，而西自襄汉，东自淮海，进兵以攻讨，则我必大得志，而中原定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229686_comment'></div>虽然，川陕之地，远在数千里外，行在诸军，力不足以应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229686_comment'></div>若坐待其胜负之报，胜固可喜，苟为不胜，岂不寒心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229686_comment'></div>以兵家之势言之，则彼向陇蜀，我当出淮汉，以牵制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229686_comment'></div>然而朝廷初不为此策，将相初不为此行，虽臣知之，亦不敢妄有所进说焉者，盖以我师事力之未足耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229686_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229686_comment'></div>自南渡后，兵无所增募，而士卒之老、疾、死、亡者岁岁有耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229686_comment'></div>诸军苟利其廪给，则多张虚籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229686_comment'></div>或因降盗，有所简汰，旋各招取，以补其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229686_comment'></div>名数虽多，非皆精练而可用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229686_comment'></div>犹赖去岁以来，一二大将皆能尽力，破灭剧贼，士稍知战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229686_comment'></div>然臣旧闻诸将之论，以为盗贼虽彊大，己必能胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229686_comment'></div>若金人之兵，则非所可敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229686_comment'></div>其论如此，不知今日厥意又复如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229686_comment'></div>顾张浚一军，士卒最为简练，器甲最为整饬，犹可驱而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229686_comment'></div>韩世忠骁勇无前，盖尝抗敌于江上，今复屡胜群盗，度其果敢，亦必不肯辞难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229686_comment'></div>其下如岳飞，皆可赖以为用，第不知士卒果能齐力一心，无所畏避，以当金人否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229686_comment'></div>舍是三将，则其馀无足倚者，缓急掎角应援，便无可使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229686_comment'></div>又况中州之地，利于用骑，吾之诸军，大率乘马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229686_comment'></div>若徒以步兵驰逐于平原广野之间，以当金人之铁骑，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229686_comment'></div>不如守长江之有险阻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229686_comment'></div>复有最所患者，财用之不丰，粮糗之不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229686_comment'></div>虽平居无事，犹难取给，况兴师动众，以深入敌境哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229686_comment'></div>今若欲乘敌未来，我先进讨，彼中原之民闻王师大举，庶几响应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229686_comment'></div>然一胜一负，兵家常势，吾以一大将将兵深入，恐彼亦不为无备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229686_comment'></div>臣之所虑，万一有所不捷，一军失利，则我便难于后无继，人情必为之震动，适足以致师而来寇，不如缓举之为愈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229686_comment'></div>臣愚以为，姑守长江之险，以俟敌衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229686_comment'></div>顾敌祸已穷，天将悔革，则彼必败于陇蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229686_comment'></div>在今日之势，陇蜀既固，则吾之气全，而人心亦壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229686_comment'></div>敌之破败，又如去冬，然后徐为之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229686_comment'></div>不然，敌师尚彊，则我素弱之兵可轻举哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229686_comment'></div>臣岂不知坐守江表，中原何时而定，盖以事力不足，要图必胜，乃可以动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229686_comment'></div>姑亦简吾师徒，励吾将帅，息吾民力，去吾冗官，丰吾财用，敌至则力战而应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229686_comment'></div>傥或以彼一失，则乘胜逐利，遂取中原，亦未可知，非谓漠然无意于恢复，而区区仅以自守而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229686_comment'></div>若淮上积粟，则吾未有因粮深入之计，谓可募人间入，燔其所聚，以伐敌情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229686_comment'></div>如近海诸处，亦可阴使范温、徐文之徒，若以盗贼钞劫而攘取之，斯亦无害于守戍之防者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229686_comment'></div>臣知识短浅，不能远图，无以上副圣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229686_comment'></div>臣不胜昧死谨录奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1229686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草张守诏。作品：《赐新除资政殿学士左中大夫知福州张守辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除资政殿学士左中大夫知福州张守辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229475")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229475'>敕张守：省所劄子奏，辞免知福州恩命，乞除一在外宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229475_comment'></div>朕以瓯闽之俗，民物夥繁，孅啬自足，安于无事旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229475_comment'></div>间者政或不良，盗贼数起，兵挐祸结，频年未定，肆兴师旅，往行天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229475_comment'></div>虽妖孽悉除，而疮痍未复，朕甚悯焉，思得辅弼旧臣，宣吾德意，往临镇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229475_comment'></div>载图其人，莫如卿者，是用辍金华之召，殿此南服，庶资雅望，于以肃清四境，安集一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229475_comment'></div>惟卿体国之诚，宜识朕志，以时上道，勿复深辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229475_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229475_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229475_comment'></div>秋热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229475_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐观文殿学士左宣奉大夫知绍兴府朱胜非乞改一外任宫观差遣不允诏》《赐观文殿学士左宣奉大夫知绍兴府事充两浙东路安抚使朱胜非辞免新除同都督江淮荆浙诸军事恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐观文殿学士左宣奉大夫知绍兴府朱胜非乞改一外任宫观差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229418")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229418'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏，乞改授一外任宫观差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229418_comment'></div>卿尝秉国钧，比更藩翰，肆图人望，召付兵权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229418_comment'></div>而乃力贡忱辞，愿回成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229418_comment'></div>莫副急贤之用，独深将母之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229418_comment'></div>朕鉴乃诚，重劳旧德，爰止趣行之使，已颁改命之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229418_comment'></div>还政近邦，俾谐私欲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229418_comment'></div>尚资绥靖，得缓顾忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229418_comment'></div>閒退之求，则非朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229418_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229418_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229418_comment'></div>秋凉，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229418_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229418_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐观文殿学士左宣奉大夫知绍兴府事充两浙东路安抚使朱胜非辞免新除同都督江淮浙诸军事恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229417")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229417'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229417_comment'></div>朕观吴、晋之主崛兴江左，陆逊、王导皆以佐命大臣督中外之师，所以尊王室而威诸夏，盖有在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229417_comment'></div>前属元宰有八路之行，顾朝廷之上不可虚位，肆令召还，以遥制于中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229417_comment'></div>且命卿以故相之重，往临于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229417_comment'></div>庶表里相与戮力，共济艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229417_comment'></div>朕岂乐夫迁令易制，以数劳吾旧德为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229417_comment'></div>安危之计，正需卿等，有不得已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229417_comment'></div>昔人以一士止百万之师，一贤制千里之难，非卿则孰任此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229417_comment'></div>尚疾其驱，毋复坚避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229417_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229417_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229417_comment'></div>秋凉，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229417_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草沈与求诏。作品：《赐新除吏部尚书兼翰林学士沈与求辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除吏部尚书兼翰林学士沈与求辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229456")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229456'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229456'>敕与求：省所奏辞免恩命，乞除一在外宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229456_comment'></div>卿历更言路，进长宪台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229456_comment'></div>纠弹不避于贵权，建明有补于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229456_comment'></div>贤劳滋久，宜在褒升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229456_comment'></div>顾自元丰而来，御史中执法盖以天官常伯、北门学士为美迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229456_comment'></div>惟卿材识疏通，辞章赡蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229456_comment'></div>政事文学之选，见谓兼长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229456_comment'></div>并命两官，以为优宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229456_comment'></div>退閒之请，非朕所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229456_comment'></div>往体眷意，勿复牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229456_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229456_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229456_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草黄叔敖诏。作品：《赐新除户部尚书兼侍读充修政局参详官黄叔敖辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除户部尚书兼侍读充脩政局参详官黄叔敖辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229481")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229481'>敕叔敖：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229481_comment'></div>自南渡以来，胡骑盗贼，迭兴干戈，江浙荆闽之间，遍罹其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229481_comment'></div>兵火所及，城邑为丘墟，南亩之民，靡有孑遗耗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229481_comment'></div>于斯时也，乃足食足兵，知取知予，地官之任，其可忽耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229481_comment'></div>朕比诏大臣，设脩政局，讲求裕国息民之策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229481_comment'></div>而卿以小司徒，实参厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229481_comment'></div>顾老成详练，取决为多，肆命卿遂为之长，以帅其属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229481_comment'></div>庶几议论推行之际，无所乖戾，克就乃功，朕之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229481_comment'></div>卿其勿辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229481_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229481_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月</a>　在钱塘，八月，草秦桧乞宫观不允诏。作品：《赐尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事秦桧乞外任宫观差遣不允诏》<div id='poem_1229490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事秦桧乞外任宫观差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229490")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229490'>敕秦桧：省所劄子奏，乞外任宫观差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229490_comment'></div>朕惟大公之道，责成辅弼，委任不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229490_comment'></div>固欲赖其心德之同，以济大业于艰难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229490_comment'></div>卿来自孤远，遂相朕躬，夙夜勤劳，于兹旬岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229490_comment'></div>谅欲行其道以有为于当世耳，胡为抗章，遽求避位？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229490_comment'></div>无乃违卿欲行之志，而异朕所以责成之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229490_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229490_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月26日</a>　在钱塘，高宗欲罢免秦桧，二十六日，召叔厚入对，以御笔词头付之。叔厚以上意草秦桧罢相制。作品：《除秦桧特授观文殿学士提举江州太平观依前通奉大夫食邑食实封如故任便居住制》<div id='poem_1229378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除秦桧特授观文殿学士提举江州太平观依前通奉大夫食邑食实封如故任便居住制<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229378")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229378'>门下：王者循至公之道，常加厚于股肱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229378_comment'></div>大臣高易退之风，欲曲全于体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229378_comment'></div>维时次辅，兹解近司，式颁上印之恩，诞布告庭之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229378_comment'></div>左通议大夫、守尚书右仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事、提举修政局、江宁郡开国公、食邑二千四百户、食实封八百户秦桧，蚤矜志行，历蹈艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229378_comment'></div>谓其尽节以事君，可膺大用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229378_comment'></div>嘉乃脱身而归国，实慰群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229378_comment'></div>擢置岩廊，俾参柄任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229378_comment'></div>自初豫政，疑若献忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229378_comment'></div>从其长，则未尝争议于当然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229378_comment'></div>私于朕，则每独指言其不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229378_comment'></div>遂令代相，倚以为邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229378_comment'></div>务推勿贰之诚，庶尽欲行之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229378_comment'></div>自诡得权而举事，当耸动于四方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229378_comment'></div>逮兹居位以陈谋，首建明于二策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229378_comment'></div>罔烛厥理，殊乖素期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229378_comment'></div>念方委听之专，更责寅恭之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229378_comment'></div>而乃凭恃其党，排拫所憎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229378_comment'></div>进用臣邻，率面从而称善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229378_comment'></div>稽留命令，辄阴訹以交攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229378_comment'></div>岂实汝心，殆为众误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229378_comment'></div>顾窃弄于威柄，虑或长于奸萌，方悉屏除，尚图改事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229378_comment'></div>遽辞机政，屡却封章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229378_comment'></div>诏谕莫回，留挽难强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229378_comment'></div>爰升华于秘殿，仍赋禄于殊庭，以示优容，以昭眷遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229378_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229378_comment'></div>予夺在我，岂云去朋党之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229378_comment'></div>始终待卿，斯无负君臣之谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229378_comment'></div>往膺涣渥，勿替令猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229378_comment'></div>可特授观文殿学士、提举江州太平观，依前通奉大夫，食邑、食实封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229378_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1229378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月29日</a>　在钱塘，八月二十九日，有青词。作品：《内中开建祈祷道场青词》<div id='poem_1229803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内中开建祈祷道场青词<span class='inlineComment2'>（八月二十九日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229803")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229803'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子，八月戊子朔，二十九日丙辰，嗣天子臣命道士二十人就内中开建祈祷道场，谨上启元始天尊太上道君太上老君混元圣德皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229803_comment'></div>伏以星文呈异，天戒动威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229803_comment'></div>永惟谴咎之来，事无虚作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229803_comment'></div>大惧照临之下，变不空生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229803_comment'></div>敢忘修省之诚，更致祷祈之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229803_comment'></div>尚其眷祐，鉴此精徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229803_comment'></div>亟消弭于妖祥，以导迎于善气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229803_comment'></div>臣无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229803_comment'></div>谨词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229803'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229803_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年8月</a>　在钱塘，八月，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐朱胜非辞免依旧知绍兴府乞除授一外任宫祠差遣不允诏》<div id='poem_1229419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐朱胜非辞免依旧知绍兴府乞除授一外任宫祠差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229419")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229419'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏，辞免依旧知绍兴府恩命，乞除一外任宫祠差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229419_comment'></div>朕以天步犹艰，边虞未靖，思时雅望，为国折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229419_comment'></div>图旧弼以临戎，督全师而开府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229419_comment'></div>烦言遽至，成命遂迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229419_comment'></div>顾东道之要藩，实行朝之近屏，用还其故，亦便乃私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229419_comment'></div>矧礼义不愆，纵多言而奚恤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229419_comment'></div>且君臣无间，于大体而何伤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229419_comment'></div>朕固循爱人以德之规，卿其尽事君以忠之道，乞閒之语，非朕欲闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229419_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229419_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229419_comment'></div>秋凉，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229419_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月1日</a>　在钱塘，九月一日，有斋文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水陆道场斋文》<div id='poem_1229831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水陆道场斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229831")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229831'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子九月朔日，皇帝为十月一日，使僧二十一人赴昭慈献烈皇后几筵前作水陆道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229831_comment'></div>伏以阳月载临，叹岁时之晼晚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229831_comment'></div>东朝不御，瞻几筵以凄洏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229831_comment'></div>广修殊胜之因，用證超升之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229831_comment'></div>式招净侣，恭启法筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229831_comment'></div>凭大雄大力之神，设无碍无遮之供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229831_comment'></div>仰资冥福，俯慰孝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229831_comment'></div>更分不尽之功，普及无情之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229831_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月8日</a>　在钱塘，九月八日，草朱胜非制词。作品：《除朱胜非特授依前左宣奉大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事加食邑食实封制》<div id='poem_1229375' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229375' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229375?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除朱胜非特授依前左宣奉大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事加食邑食实封制<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年九月乙丑）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229375")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229375_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229375'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229375'>门下：朕戒惧多虞，畴咨良辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229375_comment'></div>维持左右，繄吾二相之协心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229375_comment'></div>推挽后先，岂予一人之独济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229375_comment'></div>念得贤则国之福，而知人者帝所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229375_comment'></div>惩亟易之徒烦，盖尝轻用于新进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229375_comment'></div>怀老成之往效，曷若登庸于旧劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229375_comment'></div>爰即治朝，诞扬明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229375_comment'></div>观文殿学士、左宣奉大夫、提举万寿观、兼侍读、义阳郡开国公、食邑二千五百户、食实封七百户朱胜非，闳深而端亮，敦大而疏通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229375_comment'></div>陈平之智有馀，如晦之才能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229375_comment'></div>从予初载，蚤宣力于要津；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229375_comment'></div>嘉乃一心，遂奋庸于宰路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229375_comment'></div>骇巨奸之窃发，睨神器而莫摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229375_comment'></div>独倚精忠，阴摧元恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229375_comment'></div>驯豺狼之暴而事无遗策，卒销沮于凶谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229375_comment'></div>翊帘帷之政而人靡间言，旋复还于明辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229375_comment'></div>成功不处，巧语俄兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229375_comment'></div>嗟去位之累年，殆谤书之盈箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229375_comment'></div>朕追原曩事，弥想话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229375_comment'></div>惟当轴者三旬，岂远猷之能究；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229375_comment'></div>爰赐环而屡命，趣旧德以来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229375_comment'></div>再觌仪形，益新启沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229375_comment'></div>虽从容经幄，期入奉于咨询；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229375_comment'></div>而密勿岩廊，盍同寅于康济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229375_comment'></div>乃还升于右揆，仍兼秉于中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229375_comment'></div>增衍封租，并隆宠渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229375_comment'></div>以慰具瞻之素，以彰注意之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229375_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229375_comment'></div>谢安未起而心已系于苍生，盖大臣之重轻在望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229375_comment'></div>裴度既还而威复行于河朔，则朝廷之得失以人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229375_comment'></div>顾予共政之贤，时乃同功之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229375_comment'></div>庶几兹美，无愧前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229375_comment'></div>其戮力于我家，俾有辞于永世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229375_comment'></div>可特授依前宣奉大夫、守尚书右仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事，加食邑一千户、食实封四百户，封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229375_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1229375_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草朱胜非生日诏。作品：《赐新除尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非生日诏》<div id='poem_1229392' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229392' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229392?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非生日诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229392")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229392_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229392'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229392'>萧昴储精，申嵩禀粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229392_comment'></div>巨川待济，再膺舟楫之求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229392_comment'></div>吉梦献占，犹记熊罴之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229392_comment'></div>维忠与孝，宜寿而臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229392_comment'></div>爰分生饩之仪，用助家庭之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229392_comment'></div>今赐卿生日羊酒米面等，具如别录，至可领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229392_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1229392_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月18日</a>　在钱塘，九月十八日，御笔除翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，上辞免翰林学士奏状。作品：《辞免翰林学士奏状》<div id='poem_1229667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免翰林学士奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229667")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229667'>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229667_comment'></div>臣以荒疏不腆之学，缀缉不工之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229667_comment'></div>自忝从臣，每兼内制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229667_comment'></div>暨再还于班列，盖五被于选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229667_comment'></div>岁月空移，功能何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229667_comment'></div>过录摄承之效，甫升寓目之员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229667_comment'></div>偶入对于清光，乃近叨于眷奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229667_comment'></div>占学士久虚之次，遂俾为真；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229667_comment'></div>预明君亲擢之荣，岂胜其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229667_comment'></div>周旋自视，进退靡遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229667_comment'></div>伏望圣慈俯矜危恳，第姑容于代匮，亦奚遽于超迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229667_comment'></div>特收睿命之行，庶息烦言之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229667_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任踧踖俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229667_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，有谢启。作品：《除翰林学士谢朝官启》<div id='poem_1229732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除翰林学士谢朝官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229732")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229732'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229732'>伏被中除，进颛内职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229732_comment'></div>优解七兵之务，冒游三俊之躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229732_comment'></div>顾大册高文，宁有相如之丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229732_comment'></div>而深谋密虑，更惭陆贽之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229732_comment'></div>得宠若惊，当荣知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229732_comment'></div>重念自天之厚渥，岂无为地之先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229732_comment'></div>属制谒以攸拘，望宾闳而莫进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229732_comment'></div>其为感愧，难罄敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229732_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月19日</a>　在钱塘，九月十九日，有奏札。作品：《乞诏臣僚降诏札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月30日</a>　在钱塘，九月三十日，草邢焕制词。作品：《除邢焕特授庆远军节度使充醴泉观使特封德清县开国子食邑五百户食实封二百户制》<div id='poem_1229372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除邢焕特授庆远军节度使充醴泉观使特封德清县开国子食邑五百户食实封二百户制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229372")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229372'>门下：亲帝祠而行庆，本朝存不易之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229372_comment'></div>以后父而疏封，历世有相承之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229372_comment'></div>朕礼神而徼福，稽古而广恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229372_comment'></div>维时戚里之良，来被合宫之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229372_comment'></div>肆颁斋钺，式布明纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229372_comment'></div>保静军承宣使邢焕，禀德纯明，赋资乐易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229372_comment'></div>纳嫔朱邸，蚤联肺腑之亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229372_comment'></div>正位长秋，遂托椒房之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229372_comment'></div>方履艰难之际，实宣陪扈之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229372_comment'></div>恂恂敦谨厚之风，翼翼执谦恭之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229372_comment'></div>簉英游于延阁，尝缀从班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229372_comment'></div>承密旨于中枢，旋更使领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229372_comment'></div>求闲甚力，避宠弗居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229372_comment'></div>乃远引于荒遐，殆备尝于险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229372_comment'></div>比赐环而锡命，喜乘驿以来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229372_comment'></div>顾宫掖凄凉，重感播迁之祸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229372_comment'></div>而姻亲零落，孰宽寡恃之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229372_comment'></div>留寘行朝，复辞要地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229372_comment'></div>念恩均百辟，可独限于后家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229372_comment'></div>矧官滞五期，盍序升于将阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229372_comment'></div>是用建节旄于南屏，奉祠馆于中都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229372_comment'></div>多食圭腴，肇开封邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229372_comment'></div>茂举邦朝之典，并为贤戚之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229372_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229372_comment'></div>家重身尊，曾靡婴于吏职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229372_comment'></div>仁沾恩洽，兹共享于神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229372_comment'></div>惟富贵不离其躬，则君臣并受其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229372_comment'></div>往膺涣渥，益勉令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229372_comment'></div>特授庆远军节度使、充醴泉观使，特封德清县开国子，食邑五百户，食实封二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229372_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1229372_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草席益诏。作品：《赐新除吏部侍郎席益辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除吏部侍郎席益辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229464")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229464'>敕席益：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229464_comment'></div>自南渡以来，典籍散亡，而铨选之法敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229464_comment'></div>有司随事建明，以补苴罅漏，而条目亦已粗举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229464_comment'></div>任职者不知省，无所操执，以杜吏奸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229464_comment'></div>乃徒沽誉一时，务先人情，而忽防检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229464_comment'></div>故法益玩，奸益生，士皆趋利目前，有苟得之风，而将来者殆不可继，其敝为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229464_comment'></div>维卿学知大体，智周小物，见于已试旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229464_comment'></div>肆命卿典兹左选，庶几惩乎前而善其后，使吏无容奸，而士不失职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229464_comment'></div>所优为耳，夫尚何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229464_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229464_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229464_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草王绹诏。作品：《赐资政殿大学士左中大夫提举临安府洞霄宫王绹辞绍兴府恩命乞依旧宫祠终满此任不允诏》<div id='poem_1229437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐资政殿大学士左中大夫提举临安府洞霄宫王绹辞绍兴府恩命乞依旧宫祠终满此任不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229437")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229437'>敕王绹：省所劄子奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229437_comment'></div>朕慎图旧弼，分殿大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229437_comment'></div>资雅望之折冲，庶增隆于国势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229437_comment'></div>即便安而为政，用优宠于耆英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229437_comment'></div>纶命既孚，师言惟穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229437_comment'></div>遽披需奏，备控忱辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229437_comment'></div>顾政府周旋，尝处具瞻之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229437_comment'></div>则帅庭静治，可收坐镇之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229437_comment'></div>谅不至于勤劳，亦何烦于逊避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229437_comment'></div>亟祗乃事，庸副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229437_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229437_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229437_comment'></div>秋冷，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229437_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐新尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非辞免恩命不允诏》《赐新除尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非辞免恩命不允断来章批答》<div id='poem_1229415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229415")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229415'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229415'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229415_comment'></div>朕惟自昔之君考慎其相，求之梦卜，盖难约于常规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229415_comment'></div>拔自疏微，或未明于大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229415_comment'></div>能副忧勤之托，要先劳旧之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229415_comment'></div>卿尝秉国钧，适遭时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229415_comment'></div>笼吠主之群而无所肆暴，延勤王之旅而终以成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229415_comment'></div>明辟既还，左符径去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229415_comment'></div>谪官四载，许国一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229415_comment'></div>是用悉辨谗诬，申加收召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229415_comment'></div>俾复归于大任，庶终济于多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229415_comment'></div>君臣之间，情好弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229415_comment'></div>胡为未体，尚或有云？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229415_comment'></div>往懋乃庸，无留朕命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229415_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229415_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229415_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事朱胜非辞免恩命不允断来章批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229578")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229578'>省表具知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229578_comment'></div>朕闵国多艰，需人共济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229578_comment'></div>金谷甲兵之问，每至于庙堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229578_comment'></div>盐梅舟楫之求，实劳于岩野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229578_comment'></div>适吾旧德，归造行朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229578_comment'></div>顾雅望之素高，惜前功之未究，俾还分于台揆，以对秉于机衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229578_comment'></div>方今狄患犹滋，政多外惧，邦基未定，孰与中兴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229578_comment'></div>惟夙怀许国之诚，宜大展匡时之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229578_comment'></div>庶其戮力，用克解忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229578_comment'></div>朕既急于得贤，卿盍思于爱日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229578_comment'></div>雍容辞逊，岂所望哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229578_comment'></div>所请宜不允，仍断来章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229578_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1229578'>〔批答口宣〕有敕：卿道可致君，忠宜谋国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229578_comment'></div>用再图于旧德，以协济于多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229578_comment'></div>成命既行，谦辞何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229578_comment'></div>今差。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229578_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草沈与求诏。作品：《赐吏部尚书兼权翰林学士沈与求辞免兼侍读恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐吏部尚书兼权翰林学士沈与求辞免兼侍读恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1229458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229458'>敕与求：省所奏，辞免兼侍读恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229458_comment'></div>朕思乂时艰，若稽古典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229458_comment'></div>维始终念学，舍斯道则安从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229458_comment'></div>顾直谅多闻，需其人而自近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229458_comment'></div>卿顷司风宪，有鲠谔之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229458_comment'></div>今执铨衡，得公方之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229458_comment'></div>代予述作，溢于文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229458_comment'></div>盖学贯穿而不穷，故才纵横而皆可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229458_comment'></div>进兼劝读，亦便咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229458_comment'></div>勉迪我于大猷，姑略卿之小节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229458_comment'></div>亟祗成命，毋事谦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229458_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229458_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在钱塘，秋，得吴道子《天龙八部图》，留观于家中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年10月10日</a>　在钱塘，十月十日，有斋文。作品：《御前为太上道君皇帝就内中道场斋文》<div id='poem_1229832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御前为太上道君皇帝就内中道场斋文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年10月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229832")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229832'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子十月戊子朔，十日丁酉，御前为太上道君皇帝天宁圣节，就内中作祝圣寿道场一永日者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229832_comment'></div>伏以候当阳月，节纪诞辰，仰瞻天德之宁，虔祝圣人之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229832_comment'></div>广延开士，恭启清场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229832_comment'></div>凭我觉雄，出兹胜力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229832_comment'></div>推九龄之吉梦，进衍昌期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229832_comment'></div>指七圣之迷途，归安大养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229832_comment'></div>更资慈护，永保皇图。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1229832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年10月</a>　在钱塘，十月，草王似诏。作品：《赐新除端明殿学士川陕等路宣抚处置等副使王似辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除端明殿学士川陕等路宣抚处置等副使王似辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年10月）</span><span id='poem_sentence_1_1229426_comment'></div>肆求任重之才，就副抚戎之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229426_comment'></div>惟卿数更边阃，士安宽猛之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229426_comment'></div>久治蜀都，人咏中和之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229426_comment'></div>迨兹已试，用以不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229426_comment'></div>朕命甫通，群情应悦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229426_comment'></div>忽披忱奏，犹执谦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229426_comment'></div>盖优宠儒臣，进班联于秘殿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229426_comment'></div>而尽护诸将，俾节制于全师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229426_comment'></div>非以私卿，庶其却敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229426_comment'></div>往殚乃力，庸副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229426_comment'></div>夏热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229426_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年11月</a>　在钱塘，十一月，草洪拟诏。作品：《赐新除礼部尚书洪拟辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除礼部尚书洪拟辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1229455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229455'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229455'>敕洪拟：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229455_comment'></div>卿中违省户，出剖郡符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229455_comment'></div>允资共理之良，已报期年之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229455_comment'></div>顾瞻班列，思见老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229455_comment'></div>虽殿彼一邦，方安良翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229455_comment'></div>而典兹三礼，宜属耆儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229455_comment'></div>趣还常伯之联，俾正秩宗之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229455_comment'></div>当军旅而陈俎豆之事，固曰未遑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229455_comment'></div>披荆棘而立本朝之仪，乃其所急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229455_comment'></div>勉推旧学，来副详延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229455_comment'></div>成命不移，谦辞奚取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229455_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229455_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229455_comment'></div>冬寒，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229455_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229455_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月1日</a>　在钱塘，十二月一日，有青词。作品：《临安府天庆观禳谢青词》<div id='poem_1229804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安府天庆观禳谢青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年12月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229804")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229804'>维绍兴二年岁次壬子，十二月朔日，嗣天子臣谨遣臣某，命道士二十一人，于临安府天庆观开建禳谢道场，谨上启元始天尊太上老君混元上德皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229804_comment'></div>伏以玄冥司政，方凝闭以收威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229804_comment'></div>回禄挻灾，乃凭陵而为祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229804_comment'></div>鼓烈风而雷怒，灰比屋以埃飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229804_comment'></div>暴露中霄，苍黄万室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229804_comment'></div>由人君之失德，致黎庶之蒙辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229804_comment'></div>变或可禳，诚岂能感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229804_comment'></div>是用虔依琳宇，恭启琼科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229804_comment'></div>归命高真，冀动昭回之鉴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229804_comment'></div>闵仁生类，获逃燔燬之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229804_comment'></div>臣无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229804_comment'></div>谨词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229804'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229804_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月8日</a>　在钱塘，十二月八日，行在临安府火，叔厚所居遭焚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月18日</a>　在钱塘，十二月十八日，草张浚诏。作品：《赐检校少保定国军节度使知枢密院事张浚赴行在诏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月</a>　在钱塘，十二月，草沈与求诏。作品：《赐新除龙图阁学士充荆湖南路安抚使兼知潭州沈与求辞免恩命乞一在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除龙图阁学士充荆湖南路安抚使兼知潭州沈与求辞免恩命乞一在外宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229457")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229457'>敕与求：省所奏并辞免恩命，乞一在外宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229457_comment'></div>朕以湖湘之南，寇攘频扰，兵革之后，儆备未休，爰咨近臣，往镇方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229457_comment'></div>维卿历居台省，每陈忧国之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229457_comment'></div>久侍轩墀，与识爱民之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229457_comment'></div>察其可用，何所不宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229457_comment'></div>虽铨衡得人，无若山涛之比；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229457_comment'></div>然诗书取帅，谁居却谷之先？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229457_comment'></div>肆分藩阃之雄，并宠河图之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229457_comment'></div>顾中外迭任，乃国朝之旧章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229457_comment'></div>而险夷一心，亦臣子之常分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229457_comment'></div>胡为有请，自托不能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229457_comment'></div>惟付予之甚艰，岂忱诚之弗亮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229457_comment'></div>尚其深体，毋复多云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229457_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229457_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229457_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年1月9日</a>　在钱塘，一月九日，书恤刑诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年1月25日</a>　在钱塘，一月二十五日，奏论杨惟忠、邢焕以节度使致仕。作品：《乞讨论纳节换官札子》<div id='poem_1229653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞讨论纳节换官劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年正月二十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年1月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229653")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229653'>臣窃见近者杨惟忠、邢焕皆以节度使致仕，即不曾锁院降麻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229653_comment'></div>伏缘节度使除拜移改若加恩之类，并须宣制，岂有见带节钺致仕而不然，此一时之阙典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229653_comment'></div>臣尝记祖宗时，凡节将臣僚得谢，不以文武，论纳节，别除一官致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229653_comment'></div>如仁宗朝张耆自使宰授太子太师、杨崇勋授太子太保、神宗朝李端愿自节度使授太子少保致仕，皆武臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229653_comment'></div>惟熙宁间，富弼以元勋旧相，始令特带节钺致仕，弼犹力辞不敢当者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229653_comment'></div>其后相继者，则曾公亮、文彦博也，他人岂可援以为例也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229653_comment'></div>近岁以来，致仕者不问何人，不复纳节换官，亦恐有违旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229653_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈特降睿旨，并令三省、枢密院讨论旧典施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年1月</a>　在钱塘，一月，草席益诏。作品：《赐新除工部尚书席益辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除工部尚书席益辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229463")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229463'>敕席益：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229463_comment'></div>卿世有令名，蚤跻华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229463_comment'></div>历代言于两禁，更共理者五州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229463_comment'></div>身数器而有馀，才兼人而不匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229463_comment'></div>顷被赐环之命，载联持橐之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229463_comment'></div>执铨衡而奸欺之迹靡容，奉劝讲而补益之言屡至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229463_comment'></div>审堪还用，宁惮亟迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229463_comment'></div>维时六卿，实亚二府，有以德举，不由序升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229463_comment'></div>姑进掌于冬官，尚委成于选事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229463_comment'></div>并图乃绩，岂曰朕私？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229463_comment'></div>其即钦承，毋劳逊避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229463_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年1月</a>　在钱塘，一月，草赵仲湜诏。作品：《赐皇叔祖检校少保靖海军节度使开府仪同三司嗣濮王仲湜辞免兼大宗正事恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐皇叔祖检校少保靖海军节度使开府仪同三司嗣濮王仲湜辞免兼大宗正事恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1229412_comment'></div>朕观《麟趾》之风，而念振振之族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229412_comment'></div>读《行苇》之雅，而怀戚戚之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229412_comment'></div>遭时艰否之期，感此散离之后，肆召司属，还趋行朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229412_comment'></div>庶纠合于宗枝，以固安于根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229412_comment'></div>惟卿嗣承濮邸，贵袭王封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229412_comment'></div>属籍既尊，宗盟是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229412_comment'></div>俾总有司之务，用敦同姓之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229412_comment'></div>宜疾其驰，尚何所避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229412_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229412_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年2月</a>　在钱塘，二月，草徐俯诏。作品：《赐新除翰林学士知制诰徐俯辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除翰林学士知制诰徐俯辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229459")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229459'>敕徐俯：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229459_comment'></div>学士之职，非独以文翰，待命禁林，而深谋密议，或预参决，号称内相，尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229459_comment'></div>我祖宗优礼词臣，退朝燕閒，犹多召见，从容顾问，克广聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229459_comment'></div>而数十年来，官因人废，书诏之外，无所预闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229459_comment'></div>分釐院务，殆与外司等耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229459_comment'></div>朕甚惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229459_comment'></div>卿以豪杰之才，老成之望，比跻谏省，数对于中，嘉其告猷，宜在兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229459_comment'></div>庶几兴复之功，兼赖腹心之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229459_comment'></div>且使故事因卿而存，岂特号令文章需其用哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229459_comment'></div>益体眷知，毋烦谦避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229459_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' href='/Writing/1229462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除参知政事席益辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a id='poem_sentence_0_1229462_comment'></div>朕以神州犹梗，天步未夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229462_comment'></div>并力合谋，方圣哲共劳于驰骛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229462_comment'></div>顷得卿于远外，已属意于今兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229462_comment'></div>遭谤去朝，谪官经岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229462_comment'></div>卿其尽道，朕则知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229462_comment'></div>尚恢复古之图，毋徇好谦之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229462_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229462_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除签书枢密院事徐俯辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span
