id='poem_title_1229461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229461'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229461'>敕徐俯：省所劄子奏，辞免恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229461_comment'></div>事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229461_comment'></div>朕焦劳愿治，物色求贤，庶由多难以兴邦，思得非常之奇士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229461_comment'></div>顷召卿于閒远，初未觌于仪形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229461_comment'></div>擢在七人，居才五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229461_comment'></div>正言慷慨，尽拾遗补过之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229461_comment'></div>燕见从容，多画策含奇之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229461_comment'></div>察其可用，宁复计资？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229461_comment'></div>视草奚为，姑假途于銮禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229461_comment'></div>运筹有赖，俾列位于枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229461_comment'></div>曾无累日之淹，式表一时之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229461_comment'></div>期大摅于素蕴，以共济于康功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229461_comment'></div>谦逊之辞，卿其毋执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229461_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229461_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年2月28日</a>　在钱塘，二月二十八日，进兼侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年2月</a>　在钱塘，二月，有辞免兼侍读奏状。作品：《辞免兼侍读奏状》<div id='poem_1229668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼侍读奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229668")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229668'>闻命兢惶，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229668_comment'></div>恭惟陛下以日新之学，辅天纵之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229668_comment'></div>推大法于《春秋》，深得圣君之奥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229668_comment'></div>越诸儒于今古，独明王道之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229668_comment'></div>虽专门之师，莫望于清光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229668_comment'></div>在历世之君，孰偕于盛美？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229668_comment'></div>而臣蚤因觅举，粗亦知书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229668_comment'></div>顾伦类之不通，且见闻之非博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229668_comment'></div>盖尝涉猎三家之记，窃玩其文辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229668_comment'></div>奚暇研穷一字之微，以言其褒贬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229668_comment'></div>仰神心之自得，惭懵学之何施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229668_comment'></div>藉令裒众说于训诂之间，安得措一词于睿明之下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229668_comment'></div>况臣心思衰耗，目病昏眵，已知视草之难能，讵可执经而入侍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229668_comment'></div>愿回成命，更选鸿儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229668_comment'></div>使无妨进之讥，庶获异闻之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229668_comment'></div>披诚良确，得请是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229668_comment'></div>所有误恩，乞赐寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229668_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年3月</a>　在钱塘，三月初，有谢表。作品：《谢兼侍读表》<div id='poem_1229609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢兼侍读表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229609")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229609'>词禁代言，已极文章之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229609_comment'></div>经帷进读，益亲日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229609_comment'></div>际遇甚荣，空疏知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229609_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>惟人君之典学，有先哲之格言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229609_comment'></div>断自唐虞，至于文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229609_comment'></div>为王者事，本钦明稽古之模；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229609_comment'></div>须友以成，繄直谅多闻之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229609_comment'></div>圣狂之念或异，治乱之涂乃分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229609_comment'></div>降及后人，亦循前轨，昧于烛理，祗以为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229609_comment'></div>岂如皇家，克迈古训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229609_comment'></div>广图书之府，每纵观乙夜之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229609_comment'></div>咨讲读之臣，俾更侍旰朝之燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229609_comment'></div>欲深求于治道，用博究于经言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229609_comment'></div>迄兹嗣德之兴，克对贻谋之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229609_comment'></div>虽当右武，不废用文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229609_comment'></div>横槊赋诗，笑魏君之非务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229609_comment'></div>正坐自讲，陋汉帝之好誇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229609_comment'></div>生知已极于高明，兼听犹资于鸿博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229609_comment'></div>宜图宿望，仰赞盛猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229609_comment'></div>若臣之愚，其孰曰可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229609_comment'></div>壮年一第，书粗涉而未通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229609_comment'></div>晚岁百罹，学久荒而弗殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229609_comment'></div>误尘近密，莫报恩知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229609_comment'></div>引疾投闲，盍使避严、徐之路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229609_comment'></div>执经入侍，顾容陪马、褚之游？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229609_comment'></div>眷宠则深，颠隮是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229609_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣由天纵，习与性成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229609_comment'></div>处万机之暇，而克慎厥修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229609_comment'></div>湛六经之言，而不闻他好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229609_comment'></div>验元龟于无逸，既自得师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229609_comment'></div>讲王度于祈招，畴堪待问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229609_comment'></div>夫何浅陋，亦与详延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229609_comment'></div>臣敢不祗服训辞，温寻旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229609_comment'></div>分章摘句，知粗辨于攸司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229609_comment'></div>补过尽忠，誓弗渝于所守。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1229609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年3月27日</a>　在钱塘，三月二十七日，草韩世忠制词。作品：《除韩世忠特授开府仪同三司依前武成感徳军节度使神武左军都统制充淮南东路宣抚使加食邑食实封制》<div id='poem_1229374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除韩世忠特授开府仪同三司依前武成感德军节度使神武左军都统制充淮南东西路宣抚使加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年3月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229374")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229374'>门下：朕负斧扆而惭域中之尊，孰与慰普天之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229374_comment'></div>披舆图而怀闑外之虑，其惟先推毂之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229374_comment'></div>乃眷虎臣，久从戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229374_comment'></div>高勋当报，兹隆开府之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229374_comment'></div>大任荐更，式倚干城之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229374_comment'></div>诞扬涣号，敷告治庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229374_comment'></div>太尉、武成感德军节度使、神武左军都统制、充淮南东西路宣抚使、南阳郡开国公、食邑二千五百户、食实封九百户韩世忠，英勇冠军，纯诚许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229374_comment'></div>摧锋陷阵，绩屡载于旂常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229374_comment'></div>受命忘家，心靡渝于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229374_comment'></div>顷宣威令，往殄寇攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229374_comment'></div>楼船南下而瓯粤为清，虽尝举褒崇之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229374_comment'></div>铁马西驰而荆湘继定，顾未酬俊伟之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229374_comment'></div>属已盛秋，方营严戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229374_comment'></div>廉颇居国，讵容邻壤之加兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229374_comment'></div>李绩守边，遂致敌人之远塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229374_comment'></div>少稽信赏，及此移屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229374_comment'></div>维江表之藩篱，任淮壖之屏翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229374_comment'></div>招徕失业，务绥抚于凋残；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229374_comment'></div>备御不虞，要防闲于侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229374_comment'></div>爰资宿望，用折遐冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229374_comment'></div>贵绝右班，既典五兵之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229374_comment'></div>宠仍双节，其联三事之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229374_comment'></div>予惟必践于前言，尔尚克图于来效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229374_comment'></div>载陪多赋，加食真封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229374_comment'></div>并昭进律之常，庸示旌功之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229374_comment'></div>威严夙著，信草木之知名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229374_comment'></div>号令增新，见旌旄之动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229374_comment'></div>繄中权之有赖，庶外侮之自消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229374_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229374_comment'></div>辅周则国必强，轻敌损威者惟汝之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229374_comment'></div>将能而君不御，临机制胜者惟汝之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229374_comment'></div>顾方略之如何，期功名之未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229374_comment'></div>往服予训，毋隳乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229374_comment'></div>可特授开府仪同三司、依前武成感德军节度使、神武左军都统制、淮南东西路安抚使，泗州置司，加食邑五百户、食实封三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229374_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1229374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年3月</a>　在钱塘，三月，草李擢诏。作品：《赐新除工部侍郎李擢辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除工部侍郎李擢辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229443")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229443'>敕李擢：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229443_comment'></div>朕惟为国之务，邪正必分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229443_comment'></div>用人所先，内外孰急？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229443_comment'></div>肆简论思之旧，俾迁侍从之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229443_comment'></div>卿华国有文，事君无隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229443_comment'></div>排宿奸于朋党蔽朝之际，德音甚明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229443_comment'></div>参书命于艰难践祚之初，典册具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229443_comment'></div>顷辞青琐，再易朱幡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229443_comment'></div>惟疾恶以如仇，故遭谗而屡绌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229443_comment'></div>察孤忠之可近，乃趣召以来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229443_comment'></div>顾文昌六职之联，共裨庶政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229443_comment'></div>而起部百工之事，姑试长才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229443_comment'></div>尚疾其驱，毋复坚避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229443_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229443_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在钱塘，春，草陈规诏。作品：《赐新除徽猷阁直学士依前知德安府陈规辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除徽猷阁直学士依前知德安府陈规辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229445")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229445'>敕陈规：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229445_comment'></div>朕惟赏当功则人情劝，名当实则爵秩重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229445_comment'></div>砺世之具，无以易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229445_comment'></div>卿秉心忠谊，更陟艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229445_comment'></div>远守孤城，兼提两郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229445_comment'></div>务农脩备，屡却重围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229445_comment'></div>载省勤劳，爰加进宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229445_comment'></div>峻升学士之职，俾为文吏之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229445_comment'></div>顾惟此迁，功实并当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229445_comment'></div>亟祗成命，毋复劳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229445_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229445_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229445_comment'></div>春暖，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229445_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年4月1日</a>　在钱塘，四月一日，有祈晴文。作品：《中天竺启建祈晴文》<div id='poem_1229842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中天竺启建祈晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229842")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229842'>维绍兴三年岁次癸丑四月丙戌朔日，皇帝遣入内内侍省东头供奉官、睿思殿掌书管簿杨立本，使僧四七人，于临安府中天竺寺灵感观音院开启祈晴道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229842_comment'></div>伏以时当长养，雨或霖霪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229842_comment'></div>蚕将老而畏寒，麦及秋而恐病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229842_comment'></div>惟生民所急，孰先衣食之原；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229842_comment'></div>而大士之尊，实制龙神之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229842_comment'></div>愿施圣力，亟扫顽阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229842_comment'></div>还天宇之清明，副人心之归向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229842_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年4月14日</a>　在钱塘，四月十四日，有文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后大祥奏告櫕宫表文》<div id='poem_1229813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后大祥奏告攒宫表文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年4月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229813")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229813'>臣某言：伏以丧期有既，嗟驷隙之难停；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229813_comment'></div>祥祭遽临，望柏城而增感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229813_comment'></div>恭惟昭慈献烈皇后功存神器，德被眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229813_comment'></div>礼虽尽于三年，恩则隆于万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229813_comment'></div>永言悲慕，罔克胜任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229813_comment'></div>谨差某官奉表奏告以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229813_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚惧顿首顿首谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1229813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年4月19日</a>　在钱塘，四月十九日，草孟忠厚制词。作品：《除孟忠厚特授依前起复镇潼军节度使开府仪同三司充醴泉观使特封信安郡王加食邑食实封制》<div id='poem_1229380' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229380' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229380?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除孟忠厚特授依前起复镇潼军节度使开府仪同三司充醴泉观使特封信安郡王加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229380")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229380_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229380'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229380'>门下：朕永怀先后，克保冲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229380_comment'></div>礼尽三年，既彻几筵之奉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229380_comment'></div>泽加九族，难酬社稷之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229380_comment'></div>维时姑侄之贤，宜极侯王之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229380_comment'></div>诞扬徽册，敷告治廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229380_comment'></div>起复镇潼军节度使、开府仪同三司、充醴泉观使、东海郡开国侯、食邑一千五百户、食实封七百户孟忠厚，好学有闻，立朝无玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229380_comment'></div>地兼居于贤戚，躬自励于材猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229380_comment'></div>仪于从班，茂献纳论思之益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229380_comment'></div>建兹戎节，闻诗书礼乐之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229380_comment'></div>避远要权，从容閒馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229380_comment'></div>方倚庐之衔恤，属中壸之缠哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229380_comment'></div>窆祔甫终，尝夺苴麻之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229380_comment'></div>褒崇已尽，并联衮黻之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229380_comment'></div>及此祥除，稽诸典故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229380_comment'></div>痛念音容之邈，遂隔中天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229380_comment'></div>欲隆骨肉之恩，莫如裂地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229380_comment'></div>乃相三吴之会、肇开异姓之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229380_comment'></div>载考济阳之始王，虽由元舅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229380_comment'></div>顾如隆祐之盛烈，特鲜近亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229380_comment'></div>蔽于朕心，用作尔祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229380_comment'></div>畴其多户，衍彼爰田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229380_comment'></div>以侈大于私门，庶尊安于帝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229380_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229380_comment'></div>樊宏著戒，明天道之好谦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229380_comment'></div>阴兴遗辞，欲后宗之知退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229380_comment'></div>追维慈训，常抑贪求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229380_comment'></div>其孰慰在天之灵，将尔实保家之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229380_comment'></div>往祗茂典，益勉令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229380_comment'></div>可特授依前起复镇潼军节度使、开府仪同三司、充醴泉观使，特封信安郡王，加食邑五百户、食实封三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229380_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1229380_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年5月</a>　在钱塘，五月，草宇文虚中诏。作品：《赐宇文虚中诏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年5月</a>　在钱塘，五月，草胡松年诏。作品：《赐新除工部尚书胡松年辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除工部尚书胡松年辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229493")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229493'>敕松年：省所奏，辞免工部尚书恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229493_comment'></div>昔晋惠公在秦，阴饴甥一言，而秦伯乃归晋君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229493_comment'></div>楚汉方争，侯生一说项王，而太公、吕后复还于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229493_comment'></div>今上天悔祸，强敌欲和，信使继通，约好在此，思得辨志之士、专对之才，如彼二人往焉，庶克谕回两宫，平定邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229493_comment'></div>选于在列，肆以属卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229493_comment'></div>乃闻慨然起任吾事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229493_comment'></div>惟忠谊有激于内，而几微不见于色，成功可必，朕用嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229493_comment'></div>中台常伯，班秩虽高，顾卿绵历二省，可以序进，朕意恨薄，尚何足辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229493_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229493_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229493_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年6月21日</a>　在钱塘，六月一日，上昭慈圣献皇后改谥议。作品：《昭慈圣献皇后改谥议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《昭慈圣献皇后改谥议》为佚文，今见于《历代名臣奏议》卷二八二、《中兴礼书》卷二五八。）</span><div id='poem_1229695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈圣献皇后谥议<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年六月二十一日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年6月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229695")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229695'>臣闻圣人之应世，方其绌身以退，藏于密则静而无为，晦而不彰，歛道德于一己，谢功名于当代，民无得而称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229695_comment'></div>及乎遭天下之变，履天下之危，智士失图，勇夫拱手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229695_comment'></div>当斯时也，汹汹者待我而后定，岌岌者待我而后安，则感焉而不得不为之应，迫焉而不得不为之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229695_comment'></div>于是起而赴之，不烦指麾，不动声色，而天地之位奠，日月之翳销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229695_comment'></div>神器丕基既偾而复兴，皇纲帝纪将绝而复续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229695_comment'></div>所谓变而克正，危而克扶者，收功于俄顷之间，而垂裕有无穷之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229695_comment'></div>非天下之至圣，其孰能与于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229695_comment'></div>鸿惟昭慈献烈皇后躬柔顺之资，蕴神明之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229695_comment'></div>起家而俪宸极，若固有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229695_comment'></div>释位而避宫闱，无可愧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229695_comment'></div>进退不失其正，造次不违于仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229695_comment'></div>此圣人之至德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229695_comment'></div>逮其遭变履危，从权济难，天意所属，人望如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229695_comment'></div>挈祖宗之统而亲授圣皇，除城社之妖而再还明辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229695_comment'></div>雍容房闼，计安邦家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229695_comment'></div>仓卒一时，利泽万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229695_comment'></div>此圣人之极功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229695_comment'></div>维德与功，咸本于「圣」，而容官累行，乃独阙焉，宜乎上心以为未足，而群工有司得以追议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229695_comment'></div>夫升高而望天地，不能穷其大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229695_comment'></div>当午而瞻日月，不能极其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229695_comment'></div>由盛德全功而观圣人，亦乌得而尽名之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229695_comment'></div>前日议者以明德有功曰「昭」，视民如子曰「慈」，聪明睿知曰「献」，安民有功曰「烈」，节是四惠，为应谥法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229695_comment'></div>先后之美，固兼有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229695_comment'></div>虽然，「昭」既主功，「慈」既主民，而又以「烈」配，不几于重复而言，若有所未至者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229695_comment'></div>是则无待于「烈」，而有阙于「圣」，烝尝之际，称谓之间，恐未足以对越神灵而下袪众惑，虽更议无嫌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229695_comment'></div>维我皇朝母后之懿，由汉以来，盖未之有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229695_comment'></div>慈圣光献皇后援立英祖，传序裕陵，再御帘帷，退安大养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229695_comment'></div>宣仁圣烈皇后拥佑哲宗，始终九载，元祐之政，至今称仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229695_comment'></div>钦圣宪肃皇后当元符末命，定策宫中，扶翊上皇，决于独断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229695_comment'></div>三后继踵，如相授受，是以徽称咸主夫圣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229695_comment'></div>昭慈献烈皇后逮事宣仁钦圣，率循妇道，取法母仪，丁时之艰，再安社稷，功齐德并，力则倍之，校美于兹，实同至圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229695_comment'></div>然则鸿名显号，极其推崇，虽舍是而有称焉，臣知天下后世臣子之心为未厌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229695_comment'></div>窃尝考之，上古之时，人道未立，穴居而野处，饮血而茹毛，盖夷狄禽兽如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229695_comment'></div>圣人者出，因时之宜，而致其利，使人知所生养，而无不足之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229695_comment'></div>于是人得自别于夷狄禽兽之群，而三纲五常之道兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229695_comment'></div>《易》之《系辞》曰：「备物致用，立成器以为天下利，莫大乎圣人言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229695_comment'></div>圣人之功，其大如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229695_comment'></div>虽然，圣人岂区区有心于造为者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229695_comment'></div>时适至是，不得不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229695_comment'></div>是故由其血食，而为之作罔罟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229695_comment'></div>由其粒食，而为之作耒耜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229695_comment'></div>以有无之不齐，则合之以市易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229695_comment'></div>以往来之不通，则济之以舟楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229695_comment'></div>至于服牛乘马，重门击柝，臼杵、弧矢、宫室、书契之用，凡一物之设、一器之制，取给天下之求而已，不自为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229695_comment'></div>后世之乱，故有甚于民无生养之初，而圣人之功，固有出而救之，如古昔之为天下利者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229695_comment'></div>由是推之，则先后之圣，可得而形容矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229695_comment'></div>当其失位而退处，视邦家之计，何所容心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229695_comment'></div>及夫时移而事变，应臣民之求，良非得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229695_comment'></div>于是时也，转盼之际，呼吸之间，存亡祸福所不可测，乃以柔弱之身，立危疑之地，重安龟鼎，再扶尊极，使祖宗旧物永有所传，圣人大宝永有所定，天下神器永有所归，元元之民，还戴吾宋，而弗沦于夷狄禽兽之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229695_comment'></div>然则备是物，成是器，以为利天下，方诸罔罟耒耜之作，不亦甚大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229695_comment'></div>由所建立，要其成功，虽以母后之圣，而上追牺农可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229695_comment'></div>彼涂山兴夏，文母造周，内助称贤，夫何足道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229695_comment'></div>按《谥法》：「备物成器曰圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229695_comment'></div>今群工有司之议更出于此，臣愚知不足以合天下之公愿，而仰契孝心追报之万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229695_comment'></div>昭慈献烈皇后尊谥，请以祖宗之命，改号曰「昭慈圣献皇后」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1229695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年6月</a>　在钱塘，六月，草吕颐浩诏。作品：《赐特进尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事吕颐浩辞免监修国史恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐特进尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事吕颐浩辞免监修国史恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229497")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229497'>敕颐浩：省所劄子奏，辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229497_comment'></div>自前世以来，致详史事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229497_comment'></div>人君之言动，则起居有注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229497_comment'></div>辅相之经纶，则时政有纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229497_comment'></div>授之秘府，日而历之，则著作有官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229497_comment'></div>此其槩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229497_comment'></div>顾宰相之职无所不统，矧左右史乃其所属，时政记乃其所行，而秘府三馆则又旧制所兼隶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229497_comment'></div>朕方深念，艰难之际，记事多缺，肆命攸司，举行厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229497_comment'></div>则委卿监总，固其宜耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229497_comment'></div>昔张说以旧相居边镇，即军中修史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229497_comment'></div>今虽戎马未息，军国务繁，卿独不能以庶政馀隙董成兹事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229497_comment'></div>一代大典，方以属卿，勉副朕怀，毋复谦避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229497_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229497_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年7月6日</a>　在钱塘，七月六日，告疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年7月22日</a>　在钱塘，七月二十二日，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐新除起复左宣奉大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事朱胜非赴行在诏》<div id='poem_1229396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除起复左宣奉大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事兼知枢密院事朱胜非赴行在诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年7月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229396")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229396'>敕朱胜非：卿任居次辅，时许真贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229396_comment'></div>对秉国钧，方赖有为之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229396_comment'></div>去丁家难，遽兴何怙之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229396_comment'></div>自即倚庐，遂虚大府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229396_comment'></div>念同心相与而共吾事，维二三臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229396_comment'></div>其一日不可以远朕躬，如左右手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229396_comment'></div>礼既更于卒哭，义斯得而夺情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229396_comment'></div>矧金革多虞，固有从戎之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229396_comment'></div>而邦家大计，难伸行服之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229396_comment'></div>乃孚号以扬庭，俾辍哀而居位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229396_comment'></div>尚其趣驾，副此虚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229396_comment'></div>已起复卿左宣奉大夫、守尚书右仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事，诏书到日，卿可乘递马疾速起发赴行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229396_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229396_comment'></div>秋热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229396_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年7月24日</a>　在钱塘，七月二十四日，诏命叔厚贴改陈与义所草朱胜非起复制词“兹宅大忧”四字为“方服私艰”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草谢克家诏。作品：《赐资政殿学士左中大夫谢克家辞免提举万寿观兼侍读恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐资政殿学士左中大夫谢克家辞免提举万寿观兼侍读恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229447")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229447'>敕克家：省所劄子奏，乞除一宫观差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229447_comment'></div>朕以忧勤之暇，纵观诗书执礼之言，顾惟閒燕所亲，必有直谅多闻之士，肆求鸿博，以副详延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229447_comment'></div>卿道学精深，性资端粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229447_comment'></div>尝入陪于大政，方移守于近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229447_comment'></div>属此来朝，载嘉敷奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229447_comment'></div>与其外更符竹，徒劳剧郡之烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229447_comment'></div>曷若留寘经帷，式款话言之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229447_comment'></div>弗縻吏职，俾食真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229447_comment'></div>韦、平之辅汉朝，本由经术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229447_comment'></div>褚、马之逢唐主，盖以耆儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229447_comment'></div>卿实兼之，人谁议者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229447_comment'></div>亟祗成命，毋饰谦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229447_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229447_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月1日</a>　在钱塘，九月一日，有祝文。作品：《昭慈献烈皇后改谥昭慈圣献皇后奉册宝告宗庙祝文》<div id='poem_1229819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229819?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭慈献烈皇后改谥曰昭慈圣献皇后奉册宝告宗庙祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229819")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229819_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229819'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229819'>维绍兴三年岁次癸丑某月朔日，孝曾孙嗣皇帝臣某，伏维昭慈献烈皇后改谥曰昭慈圣献皇后，谨遣某官奉谥册宝，敢昭告于僖祖立道肇基积德起功懿文宪武睿和至孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229819_comment'></div>伏以泰陵元配，隆后母仪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229819_comment'></div>两御帘帷，再安社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229819_comment'></div>事希古昔，勋在邦家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229819_comment'></div>尚惟累行之功，未极易名之懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229819_comment'></div>册乂新于徽称，庶克协于圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229819_comment'></div>今群工有司请以祖宗之命，改谥曰昭慈圣献皇后，不敢不告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229819_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229819_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229819'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1229819_0'>⑴ 哲宗皇帝祝文改云「伏以于皇世母，克保冲人」。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1229819_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月7日</a>　在钱塘，九月七日，草授吕颐浩旧节奉祠制词。作品：《除吕颐浩特授镇南军节度使开府仪同三司提举临安府洞霄宫加食邑食实封如故制》<div id='poem_1229377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除吕颐浩特授镇南军节度使开府仪同三司提举临安府洞霄宫食邑食实封如故制<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229377")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229377'>门下：王者崇德以报功，务极始终之遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229377_comment'></div>君子难进而易退，要明去就之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229377_comment'></div>若时元臣，久秉魁柄，方切仰成之意，遽披引疾之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229377_comment'></div>爰锡徽章，诞敷群听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229377_comment'></div>特进、尚书左仆射、同中书门下平章事、兼知枢密院事、领江淮荆浙都督诸军事、文安郡开国公、食邑五千五百户、食实封二千二百户吕颐浩，才周万变，望折遐冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229377_comment'></div>奋不顾身，仗天戈而济难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229377_comment'></div>忠以卫上，扶日毂以安行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229377_comment'></div>谊动神明，功存社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229377_comment'></div>用再登于台鼎，兹继阅以星霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229377_comment'></div>主调阴阳，觊天心之克享；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229377_comment'></div>典正法度，期王化之复行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229377_comment'></div>备观夙夜之勤，莫测灾祥之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229377_comment'></div>骇人言之归咎，指国政之失平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229377_comment'></div>朕则责躬，乡胡辞位？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229377_comment'></div>览叠陈于恳款，良感予怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229377_comment'></div>欲终保其功名，重违乃志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229377_comment'></div>姑解钧衡之极任，还兼将相之崇资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229377_comment'></div>拥节旧邦，奉祠閒馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229377_comment'></div>盖闵劳于机务，庶均逸于耆英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229377_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229377_comment'></div>从赤松之游，卿岂遽遗于世事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229377_comment'></div>申丹书之信，朕将差定于勋盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229377_comment'></div>尚勉令猷，永膺遐福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229377_comment'></div>可特授镇南军节度使、开府仪同三司、提举临安府洞霄宫，食邑、食实封、封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229377_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1229377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月21日</a>　在钱塘，九月二十一日，诏叔厚草诏赐刘光世、韩世忠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月24日</a>　在钱塘，九月二十四日，草成刘光世制。作品：《赐新除江东淮西路宣抚使刘光世诏》<div id='poem_1229400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除江东淮西路宣抚使刘光世诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229400")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229400'>敕光世：朕惟吴越之区，既留警跸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229400_comment'></div>江淮之险，宜植藩篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229400_comment'></div>顾贵池、姑熟之津，直下蔡、历阳之会，接九江之冲要，临建业之上游，分宿重兵，是资伟望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229400_comment'></div>眷予勋旧，深体艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229400_comment'></div>闻指意以具孚，请从移戍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229400_comment'></div>驰封章而来上，曾靡告劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229400_comment'></div>卿能若斯，朕复何虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229400_comment'></div>载嘉恭顺，深动叹咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229400_comment'></div>惟孝于亲，则必扬后世之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229400_comment'></div>惟忠于君，则当徇公家之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229400_comment'></div>此中外安危之计，属卿二三将帅之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229400_comment'></div>情若弟兄，毋蓄阋墙之怨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229400_comment'></div>义均寮寀，共输许国之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229400_comment'></div>所期戮力以同心，用克折冲而御侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229400_comment'></div>丹青不朽，将并列于云台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229400_comment'></div>带砺弗渝，亦咸书于盟府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229400_comment'></div>乃所望也，岂不韪欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229400_comment'></div>已除卿江东淮西两路宣抚使，池州置司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229400_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229400_comment'></div>秋冷，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229400_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1229400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月24日</a>　在钱塘，九月二十四日，草成韩世忠制。作品：《赐新除镇江府建康府淮南东路宣抚使韩世忠诏》<div id='poem_1229402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除镇江府建康府淮南东路宣抚使韩世忠诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229402")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229402'>敕世忠：朕惟时以戒寒，守当严备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229402_comment'></div>循江流而镇险，顾力散以难周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229402_comment'></div>联形胜以宿师，则势专而易应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229402_comment'></div>眷升、润东西之府，据江淮南北之冲，走集所趋，舳舻交会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229402_comment'></div>封疆之接，鸡犬相闻，曾无数舍之遥，奚假两军之重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229402_comment'></div>乃命江东之戍，更涖池阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229402_comment'></div>遂因京口之屯，并临建邺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229402_comment'></div>仍资威望，分控长淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229402_comment'></div>惟卿勇不顾身，忠无择事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229402_comment'></div>宽其分部，庶能展足以赴功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229402_comment'></div>睦乃比邻，尚克同心而济务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229402_comment'></div>念国家之至计，繄将相之协恭，勉就大勋，毋怀小忿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229402_comment'></div>譬犹捕鹿，要为犄角之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229402_comment'></div>有若献豜，皆获公私之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229402_comment'></div>往体朕意，伫观厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229402_comment'></div>已除卿镇江、建康府、淮南东路宣抚使，镇江府置司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229402_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229402_comment'></div>秋冷，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229402_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1229402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草吕颐浩诏。作品：《赐观文殿大学士提举临安府洞霄宫吕颐浩辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐观文殿大学士提举临安府洞霄宫吕颐浩辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1229495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229495'>敕颐浩：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229495_comment'></div>卿事朕艰难，为时勋业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229495_comment'></div>三陟蒙司之峻，亦既累年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229495_comment'></div>再辞魁柄之崇，宜加异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229495_comment'></div>迫人言之荐至，怅朕意之莫伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229495_comment'></div>收建旄开府之仪，更秘殿隆儒之职，用宠光于故弼，俾休逸于殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229495_comment'></div>终始厚恩，应识保全之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229495_comment'></div>优游晚岁，毋忘兢慎之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229495_comment'></div>其即钦承，尚奚逊避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229495_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229495_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229495_comment'></div>秋冷，卿比平安好？<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年9月</a>　在钱塘，九月，草李擢诏。作品：《赐尚书工部侍郎兼权侍讲李擢乞除僻小一郡或在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229444' class='poemTitle </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229444")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229444'>敕李擢：省奏，乞除一僻小郡或在外宫观差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229444_comment'></div>朕求士虽广，用人敢轻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229444_comment'></div>除目甫行，待佥谐而得下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229444_comment'></div>周行并进，察众好而始安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229444_comment'></div>仅有获焉，可谓艰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229444_comment'></div>如卿艺文之富，议论之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229444_comment'></div>卓尔不群，高映一时之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229444_comment'></div>慨然有意，每怀当世之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229444_comment'></div>还寘近严，是资裨益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229444_comment'></div>勉摅素蕴，毋惑他虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229444_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在钱塘，秋，草宇文虚中诏。作品：《草宇文虚中诏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年10月</a>　在钱塘，十月，草洪拟诏。作品：《赐新除徽猷阁直学士提举江州太平观洪拟辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229453' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_1229453_comment'></div>卿仕阅四朝，位登八座，外历专城之寄，中更持橐之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229453_comment'></div>迨此请闲，可无加宠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229453_comment'></div>寓西清之禁直，仍列从班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229453_comment'></div>贲学士之荣名，式彰儒效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229449_comment'></div>朕以伋学蚤传家，允为令器，仕能举职，尝摄名郎，乃由司属之联，俾正列星之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229449_comment'></div>是惟才选，宜以序升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229449_comment'></div>甫嘉济美之贤，遽览辞荣之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229449_comment'></div>念前载教忠之谊，固将勉其事君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229449_comment'></div>稽昔人举善之公，犹靡嫌于称子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229449_comment'></div>矧卿久离政地，方领闲官；<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年12月</a>　在钱塘，十二月，草朱胜非诏。作品：《赐朱胜非辞免监修国史命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐朱胜非辞免监修国史命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229414")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229414'>敕胜非：省所劄子奏，辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229414_comment'></div>自艰难以来，乱靡有定，史牒散落，干戈岁兴，未遑编削之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229414_comment'></div>虽载笔赤墀，属书东观，官存其名，而漫不举职，朕甚悯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229414_comment'></div>夫君举必书，善恶不隐，所以垂训于后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229414_comment'></div>今阙无所记者几年矣，久或失传，后将奚考？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229414_comment'></div>若事有过举，言有失中，而不见其迹，朕亦于何而自鉴耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229414_comment'></div>是用申饬厥官，趣行记录，而属吾相臣，以董成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229414_comment'></div>惟卿学冠古今，资兼才识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229414_comment'></div>从朕初载，以迄于今，顾其阅历之详、笔削之善，取正多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229414_comment'></div>勉副朕志，何以辞为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229414_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229414_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在钱塘，冬，草郑滋诏。作品：《赐左朝议大夫试尚书吏部侍郎郑滋乞除知州或外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229433' class='poemTitle </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229433")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229433'>敕郑滋：省三省进呈所乞除知州差遣或在外宫观一次，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229433_comment'></div>卿蚤以美才，发闻庠序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229433_comment'></div>出入侍从，见谓老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229433_comment'></div>召自远方，历跻省户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229433_comment'></div>允赖清通之目，庶几铨序之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229433_comment'></div>曾未期年，方观成绩，胡为引疾，遽欲外迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229433_comment'></div>宰辅以闻，殊非朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229433_comment'></div>顾政事外修之际，惟人材难得之忧，姑安厥官，毋怀谦退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229433_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年1月15日</a>　在钱塘，一月十五日，草赵士㒟诏。作品：《赐检校少保光山军节度使知大宗正事士㒟乞收叙衔在令畤下允诏》<div id='poem_1229405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐检校少保光山军节度使知大宗正事士袅乞收叙衔在令畤下允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1229405_comment'></div>卿蚤建戚藩，久司属籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229405_comment'></div>蔼亲贤之雅望，播在搢绅；<div class='inline' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>面对第一劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229649")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229649'>臣观近者金人议和，托言刘豫所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229649_comment'></div>虽敌情叵信，然而中原残破，民力困瘁，不堪驱役，豫、麟父子特倚金人为重，以拒王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229649_comment'></div>如闻敌自有故，且倦于南牧，则议出于豫，欲款吾问罪之举，延旦夕之命，理亦或然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229649_comment'></div>今敌人遣使先至豫所乃来，而所持书辄有封疆之画，其为豫计无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229649_comment'></div>陛下灼见其情，报书曲折，事理详尽，固应夺其狡谋，破其奸胆，不复敢肆桀骜，庶能听顺，以定和约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229649_comment'></div>然而犹可虑者，万一负恃彊敌，尚怀逆图，必欲窥吾境土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229649_comment'></div>或恐稽留使人，呼敌骑以来邀胁，则吾可以不为之备乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229649_comment'></div>今已过防秋，且远近传闻通使，人情恐便舒缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229649_comment'></div>臣愚欲望圣慈申戒沿江将帅明远斥候，防扼险要，选练士卒，日训于师，常如遇敌，以为先事之备，庶无后悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229649_comment'></div>苟和议遂成，亦未可以弛备，况今日耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229649_comment'></div>臣过计如此，惟陛下裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229649_comment'></div>取进止<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229649_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1229649'>年月原无，据《建炎以来系年要录》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229649'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229649_0'>⑴ 《北海集》卷二八。又见《建炎以来系年要录》卷七二。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1229649_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1229650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>面对第二劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229650")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229650'>臣伏观陛下惩彊敌之侵凌，念两宫之阻远，不惮卑词以通使，屈己以议和，上以为宗庙社稷灵长之计，下以息海内元元战伐之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229650_comment'></div>至诚交感，异类革心，甚盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229650_comment'></div>然以臣愚私窃度之，如陛下神圣之资、英武之略，内有拨乱之志，而乃郁郁居此，忍自卑屈，以求成请好，岂得已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229650_comment'></div>徒以事势未竞，国步未夷，生民未安，故为计出此，庶几天诱其衷，还我二圣，休兵蓄力，徐为后图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229650_comment'></div>非谓旧事可忘，中国可弃，敌情可信，能恃以久安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229650_comment'></div>然则约和之后，便欲高枕而卧，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229650_comment'></div>仰惟圣志，固将大有所为，兴起庶政，观时俟衅，期复旧业，不唯苟纾目前之急而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229650_comment'></div>臣愿陛下坚坐薪尝胆之志，励宵衣旰食之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229650_comment'></div>深诏大臣简贤能、慎名器、明殿最、严赏罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229650_comment'></div>申饬百执事之列，下至州县之吏，各修厥官，毋敢媮堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229650_comment'></div>革因循之弊，去苟且之习，要使人人公心为国，诚意在民，而无养资尸禄、计日待迁之患，则众治举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229650_comment'></div>于是生财积谷，缮甲治兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229650_comment'></div>啬用度，宽赋歛，以实民力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229650_comment'></div>汰冗弱，精选练，以作士气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229650_comment'></div>日伸月长，假以岁年，一旦起而用之，则大计可图，成功可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229650_comment'></div>顾惟今日权宜之议，所利在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229650_comment'></div>昔周宣复古，盖以内修政事，外攘夷狄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229650_comment'></div>越之报吴，亦曰「十年生聚，十年教训」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229650_comment'></div>兹非往事之明验，而陛下之所熟闻者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229650_comment'></div>伏望陛下不以臣言为腐儒常谈，留神而勉勉焉，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229650_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1229650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年1月27日</a>　在钱塘，一月二十七日，草赵鼎诏。作品：《赐端明殿学士左朝奉大夫江南西路安抚大使兼知洪州赵鼎赴行在诏》<div id='poem_1229395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐端明殿学士左朝奉大夫江南西路安抚大使兼知洪州赵鼎赴行在诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229395")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229395'>敕赵鼎：卿以忠纯无隐之诚，鲠亮不回之操，张明纲纪，风宪为尊，密勿枢机，话言犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229395_comment'></div>顷就閒于真馆，荐倚重于藩符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229395_comment'></div>政洽群情，军民各得其所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229395_comment'></div>威闻四境，盗贼不窥其封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229395_comment'></div>惟显绩之既彰，知远猷之可赖，肆更召节，趣奉觐圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229395_comment'></div>朕方渴想于仪形，卿亦得披其心腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229395_comment'></div>行无俟驾，宁辞趋命之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229395_comment'></div>见不以时，伫副虚怀之访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229395_comment'></div>已降指挥，权交安抚大使司职事并州事曾纡，诏书到日，可乘递马速疾起发赴行在奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229395_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229395_comment'></div>春暖，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229395_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年1月</a>　在钱塘，一月，草章谊诏。作品：《赐新除龙图阁学士依前枢密院都承旨章谊辞免恩命不允诏》《赐新除龙图阁直学士章谊再辞免恩命不允诏》《赐龙图阁学士左中大夫枢密院都承旨充大金国军前通问使章谊辞免特赐起发钱一千贯银绢二百疋两恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除龙图阁学士依前枢密院都承旨章谊辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229440")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229440'>敕章谊：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229440_comment'></div>朕闻古者以礼使臣，量才授职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229440_comment'></div>礼不备，则是待人以犬马；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229440_comment'></div>才不称，则将假人以器名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229440_comment'></div>缓急何由而尽心，爵禄亦无以励世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229440_comment'></div>谨守兹戒，朕焉敢私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229440_comment'></div>卿学粹而通经，识明而知务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229440_comment'></div>贰剧曹于兰省，承密旨于枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229440_comment'></div>左右其宜，周旋匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229440_comment'></div>欲加烦使，爰锡徽章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229440_comment'></div>顾内阁之联，河图为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229440_comment'></div>而学士之选，寓直则轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229440_comment'></div>俾超缀于新班，用增华于旧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229440_comment'></div>盖将有待，尚何可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229440_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229440_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229440_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除龙图阁直学士章谊再辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229441")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229441'>敕章谊：省所奏再辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229441_comment'></div>朕以强敌欲和，择才充使，必得一时之隽，继图二国之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229441_comment'></div>顾孰可行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229441_comment'></div>独卿称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229441_comment'></div>肆分朌于宠渥，以显示于光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229441_comment'></div>苟怀利事君，卿固所当戒者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229441_comment'></div>而不遑将母，朕其何以慰之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229441_comment'></div>况延阁之序迁，亦从班之常数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229441_comment'></div>惟朝廷之爵禄，本以劝功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229441_comment'></div>体臣下之勤劳，可无加礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229441_comment'></div>亟祗成命，勿复固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229441_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229441_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229441_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐龙图阁学士左中大夫枢密院都承旨充大金国军前通问使章谊辞免特赐起发钱一千贯银绢二百疋两恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229442")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229442'>敕章谊：省所奏，辞免特赐钱一千贯、银绢二百疋两恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229442_comment'></div>卿暂远亲颜，出从王事，靡见几微之色，备闻激切之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229442_comment'></div>然自历修途，既有赍装之费；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229442_comment'></div>而还观私室，岂无服用之需？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229442_comment'></div>载轸朕怀，是加兹锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229442_comment'></div>初非妄予，奚足深辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229442_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229442_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月21日</a>　在钱塘，二月二十一日，兼史馆修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月</a>　在钱塘，二月，有辞免兼史馆修撰奏状。作品：《辞免兼史馆修撰奏状》<div id='poem_1229666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼史馆修撰奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229666")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229666'>臣伏准敕命，差臣兼史馆修撰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229666_comment'></div>臣窃见陛下躬上圣之资，建中兴之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229666_comment'></div>经营图治，七年于兹，拨乱反正，功德甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229666_comment'></div>而史家之历，阙而不书，非帝王所以垂训之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229666_comment'></div>乃因有司之请，设局命官，付以兹事，惟择所逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229666_comment'></div>盖将课其编纂之功，而程其述作之能，不徒苟以一职荣之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229666_comment'></div>如臣固陋有素，加以病昏，聪明不及于前，学术寖忘其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229666_comment'></div>久尘法从，无补皇猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229666_comment'></div>盖尝三贡封章，祈解近职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229666_comment'></div>恩私隆厚，未忍弃捐，黾勉备官，进退惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229666_comment'></div>今以衰残之质，使其摛文词禁，劝学经帷，常惧弗给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229666_comment'></div>而况一代笔削之重，敢复冒昧贪荣，而兼斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229666_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察其不逮，追寝误恩，别选作者，庶协公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229666_comment'></div>所有敕命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229666_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年2月26日</a>　在钱塘，二月二十六日，有青词。作品：《徽州天庆观奉安圣像告圣祖天尊大帝青词》<div id='poem_1229806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州天庆观奉安圣像奏告圣祖天尊大帝青词<span class='inlineComment2'>（二月二十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年2月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229806")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229806'>维绍兴四年二月朔日，嗣皇帝谨遣某官于徽州天庆观，以某月日奉安圣像，奏告圣祖天尊大帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229806_comment'></div>伏以授策先皇，尝觌飙游之降；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229806_comment'></div>朝真庶国，可忘馆御之修？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229806_comment'></div>乃眷殊庭，载严宝像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229806_comment'></div>将因良日，祗奉睟容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229806_comment'></div>尚克顾临，用光昭荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229806_comment'></div>无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229806_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229806'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229806_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年3月</a>　在钱塘，三月，草赵鼎诏。作品：《赐新除参知政事赵鼎辞免恩命乞改除一在外宫观差遣不允诏》<div id='poem_1229422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除参知政事赵鼎辞免恩命乞改除一在外宫观差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229422")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229422'>敕赵鼎：省所劄子奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229422_comment'></div>朕以临政之未明，求贤而自辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229422_comment'></div>深戒取人之失，选于众而敢轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229422_comment'></div>永怀用旧之宜，简诸心而素定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229422_comment'></div>率由公听，庶协佥谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229422_comment'></div>卿以直道正言，历跻宪府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229422_comment'></div>以嘉谋硕画，尝赞筹帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229422_comment'></div>名声推重于朝廷，风采耸闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229422_comment'></div>属虚近弼，思究远猷，乃趣召于帅藩，俾参陪于国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229422_comment'></div>惟君臣之遇合，昔以为难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229422_comment'></div>而政事之图维，今尤匪易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229422_comment'></div>卿方得位，朕所委心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229422_comment'></div>勉戮力于治功，毋执谦于辞逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229422_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229422_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在钱塘，春，草刘洪道奖谕诏。作品：《赐徽猷阁直学士降授左中奉大夫知鄂州荆湖北路安抚使刘洪道奖谕诏》<div id='poem_1229407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐徽猷阁直学士降授左中奉大夫知鄂州荆湖北路安抚使刘洪道奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229407")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229407'>敕洪道：省所荆湖北路监司奏：「契勘本路州累年以来，屡经剧寇焚劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229407_comment'></div>自帅臣刘洪道到任以来，方始措画，整治军旅，张大声势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229407_comment'></div>即今沿流上下，并皆宁肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229407_comment'></div>客旅舟船，渐见通快；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229407_comment'></div>远近居民，各已安妥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229407_comment'></div>鼎澧道路，文移往来，悉无限碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229407_comment'></div>措置已向就绪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229407_comment'></div>事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229407_comment'></div>朕惟荆汉之地，鞠为盗区，荒芜连城，白骨蔽野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229407_comment'></div>眷焉西顾，焚灼于怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229407_comment'></div>谋帅属卿，往图绥定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229407_comment'></div>果能为朕，宽忧一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229407_comment'></div>军声既张，鼠窃自遁，叛亡降附，奸宄寖销，道梗复清，江流无壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229407_comment'></div>事滋就绪，民若更生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229407_comment'></div>究观设施，咸有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229407_comment'></div>使者言状，朕甚嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229407_comment'></div>故兹奖谕，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229407_comment'></div>春寒，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229407_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1229407_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在钱塘，春，草王绹诏。作品：《赐资政殿大学士左中大夫知绍兴府王绹乞除依旧外任宫观不允诏》《赐资政殿大学士左中大夫知绍兴府王绹再乞除依旧外任宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐资政殿大学士左中大夫知绍兴府王绹乞除依旧外任宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229438")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229438'>敕王绹：省所劄子奏，乞除依旧外任宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229438_comment'></div>朕惟方面之地，势有轻重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229438_comment'></div>股肱之臣，义同休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229438_comment'></div>眷彼近邦之要，属于旧辅之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229438_comment'></div>列辟视其表仪，行朝倚为根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229438_comment'></div>方资镇静，得缓顾忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229438_comment'></div>乃贡需章，愿休閒馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229438_comment'></div>虽雅怀知止，自安身退之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229438_comment'></div>然多士闻风，孰共时艰之虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229438_comment'></div>矧神明之尚壮，且条教之既孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229438_comment'></div>毋复告劳，为予卧治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229438_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229438_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229438_comment'></div>春暖，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐资政殿大学士左中大夫知绍兴府王绹再乞除依旧外任宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229439")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229439'>敕王绹：省所再上劄子奏，乞除依旧宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229439_comment'></div>朕以天时少康，边候无警，方内修于庶政，其力复于丕基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229439_comment'></div>虽纪律设张，本朝廷而出治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229439_comment'></div>然诏条宣布，繄郡邑之承流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229439_comment'></div>维彼近藩，属吾旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229439_comment'></div>正有赖同心之助，乃继陈引疾之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229439_comment'></div>若耆宿大臣，咸欲奉身而去事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229439_comment'></div>则疏远下吏，孰肯捐躯而赴功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229439_comment'></div>卿犹服勤，人敢自逸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229439_comment'></div>矧师庭安静，初无戎务之繁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229439_comment'></div>而郡政宽平，已见民心之悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229439_comment'></div>但资坐啸，何至贤劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229439_comment'></div>朕意不移，卿辞无费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229439_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229439_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229439_comment'></div>春暖，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229439_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1229439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年4月1日</a>　在钱塘，四月一日，有青词。作品：《徽州天庆观奉安圣祖天尊大帝圣像青词》<div id='poem_1229807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州天庆观奉安圣祖天尊大帝圣像青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1229807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229807'>维绍兴四年四月朔日，嗣皇帝臣谨差某官，于徽州天庆观奉安圣祖天尊大帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229807_comment'></div>伏以仙源所自，皇祚有开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229807_comment'></div>生而神灵，既禀在躬之盛德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229807_comment'></div>施于子孙，用昭受命之珍符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229807_comment'></div>示现之祥，延鸿可卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229807_comment'></div>属新像设，虔奉真游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229807_comment'></div>尚希肸蚃之通，永格和平之应。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1229807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229807'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229807_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年4月</a>　在钱塘，四月，草徐俯诏。作品：《赐端明殿学士左中大夫新除提举临安府洞霄宫徐俯辞免依旧职名不允诏》<div id='poem_1229460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐端明殿学士左中大夫新除提举临安府洞霄宫徐俯辞免依旧职名不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229460")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229460'>敕徐俯：省所奏劄子，辞免依旧职名，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229460_comment'></div>朕惟功名之士乐朝廷，高尚之人轻轩冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229460_comment'></div>用之弗及，则琬琰有煨尘之叹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229460_comment'></div>去而不顾，则山林无廊庙之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229460_comment'></div>盖出处之累，靡留于心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229460_comment'></div>故荣悴之情，莫见于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229460_comment'></div>卿之遇合，朕所简知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229460_comment'></div>有不得于重轻之间，遂自决于进退之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229460_comment'></div>身已江湖之远，名奚禁殿之嫌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229460_comment'></div>往体眷怀，毋烦谦逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229460_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229460_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1229460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月1日</a>　在钱塘，五月一日，有祈晴文。作品：《下天竺寺启建祈晴文》<div id='poem_1229843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>下天竺寺启建祈晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼",
