class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229843'>维绍兴四年岁次甲寅五月朔日，皇帝遣某官，于临安府下天竺寺启建祈晴道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229843_comment'></div>伏以公私之计，既寡盖藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229843_comment'></div>水旱之虞，动关念虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229843_comment'></div>属兹苦雨，害彼力田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229843_comment'></div>三日成霖，乃逾期而未止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229843_comment'></div>六师仰哺，则望岁之未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229843_comment'></div>孰宽否德之忧，盖仗能仁之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229843_comment'></div>式投净宇，恭启清场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229843_comment'></div>愿回慧日之光，亟扫积阴之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229843_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月8日</a>　在钱塘，五月八日，纂修建炎元年以来日历。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月9日</a>　在钱塘，五月九日，以言者论词臣失职，与陈与义、张纲上书待罪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月12日</a>　在钱塘，五月十二日，草赵士㒟诏。作品：《赐检校少保光山军节度使司知大宗正事士㒟乞罢宗正职事除一外任宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐检校少保光山军节度使司知大宗正事士袅乞罢宗正职事除一外任宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229435")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229435'>敕士袅：省所劄子奏，乞罢宗正职事，除一外任宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229435_comment'></div>卿顷以宗英，典兹属籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229435_comment'></div>方敌师之大入，率近族以南迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229435_comment'></div>隔阔五年，流离万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229435_comment'></div>谅备更于艰险，每深念于勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229435_comment'></div>幸此小康，载加趣召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229435_comment'></div>嘉介圭之来觐，览需奏之上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229435_comment'></div>愿解攸司，少休閒馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229435_comment'></div>顾忧未忘于多垒，则势有重于维城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229435_comment'></div>欲彰惇睦之风，正赖表仪之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229435_comment'></div>勉安乃职，庸副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229435_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229435_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月</a>　在钱塘，五月，草范冲诏。作品：《赐参知政事赵鼎乞罢范冲宗正少卿直史馆除命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐参知政事赵鼎乞罢范冲宗正少卿直史馆除命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229424")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229424'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229424'>敕赵鼎：省所劄子奏：「新除宗正少卿、直史馆范冲系臣姻家，伏望罢冲除命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229424_comment'></div>事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229424_comment'></div>朕惟神宗、哲宗两朝史录更京、卞之手，笔削是非，多其私意，传之后世，实损盛德，方诏有司，俾加更定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229424_comment'></div>载念当时直笔之臣今皆逝矣，而祖禹之子在，遗范未泯，召用为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229424_comment'></div>矧列职宗卿，乃其旧物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229424_comment'></div>而䌷书史馆，则彼世官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229424_comment'></div>断于朕心，可因卿废？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229424_comment'></div>昔祁奚内举犹不避子，而祐甫除吏亦多所亲，顾今事匪自卿，夫何嫌者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229424_comment'></div>勉循公道，毋执谦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229424_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229424_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月12日</a>　在钱塘，六月十二日，乞追寝韩世忠所藏御书赐阁名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月</a>　在钱塘，六月，草胡松年诏。作品：《赐左朝奉大夫试吏部尚书兼侍讲胡松年乞除一在外宫观不允诏》<div id='poem_1229425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐左朝奉大夫试吏部尚书兼侍讲胡松年乞除一在外宫观不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229425")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229425'>敕松年：省所奏乞除一在外宫观，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229425_comment'></div>卿以通方之学，周物之才，历事三朝，越跻八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229425_comment'></div>奉輶轩之使，而君命不辱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229425_comment'></div>冠从橐之班，而时论尽倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229425_comment'></div>方坐执于铨衡，且入陪于劝讲，实资策虑，以济艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229425_comment'></div>顾夙夜之宣劳，偶阴阳之爽裕，俾从优告，宜即有瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229425_comment'></div>毋辞曳履之勤，难徇抗章之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229425_comment'></div>所请宜不允，仍给宽假将理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229425_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229425_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在钱塘，夏，草吴玠诏。作品：《赐检校少保定国军节度使川陜宣抚副使吴玠辞免新除少保恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐检校少保定国军节度使川陕宣抚副使吴玠辞免新除少保恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229450")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229450'>敕吴玠：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229450_comment'></div>卿勇略无前，威名有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229450_comment'></div>挐兵百战，每闻三捷之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229450_comment'></div>捍寇四川，独倚一军之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229450_comment'></div>隐如敌国，贤甚长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229450_comment'></div>自建将旄，载更岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229450_comment'></div>四举旌劳之典，爰颁进律之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229450_comment'></div>增贲元戎，升华亚保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229450_comment'></div>是姑从于常数，方继册于茂勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229450_comment'></div>其即钦承，毋多辞逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229450_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229450_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229450_comment'></div>夏热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229450_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月9日</a>　在钱塘，七月九日，草吴玠制词。作品：《除吴玠特授检校少师奉寜保静军节度使依前川陕宣抚副使进封建安郡开国侯加食邑食实封制》<div id='poem_1229371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除吴玠特授检校少师奉宁保静军节度使依前川陕宣抚副使进封建安郡开国侯加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229371")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229371'>门下：朕躬临江表，虑在坤维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229371_comment'></div>陆海神皋，既失秦川之利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229371_comment'></div>铜梁、剑阁，敢言蜀道之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229371_comment'></div>属予屏翰之良，扼彼关山之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229371_comment'></div>连摧巨敌，继上殊勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229371_comment'></div>将大耸于师瞻，用显颁于廷号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229371_comment'></div>检校少保、定国军节度使、川陕宣抚副使、建安郡开国侯、食邑一千五百户、食实封六百户吴玠，沉雄而先计，壮决而尚谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229371_comment'></div>结发戎行，勇气夙闻于绝塞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229371_comment'></div>建牙方面，威名自折于遐冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229371_comment'></div>顷典护军，尝资捍敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229371_comment'></div>据其胜地，初营原上之屯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229371_comment'></div>克彼全师，悉殄目中之寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229371_comment'></div>能保四川之固，尽凭一战之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229371_comment'></div>何忿戾之罔悛，尚窥觎而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229371_comment'></div>维此杀金之役，实当全蜀之蹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229371_comment'></div>豫料敌情，逆为战备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229371_comment'></div>交锋百斗，尝以逸而待劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229371_comment'></div>捣垒四攻，乃用寡而覆众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229371_comment'></div>酋渠各遁，党类几歼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229371_comment'></div>载嘉三捷之闻，独赖一军之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229371_comment'></div>方趣第战多之赏，肆稍稽国典之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229371_comment'></div>制在中权，顾孰先于主帅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229371_comment'></div>位升左棘，俾首视于孤卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229371_comment'></div>加两镇之节旄，盛元戎之仪物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229371_comment'></div>肇开公社，并衍圭腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229371_comment'></div>以侈大于俊功，以昭明于褒律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229371_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229371_comment'></div>懋贤贤之道，名遂亚于师臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229371_comment'></div>恢将将之模，任亦兼于连帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229371_comment'></div>往钦服命，思广尔庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229371_comment'></div>斯西鄙之载宁，觊中原之可定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229371_comment'></div>繄乃忠力，岂烦训言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229371_comment'></div>可特授检校少师、奉宁保静军节度使，依前川陕宣抚副使，进封安定郡开国侯，加食邑五百户、食实封二百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229371_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1229371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月11日</a>　在钱塘，七月十一日，进待罪奏状。作品：《待罪奏状》<div id='poem_1229669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>待罪奏状<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年七月十一日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229669")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229669'>臣今月十日，学士院准尚书劄子：臣寮上言，臣所草吴玠麻制有曰：「陆海神皋，既失秦川之利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229669_comment'></div>铜梁剑阁，敢言蜀道之难」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229669_comment'></div>以「秦川」字有疑，及不识「敢言」之义何谓，乞改正行下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229669_comment'></div>奉圣旨：令学士贴改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229669_comment'></div>臣已遵依圣旨贴改讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229669_comment'></div>缘臣识虑不明，语言失当，因臣寮所论，始见其非，不职之辜，其何可逭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229669_comment'></div>臣见在病假，居家待罪，伏望圣慈特赐黜责施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229669_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1229669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，乞宫观。作品：《乞宫观奏状》<div id='poem_1229670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞宫观奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229670")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229670'>臣辄沥危恳，上渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229670_comment'></div>臣一介孤生，遭遇明圣，服在侍从，首尾七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229670_comment'></div>昨缘病衰，屡求閒外，恩私未憖，获畀近藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229670_comment'></div>到官五旬，即闻海道之警，淮甸俶扰，远近戒严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229670_comment'></div>戍辂亲征，六师既发，浙东心腹之地，形势顿孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229670_comment'></div>臣职在抚绥，实分忧寄，虽随事加备，力岂足支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229670_comment'></div>仰赖陛下神武英决，伐谋制胜，将士用命，贼计遂穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229670_comment'></div>臣既恃而不恐，因一切安之以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229670_comment'></div>洎敌众远遁，法驾凯还，一路军民，讫皆安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229670_comment'></div>向非王师却敌，江上用克无虞，臣之么么，其将何以塞责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229670_comment'></div>方朝廷儆戒，为盛秋捍御之防，将相协同，图中原恢复之策，小大臣子，咸思自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229670_comment'></div>而臣抱疾寖久，老境日侵，臂痛指挛，胸满气急，目视昏近，怯理簿书，精力疲乏，难周职务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229670_comment'></div>重以陛辞之日，训戒丁宁，事无钜细，皆躬亲省阅，不敢委之僚属，以偷安自暇，姑欲彊勉夙夜，图报毫分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229670_comment'></div>而其惫如此，一有旷弛，宁不上误陛下使令之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229670_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣情悃，实怀此忧，非敢无名辞难避事，特降睿旨，除臣一在外宫观差遣，任便居住，使得专意医药，以养残年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229670_comment'></div>改命能臣，付之方面，庶几公私义分，两得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229670_comment'></div>傥沉痾之有瘳，岂捐躯之无日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229670_comment'></div>臣不胜俯伏俟罪、激切拳拳之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1229670'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草汪藻诏。作品：《赐龙图阁直学士左朝请大夫知湖州汪藻再乞除在外宫观差遣不允诏》<div id='poem_1229430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐龙图阁直学士左朝请大夫知湖州汪藻再乞除在外宫观差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229430")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229430'>敕汪藻：省所奏，再乞除一在外宫观差遣，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229430_comment'></div>卿厌直承明，出临便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229430_comment'></div>奉三年之最，将讫外庸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229430_comment'></div>披再至之辞，荐陈中悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229430_comment'></div>愿归印绶，祈领宫祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229430_comment'></div>俯惟私室之情，虽欲从于閒佚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229430_comment'></div>顾在公家之计，正深赖于循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229430_comment'></div>繄乃尔臣，体予德意，姑少安于所守，以终惠于斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229430_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229430_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229430_comment'></div>夏热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229430_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229430_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　在钱塘，七月，草范宗尹诏。作品：《赐新除资政殿大学士知温州范宗尹辞免恩命乞依旧宫祠不允诏》<div id='poem_1229428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除资政殿大学士知温州范宗尹辞免恩命乞依旧宫祠不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229428")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229428'>敕宗尹：省所奏，辞免资政殿大学士、知温州恩命，乞依旧宫祠，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229428_comment'></div>朕降登承弼，稽法祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229428_comment'></div>虽上印均劳，既中辞于机柄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229428_comment'></div>而分符共理，犹外寄于藩宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229428_comment'></div>盖将倚重其德名，非以课功于吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229428_comment'></div>嘉我钧衡之旧，即安山海之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229428_comment'></div>载想英风，出处独由于公道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229428_comment'></div>还观素节，比周罔见于私交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229428_comment'></div>初不自明，久斯可覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229428_comment'></div>是用起之閒馆，付以便邦，稍升秘殿之华，始正辅班之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229428_comment'></div>乃缘宠命，荐列忱辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229428_comment'></div>矧进退大臣，朕有不得已者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229428_comment'></div>而铺陈往咎，卿何念之深耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229428_comment'></div>虽抱志而未伸，岂酬恩之无日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229428_comment'></div>体兹深眷，毋复多云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229428_comment'></div>所请宜不允，仍不许再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229428_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229428_comment'></div>秋热，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229428_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1229428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月15日</a>　在钱塘，七月十五日，授宝文阁学士、知绍兴军府事、兼管内劝农使、充两浙东路安抚使、马步军都总管。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
浙江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e1a94b615363422bae1270d9664417db_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1a94b615363422bae1270d9664417db");'><span id='e1a94b615363422bae1270d9664417db_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月20日</a>　四月二十日，随高宗发杭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月</a>　四月，除起居郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月26日</a>　四月二十六日，上《辞免起居郎奏状》<div id='poem_1229663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免起居郎奏状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229663")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229663_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1229663_0'>① 建炎三年四月二十六日，工部员外郎上。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229663'>臣四月二十六日准尚书省劄子：奉圣旨，除臣起居郎，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229663_comment'></div>闻命震惊，抚躬罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229663_comment'></div>窃以左右置史，起居是司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229663_comment'></div>入奉严宸，记事言于螭陛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229663_comment'></div>出陪清跸，随伏卫于銮舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229663_comment'></div>密迩从班，最为妙选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229663_comment'></div>必得通今博古，守官而不挠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229663_comment'></div>乃能执兰载笔，书法而可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229663_comment'></div>如臣者识类枣昏，材同樗散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229663_comment'></div>学污而近，讵当良臣之评；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229663_comment'></div>性蠢而疏，难处侍臣之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229663_comment'></div>愿回睿照，追寝误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229663_comment'></div>俾更选于时髦，庶克谐于议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229663_comment'></div>臣无任祈天俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229663_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月</a>　四月，有文。作品：《代李邴辞免尚书左丞表》《代李邴谢除尚书左丞表》《代吕颐浩辞免尚书右仆射表》《代吕颐浩谢尚书右仆射表》《代郑瑴谢依同知枢密院恩数表》<div id='poem_1229621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李邴辞免尚书左丞表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229621")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229621'>参右府枢机之任，政恐惧以循墙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229621_comment'></div>备中台管辖之司，载褒扬而出綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229621_comment'></div>顾辞尊而益进，惊避宠以加荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229621_comment'></div>更沥愚诚，重纡天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229621_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣器难大受，学谢多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229621_comment'></div>委质效官，徒守诗书之素业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229621_comment'></div>逢时得路，幸联翰墨之清资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229621_comment'></div>顷流落以还朝，属仓黄而扈跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229621_comment'></div>戡奉天之难，乏陆贽居中之筹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229621_comment'></div>寝淮南之谋，惭汲黯在朝之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229621_comment'></div>不虞孽将，辄肆奸图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229621_comment'></div>窃怀愤懑之诚，力折凶邪之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229621_comment'></div>惟节义之闲敢废，仅效小忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229621_comment'></div>顾灵长之祚重新，方恢大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229621_comment'></div>曾谓薪樗之质，乃堪栋宇之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229621_comment'></div>虽亲诏丁宁，诚圣君之深眷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229621_comment'></div>而危躬踧踖，知高位之疾颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229621_comment'></div>祈反汗以无从，敢叩阍而有请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229621_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下广尧舜知人之鉴，稽宣王复古之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229621_comment'></div>咨四岳以旁搜，俾熙庶绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229621_comment'></div>任真贤而共治，用佐中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229621_comment'></div>简黜罢庸，退居冗散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229621_comment'></div>则得人之效，庶克济于艰难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229621_comment'></div>而非据之危，亦或逃于颠覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229621_comment'></div>陈词已确，得请为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229621_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1229621_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李邴谢尚书左丞表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229622")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229622'>备言语侍从之流，或能陈力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229622_comment'></div>参辅弼疑丞之后，岂所当仁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229622_comment'></div>循墙莫奉于俞音，造膝载烦于温谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229622_comment'></div>凌兢拜命，惭汗在颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229622_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣术昧经纶，才非康济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229622_comment'></div>被道皇之眷遇，颛由文艺而进升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229622_comment'></div>蒙圣主之记怜，复采畸孤而收召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229622_comment'></div>每思奇节，少报大恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229622_comment'></div>属陪扈以南巡，遇仓黄而内禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229622_comment'></div>折冲御侮，曾无却敌之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229622_comment'></div>正色立朝，固有疾邪之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229622_comment'></div>阻凶焰于方炽，扶圣日而再中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229622_comment'></div>时惟将相之叶诚，允副神人之共愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229622_comment'></div>顾司败之刑不及，已荷宽仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229622_comment'></div>而左纲之任旁求，乃先庸妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229622_comment'></div>服宠章之优异，出亲诏以褒扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229622_comment'></div>名愧旧儒，辄践久虚之位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229622_comment'></div>勋惭上相，亦叨连茹之优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229622_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乃圣乃神，克勤克俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229622_comment'></div>念皇家之多故，图大政以更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229622_comment'></div>成祀夏配天之功，期复少康之旧业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229622_comment'></div>推任贤使能之效，将隆周室之中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229622_comment'></div>俯收一介之长，俾预四邻之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229622_comment'></div>忧深责重，恩厚命隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229622_comment'></div>臣谨当奋励猷为，激昂衰懦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229622_comment'></div>同心济务，敢忘可否之和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229622_comment'></div>一节事君，愿尽縻捐之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229622_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1229622_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代吕颐浩辞免尚书右仆射表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229617")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229617'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229617'>对清光于行殿，重瞻天日之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229617_comment'></div>敷大号于路朝，遽被钧衡之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229617_comment'></div>揣力小而任重，觉恩深而报难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229617_comment'></div>敢露愚忱，仰干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229617_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以宰相之任，天子是毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229617_comment'></div>丛万务之几微，职无不统；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229617_comment'></div>极四方之遐远，民所具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229617_comment'></div>惟时重轻，系人得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229617_comment'></div>矧皇家之多故，当国步之载艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229617_comment'></div>戎马新逼于江淮，狐鼠甫离于城社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229617_comment'></div>正倚赖庙堂之重，以镇安中外之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229617_comment'></div>若无救于颠危，焉用彼相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229617_comment'></div>盍委成于劳旧，以靖国人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229617_comment'></div>如臣之愚，惟上所察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229617_comment'></div>参鸿枢而出使，初无却敌之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229617_comment'></div>护诸将以来朝，安有勤王之绩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229617_comment'></div>谓方议罪，更误畴庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229617_comment'></div>孰师孰表，而进长于百僚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229617_comment'></div>何德何功，而超登于一相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229617_comment'></div>忽膺朝命，深悸危衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229617_comment'></div>辄自列于君慈，冀少宽于众谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229617_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下神心独断，睿鉴曲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229617_comment'></div>亮微臣非经济之才，难居大任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229617_comment'></div>体旧弼有保调之效，可倚成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229617_comment'></div>勿轻事于改图，俾获辞于误宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229617_comment'></div>庶易盈之量，进逃覆餗之辜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229617_comment'></div>而非据之资，退免危身之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229617_comment'></div>陈情良切，得请是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229617_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1229617_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代吕颐浩谢尚书右仆射表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229618")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229618'>帅师入觐，还超拱极之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229618_comment'></div>论相畴庸，遽被扬廷之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229618_comment'></div>既循墙而有请，终反汗以无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229618_comment'></div>责与恩深，感随惧集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229618_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣识非致远，材不踰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229618_comment'></div>起齐鲁之诸生，历试剧繁之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229618_comment'></div>习唐虞之久治，晚罗剥乱之伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229618_comment'></div>嗟艰险之备尝，慨功名之未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229618_comment'></div>误蒙知奖，引寘近岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229618_comment'></div>版部理材，无足国裕民之术；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229618_comment'></div>天官典选，乏扬清激浊之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229618_comment'></div>属陪扈以时巡，适参裨于军务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229618_comment'></div>愿屯江险，以遏淮冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229618_comment'></div>进升秘殿之华，擢预中枢之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229618_comment'></div>顾外虞之未靖，方事抚宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229618_comment'></div>骇内禅之无名，窃怀忠愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229618_comment'></div>鼓鹰扬而朝下，驱鼠窃以宵逋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229618_comment'></div>宝祚重新，还正当阳之位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229618_comment'></div>皇慈过听，亟膺赉弼之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229618_comment'></div>惟中原当艰否之期，念彊敌肆侵凌之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229618_comment'></div>典章尽废，奸宄未销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229618_comment'></div>熙庶绩而弼一人，宜更理纪纲之务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229618_comment'></div>抚四夷而安百姓，在调和中外之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229618_comment'></div>欲图再造之功，宜得非常之佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229618_comment'></div>夫何庸妄，乃许叨尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229618_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下躬大禹之俭勤，负成汤之勇智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229618_comment'></div>念二圣蒙尘之久，盖尝胆而不忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229618_comment'></div>轸三军暴骨之伤，宁责躬而自咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229618_comment'></div>初还明辟，益务远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229618_comment'></div>敷求辅相之材，俾济艰难之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229618_comment'></div>曷容衰懦，辄与登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229618_comment'></div>臣敢不尽力百为，矢心一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229618_comment'></div>振皇纲之已坠，扶国势以不倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229618_comment'></div>才谢魏侯，粗识汉家之故事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229618_comment'></div>贤希山甫，庶歌周室之中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229618_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1229618_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑瑴谢依同知枢密院恩数表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229631")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229631'>位列中枢，既被非常之遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229631_comment'></div>宠均近辅，更叨越次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229631_comment'></div>荷德不赀，抚躬罔措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229631_comment'></div>伏念臣器微有限，量狭易充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229631_comment'></div>参法从之华，窃荣名于秘殿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229631_comment'></div>赞本兵之寄，预密议于筹帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229631_comment'></div>虽任阶廊庙之崇，顾班在疑丞之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229631_comment'></div>惟器名之不假，视资望以犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229631_comment'></div>国有彝章，礼存异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229631_comment'></div>于臣侈矣，敢妄意于殊私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229631_comment'></div>何锡予之，是齐肩于同列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229631_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下受天申命，图国中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229631_comment'></div>眷兹政事之联，同任艰难之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229631_comment'></div>用均上赐，俾一乃心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229631_comment'></div>小才不离小官，已愧超升之异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229631_comment'></div>大言则望大利，敢忘报称之难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229631_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1229631_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='68f3b29a2bda40719b22ed41050dcc3c_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月</a>　一月，有诗。作品：《扈从书事》<div id='poem_535510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_535510")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_535510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535510'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535510'>扈从官班近，艰难报效微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535510'>又同陪法驾，复共著征衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535510'>举目江山好，伤心井社非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535510'>何当戎马定，却作故乡归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535510'>负郭田园美，迎霜雉兔肥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_535510'>风尘嗟澒洞，梦寐怅依稀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_535510'>圣主兴皇祚，群公翊政机。<div id='poem_sentence_6_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_535510'>时平当自劾，还采故山薇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_535510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_535510'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年3月</a>　三月，草季陵制词。作品：《朝请郎新除中书舍人季陵可除徽猷阁待制知临安府制》<div id='poem_1229311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请郎新除中书舍人季陵可除徽猷阁待制知临安府制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229311")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229311'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229311'>敕：乃者长江失守，敌骑南凌，爰及钱塘，亦陷蹂躏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229311_comment'></div>念戎马之退，徒委空城，而兵火之馀，尚多失业，肆择循良之牧，得予侍从之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229311_comment'></div>具官某学贯圣言，才周世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229311_comment'></div>处米盐之密，明既析于秋毫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229311_comment'></div>当盘错之时，刃亦游于馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229311_comment'></div>顷从纶阁，丐领真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229311_comment'></div>式资尔雅之文，方复代言之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229311_comment'></div>属吴江之谋帅，辍禁掖以抡才，佥曰汝宜，勉为朕往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229311_comment'></div>仍还近职，以示宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229311_comment'></div>载念浙江，重罹戎寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229311_comment'></div>烟尘甫熄，益脩御敌之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229311_comment'></div>井邑新残，务致安民之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229311_comment'></div>亟回驿骑，往慰吾人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229311_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229311_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8754aead92604c8fa0cdff0df49e39c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8754aead92604c8fa0cdff0df49e39c3");'><span id='8754aead92604c8fa0cdff0df49e39c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，48岁</div><div id='8754aead92604c8fa0cdff0df49e39c3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月4日</a>　四月四日，随高宗发明州。<br /></div>

-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e62f5a338c014350be3ed3405cb4b135_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e62f5a338c014350be3ed3405cb4b135");'><span id='e62f5a338c014350be3ed3405cb4b135_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，47岁</div><div id='e62f5a338c014350be3ed3405cb4b135' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年5月8日</a>　五月八日，随高宗驻跸建康，有文。作品：《大驾驻跸建康府起居表》<div id='poem_1229647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大驾驻跸建康府起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229647")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229647'>地钟五气，兆夙见于前朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229647_comment'></div>名协藩封，祥寔开于上圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229647_comment'></div>仰銮舆之再驾，知寰宇之将同<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229647_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下德迈宣、光，孝如舜、禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229647_comment'></div>励枕戈之志，勤万乘以亲行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229647_comment'></div>均挟纩之恩，抚六师而争奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229647_comment'></div>遂临江次，以定域中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229647_comment'></div>神灵所扶，夷夏咸耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229647_comment'></div>臣昔从清跸，叨侍禁墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229647_comment'></div>梦越秦淮，已远同朝之侣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229647_comment'></div>功成京邑，庶陪复会之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229647_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年6月27日</a>　在建康，六月二十七日，以起居郎权给事中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月24日</a>　在建康，七月二十四日，召试政事堂，试中书舍人，有文。作品：《辞免召试中书舍人奏状》<div id='poem_1229664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免召试中书舍人奏状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年7月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229664")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229664_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1229664_0'>① 建炎三年七月二十四日，起居郎权给事中上。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229664'>宣教郎、试起居郎、兼权给事中綦崇礼奏：今月二十四日，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨召试中书舍人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229664_comment'></div>闻命震惊，抚躬自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229664_comment'></div>伏念臣顷罹忧患，重历艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229664_comment'></div>心术耗昏，学殖荒落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229664_comment'></div>濡毫史策，已惭记事之能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229664_comment'></div>给札词闱，宁识代言之体？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229664_comment'></div>忽膺严召，深悸危衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229664_comment'></div>愿追寝于误恩，庶少安于愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229664_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月</a>　在建康，七月，除中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月29日</a>　在建康，七月二十九日，上辞免中书舍人奏状。作品：《辞免中书舍人奏状》<div id='poem_1229665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免中书舍人奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年7月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229665")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229665'>臣七月二十九日准尚书省劄子：奉圣旨，除臣中书舍人，日下供职，及与转通直郎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229665_comment'></div>升华法从，通籍朝闺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229665_comment'></div>省踰分以难安，敢陈诚而有请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229665_comment'></div>臣以冒居左史，尚补西垣，偶此缺官，例从给札。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229665_comment'></div>素乏涌泉之思，几成阁笔之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229665_comment'></div>虽趣以终篇，初不识凤阁文辞之样；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229665_comment'></div>苟责其视草，将曷裨淮南书诏之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229665_comment'></div>反复自惟，周章失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229665_comment'></div>愿收还于成命，庶弭息于烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229665_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月</a>　在建康，七月末，有谢表。作品：《谢除中书舍人表》<div id='poem_1229605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229605")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229605'>记事螭坳，已玷侍臣之列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229605_comment'></div>代言凤阁，遂尘法从之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229605_comment'></div>升阶序于朝闺，焕身章于命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229605_comment'></div>得踰所望，愧甚于荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229605_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>维禁垣清切之司，极儒者高华之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229605_comment'></div>奉扬命令，典掌丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229605_comment'></div>视草誇工，岂独取文章之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229605_comment'></div>判花傅美，抑兼收政事之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229605_comment'></div>称职尤难，择才宜慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229605_comment'></div>必有一时之秀，来充六押之员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229605_comment'></div>如臣者，器局甚卑，机灵不颖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229605_comment'></div>词多骳骫，初非深厚之文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229605_comment'></div>思苦穷愁，安得中和之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229605_comment'></div>顷预师儒之任，获陪英俊之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229605_comment'></div>雠秘府之图书，剡外庭之笺奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229605_comment'></div>用既颛于文字，名稍见于搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229605_comment'></div>中遇家艰，继丁寇乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229605_comment'></div>举青箱而尽弃，指黄屋以来奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229605_comment'></div>积千虑之薰心，都忘旧学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229605_comment'></div>乏一言之悟意，徒冒新恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229605_comment'></div>握兰画省之中，执笔赤墀之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229605_comment'></div>未能一岁，遽俾三迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229605_comment'></div>试艺靡工，乌识王言之体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229605_comment'></div>奏篇称善，误蒙天语之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229605_comment'></div>歆艳儒冠，宠光从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229605_comment'></div>自惟寒迹，孰与游谈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229605_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣学高明，神心昭晰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229605_comment'></div>谓艰难之际，可能渊默而深居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229605_comment'></div>在号令之中，正欲风行而鼓动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229605_comment'></div>稍罗文士，使备词臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229605_comment'></div>庶其播告之修，能致中兴之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229605_comment'></div>乃容疏贱，亦预推扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229605_comment'></div>臣敢不仰体深知，益殚末技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229605_comment'></div>守勿欺之节，或有补于论思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229605_comment'></div>斥无用之言，冀少存于体要。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1229605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月15日</a>　在建康，闰八月十五日，草韩世忠制词。作品：《韩世忠可除西路制置使应沿江防守战守备御之事并听节制依旧镇江府驻札制》<div id='poem_1229278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韩世忠可除西路制置使应沿江防守战守备御之事并听节制依旧镇江府驻劄制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229278")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229278'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229278'>敕：控长江而作镇，既先十乘之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229278_comment'></div>护诸将以临屯，兹属三军之帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229278_comment'></div>爰加使号，用壮军容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229278_comment'></div>具官某，沈毅有谋，骁雄无匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229278_comment'></div>临机而出方略，弗资金版之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229278_comment'></div>定乱而事干戈，曷取毛锥之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229278_comment'></div>奋身边塞，宣力颜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229278_comment'></div>勇盖北方，夜捣全师之坚垒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229278_comment'></div>勋高南土，生俘同恶之逋囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229278_comment'></div>乃视秩于三孤，仍兼荣于双节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229278_comment'></div>属当备险，方俾移军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229278_comment'></div>列戍江津，实倚长城之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229278_comment'></div>分釐浙部，宜归大将之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229278_comment'></div>遂专节制之雄，庶一师徒之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229278_comment'></div>临淮号令，觉士气之增新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229278_comment'></div>道济威名，想敌人之严惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229278_comment'></div>宽予忧顾，勉尔成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229278_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229278_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
江苏

style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>闰八月二十七日，随高宗往浙西途中，草叶焕制词。作品：《叶焕可落职提举亳州明道宫制》《朝散大夫充徽猷阁待制知镇江府充两浙西路安抚使叶焕降授朝散郎制》<div id='poem_1229315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叶焕可落职提举亳州明道宫制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年8月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229315")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229315'>敕：西清次对之联，是为近侍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229315_comment'></div>京口抚绥之任，实控要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229315_comment'></div>傥公议之靡容，岂非才之宜处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229315_comment'></div>具官某术疏而果，志浅而狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229315_comment'></div>尝更践于剧烦，或推称其风力，遂膺选择，往备藩宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229315_comment'></div>进书殿之名，越持从橐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229315_comment'></div>徙帅垣之节，增重守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229315_comment'></div>期镇理之可能，肆要求而拂拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229315_comment'></div>顾未闻于治状，忽继览于弹章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229315_comment'></div>宿负隐愆，既犯士夫之清议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229315_comment'></div>轻谋妄作，徒传中外之笑端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229315_comment'></div>初无忧国之诚，何望折冲之效？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229315_comment'></div>盖获利则怀自营之计，将脱身而为微罪之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229315_comment'></div>原情信然，明罚奚逭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229315_comment'></div>收还禁职，黜领真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229315_comment'></div>姑从邦宪之常，薄示守官之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229315_comment'></div>益思厥咎，毋遂尔非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229315_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229315_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫充徽猷阁待制知镇江府充两浙西路安抚使叶焕降授朝散郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年8月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229314")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229314'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229314'>敕：膺师帅之托，莫尚于循良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229314_comment'></div>制方面之雄，尤先于镇静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229314_comment'></div>苟辜委遇，宜抵谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229314_comment'></div>具官某夙有能名，疑堪剧任，为徙帅藩之寄，俾增州牧之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229314_comment'></div>弗能慎重以济功，乃尔狂疏而生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229314_comment'></div>请不待报，辄募兵于他邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229314_comment'></div>用非其人，几召乱于属邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229314_comment'></div>顾京口要冲之地，正江津备御之秋，轻率若斯，设施何赖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229314_comment'></div>聊举黜官之罚，用惩失职之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229314_comment'></div>往讼前非，尚图后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229314_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229314_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c2640be2ee274d969e7dd1980521f7a0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2640be2ee274d969e7dd1980521f7a0");'><span id='c2640be2ee274d969e7dd1980521f7a0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，47岁</div><div id='c2640be2ee274d969e7dd1980521f7a0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　秋，草詹乂诏。作品：《赐新除徽猷阁学士提举临安府洞霄宫詹乂辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除徽猷阁学士提举临安府洞霄宫詹乂辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229552")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229552'>敕詹乂：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229552_comment'></div>卿年加耆艾，时谓老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229552_comment'></div>从朕于艰，勤劳惟旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229552_comment'></div>名还东省，曾未淹时，惜其旅力之愆，重烦官职之事，畀真祠之优廪，仍延阁之近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229552_comment'></div>示朕至恩，皆卿旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229552_comment'></div>往绥寿祉，毋事谦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229552_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229552_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229552_comment'></div>秋冷，卿比平安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229552_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229552_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7865285e15f0424dbf62c14f3705074f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7865285e15f0424dbf62c14f3705074f");'><span id='7865285e15f0424dbf62c14f3705074f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，47岁</div><div id='7865285e15f0424dbf62c14f3705074f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月6日</a>　九月六日，随高宗次平江府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月8日</a>　在平江府，九月八日，草周望制词。作品：《端明殿学士朝奉大夫同签书枢密院事周望可除两浙宣抚使制》<div id='poem_1229340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端明殿学士朝奉大夫同签书枢密院事周望可除两浙宣抚使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229340")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229340'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229340'>敕：自南渡以来，乱靡有定，敌不去境，人情未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229340_comment'></div>思得魁垒之臣，付以折冲之寄，尽护诸将，镇兹要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229340_comment'></div>我求其人，得于近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229340_comment'></div>具官某深沈而精敏，敦大而高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229340_comment'></div>行义足以厉风俗之媮，忠诚足以荷邦家之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229340_comment'></div>居无择事，任不辞难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229340_comment'></div>北使强邻，衔命冒兵交之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229340_comment'></div>南平逋寇，出师行天讨之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229340_comment'></div>载畴勋庸，延置宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229340_comment'></div>摅发经纶之蕴，备闻帷幄之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229340_comment'></div>朕方移跸南巡，留屯近戍，其即枢机之任，往宣鈇钺之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229340_comment'></div>维患必豫防，正循江而严备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229340_comment'></div>顾兵难预度，烦总众以亲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229340_comment'></div>伫闻绥靖之期，还倚赞襄之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229340_comment'></div>体予注意，勉尔成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229340_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月8日</a>　在平江府，九月八日，草李棁制词。作品：《责授平海军节度副使李棁可与复旧官除户部尚书留建康府掌户部钱斛官物及分劈钱物应副本府镇江府太平州驻札军兵制》<div id='poem_1229310' class='_poem'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229310'>敕：地官掌邦赋之繁，最称剧部：常伯居从班之首，实资辅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229310_comment'></div>稽考国朝之旧章，参用庙堂之故弼，庶图宿望，以重厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229310_comment'></div>具官某器博而用周，才高而识远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229310_comment'></div>被道皇之眷遇，已更践于六卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229310_comment'></div>膺渊圣之简求，亟延登于二府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229310_comment'></div>谋谟尽美，功烈未终，属兴祸于狄人，或归尤于使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229310_comment'></div>继从迁谪，久乃辩明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229310_comment'></div>召自遐陬，对于行殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229310_comment'></div>惜才猷之尚壮，念风绩之素闻，其还省计之崇，尽复文阶之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229310_comment'></div>昔萧何居国，常足食于军中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229310_comment'></div>而刘晏笼财，不收民于赋外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229310_comment'></div>维恃耆哲，无愧古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229310_comment'></div>方师徒留戍于江津，念馈饷实资于心计，勉济中兴之业，岂忘旧德之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229310_comment'></div>往体朕怀，奚烦多训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229310_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229361'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229361'>敕：端木赐，孔门高第，而货殖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229361_comment'></div>韩安国，汉朝名臣，而资贪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229361_comment'></div>如彼昔人之贤，未免后世之议，矧非其匹，可有是疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229361_comment'></div>具官某，早陟近班，久更烦使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229361_comment'></div>属此艰虞之际，起于摈废之中，图有一日之长，付以九江之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229361_comment'></div>驱攘盗贼，实宣捍御之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229361_comment'></div>抚养罢羸，顾乏廉平之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229361_comment'></div>掊取无艺，侵渔一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229361_comment'></div>既徙厥官，尽去其籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229361_comment'></div>会枢臣之出使，按罪迹以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229361_comment'></div>方劾实于台僚，难厕名于从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229361_comment'></div>其镌禁职，往对狱辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229361_comment'></div>尚省尔愆，无尤邦宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229361_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229361_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月16日</a>　在平江府，九月十六日，草邢倞制词。作品：《邢倞责授汝州团练副使英州安置制》<div id='poem_1229352' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229352' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229352?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邢倞责授汝州团练副使英州安置制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229352")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229352_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229352'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229352'>敕具官某：乃者靖康之难，戎骑既旋，盍思守约以靖民，何至徼功而生事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229352_comment'></div>维时愚相，信尔狂生，弗量用间之难，徒负败盟之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229352_comment'></div>结其贵将，为此厉阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229352_comment'></div>肆敌国之有辞，乘中原之无备，荐兴军旅，再犯京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229352_comment'></div>致两宫勤沙漠之行，使万民罹涂炭之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229352_comment'></div>噬脐靡及，流涕何追！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229352_comment'></div>顾当时主议之臣，既从远斥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229352_comment'></div>独先事首谋之罪，未抵严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229352_comment'></div>犹窃任于藩宣，乃安临于民社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229352_comment'></div>尔则无耻，国当有刑，其更散秩之员，往即遐荒之窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229352_comment'></div>尚知宽宥，无重悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229352_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229352_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫秘阁修撰知衢州胡唐老可除徽猷阁待制知镇江府充浙西路安抚使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229277")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229277'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229277'>敕：西清次对之联，是为近侍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229277_comment'></div>京口抚绥之任，实控要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229277_comment'></div>敷求文武之通才，庶协搢绅之公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229277_comment'></div>具官某系出华胄，名闻上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229277_comment'></div>提椠怀铅，饱艺文于芸省；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229277_comment'></div>明目张胆，耸风采于霜台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229277_comment'></div>出分师帅之忧，适据闽吴之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229277_comment'></div>比更大盗，安保坚城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229277_comment'></div>恩威既著于吏民，施设具存于条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229277_comment'></div>载畴绩用，进易藩宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229277_comment'></div>升延阁之近班，俾参法从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229277_comment'></div>付临江之雄镇，兼制列城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229277_comment'></div>庶均一郡之功，并浃七州之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229277_comment'></div>国方多难，奖扶允赖于折冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229277_comment'></div>时已盛秋，备御正资于设险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229277_comment'></div>奠兹南土，倚尔长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229277_comment'></div>往服训词，伫观成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229277_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229277_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月26日</a>　在平江府，九月二十六日，草邹浩制词。作品：《邹浩可特与追复龙图阁待制制》<div id='poem_1229272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹浩可特与追复龙图阁待制制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229272")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229272'>敕：朕履兹艰运，迹彼乱源，伤谄佞之成风，悼忠良之获罪，肆褒遗直，用劝在官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229272_comment'></div>故具官某处心不欺，养气至大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229272_comment'></div>言期寤意，引裾尝犯于雷霆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229272_comment'></div>计不惜身，去国再迁于岭徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229272_comment'></div>具臣动色，志士倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229272_comment'></div>英爽不亡，想生气之犹在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229272_comment'></div>奸谀亦死，知朽骨之尚寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229272_comment'></div>其还延阁之清资，少慰重泉之幽愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229272_comment'></div>噫，为善之效，其报也长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229272_comment'></div>身虽抑于生前，志卒伸于地下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229272_comment'></div>尚其肸蚃，歆此宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229272_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月26日</a>　在平江府，九月二十六日，草沈积中制词。作品：《沈积中可特追复资政殿学士还旧官与合得致仕恩泽制》<div id='poem_1229273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沈积中可特追复资政殿学士还旧官与合得致仕恩泽制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229273")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229273'>敕：乃者燕山之役，谋之不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229273_comment'></div>贪目前尺寸之利，而亡以善其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229273_comment'></div>靡敝中国，启衅夷狄，卒成意外之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229273_comment'></div>呜呼，谁生厉阶，至今为梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229273_comment'></div>既往何及，言之痛心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229273_comment'></div>以尔故具官某，顷使朔陲，备闻初议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229273_comment'></div>迨今师阃，实始兴言，乃独抗章，陈其不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229273_comment'></div>致权臣之甚恶，陷狱吏之深文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229273_comment'></div>奄至没身，遂遭削籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229273_comment'></div>载惟前事，良恻朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229273_comment'></div>矧元恶之已诛，顾重辜之未洗，是用还文阶之峻秩，复秘殿之隆名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229273_comment'></div>仍推延世之恩，并视漏泉之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229273_comment'></div>魂而不泯，尚克歆承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229273_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229273_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
绍兴（会稽）
-----detail
