href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，随高宗至越州，入居州廨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月25日</a>　十一月二十五日，随高宗发会稽，次钱清镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月26日</a>　十一月二十六日，随高宗还会稽，次城下，支持取海道避金兵之策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月26日</a>　十一月二十六日，草周望制词。作品：端明殿学士朝奉大夫同签枢密院事周望可除中大夫同知枢密院事制。<div id='poem_1229313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端明殿学士朝奉大夫同签枢密院事周望可除中大夫同知枢密院事制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229313")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229313'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229313'>敕：入则总枢机之任，以制胜于庙堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229313_comment'></div>出则宣军旅之威，以折冲于戎敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229313_comment'></div>膺此艰难之托，属予魁垒之臣，不有褒隆，曷昭眷倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229313_comment'></div>具官某直方而不挠，庄重而有谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229313_comment'></div>将命出疆，数冒干戈之险；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229313_comment'></div>奉辞伐罪，克申鈇钺之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229313_comment'></div>忠信弗渝，勋劳备著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229313_comment'></div>进举本兵之务，俾参近辅之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229313_comment'></div>惟著意以方深，顾循名而未称，宜深位次，以正官仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229313_comment'></div>眷吴会之要津，扼敌人之要路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229313_comment'></div>王师在戍，姑授印于军中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229313_comment'></div>巨寇即平，还运筹于幄内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229313_comment'></div>安危所系，中外维均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229313_comment'></div>益既乃心，无忘朕训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229313_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229313_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，代范宗尹撰辞免参知政事表。作品：《代范宗尹辞免参知政事表》<div id='poem_1229627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代范宗尹辞免参知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229627")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229627'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229627'>引当言路，方愧空餐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229627_comment'></div>进贰政机，遽容充任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229627_comment'></div>令出虽难于反汗，忧深犹切于循墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229627_comment'></div>敢露愚衷，仰干聪听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229627_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣奋由一介，被遇三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229627_comment'></div>得于射策之初，识其无隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229627_comment'></div>擢在可言之地，许以不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229627_comment'></div>历长谏垣，骤持从橐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229627_comment'></div>属乾坤之震荡，仅免诛夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229627_comment'></div>眇江海以流离，未知报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229627_comment'></div>岂谓大明之照，亮兹小己之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229627_comment'></div>纶掖代言，方从收召；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229627_comment'></div>霜台执法，俄俾超踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229627_comment'></div>力难振于颓纲，言莫裨于圣智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229627_comment'></div>忽惊严命，延寘近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229627_comment'></div>顾艰难险阻之中，孰当大任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229627_comment'></div>岂辅弼疑丞之选，可用非才？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229627_comment'></div>时危敢计于爱身，器小实虞于误国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229627_comment'></div>周章自省，颠倒失容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229627_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下曲轸皇慈，俯回睿鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229627_comment'></div>改图贤德，冀多难之可安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229627_comment'></div>罢退妄庸，庶烦言之克弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229627_comment'></div>陈词良确，得请是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229627_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1229627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故曾祖德制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故曾祖德赠太子少保制》<div id='poem_1229284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故曾祖德赠太子少保制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229284")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229284'>敕：朕眷礼大臣，盖俯殊于庶位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229284_comment'></div>褒崇先世，乃上及于曾门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229284_comment'></div>惟流庆之有来，顾疏恩之可后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229284_comment'></div>具官故曾祖某，韬光布素，隐迹丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229284_comment'></div>独矜天爵之修，曾靡世荣之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229284_comment'></div>考之报施，宜有吉祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229284_comment'></div>生而不享于其躬，没乃克兴于厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229284_comment'></div>钟之三世，大彼一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229284_comment'></div>方延置于疑丞，俾参陪于政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229284_comment'></div>首举显先之典，用章积善之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229284_comment'></div>贲嘉命于九原，陟春宫之二品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229284_comment'></div>尚其肸蚃，知克歆承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229284_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229284_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故曾祖母制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故曾祖母朱氏杨氏制》<div id='poem_1229285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故曾祖母朱氏杨氏制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229285")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229285'>敕：眷礼大臣，盖俯殊于众位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229285_comment'></div>褒崇先世，乃上及于曾门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229285_comment'></div>惟衍庆之有来，顾疏恩之可后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229285_comment'></div>具官故曾祖母某氏，出自良族，嫔于吉人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229285_comment'></div>既无愧于平生，肆有兴于后裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229285_comment'></div>钟此三世，大其一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229285_comment'></div>方延置于疑丞，俾参陪于政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229285_comment'></div>首举显先之典，用彰积善之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229285_comment'></div>锡嘉号于小君，贲新恩于幽穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229285_comment'></div>尚其肸蚃，知克钦承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229285_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229285_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故祖昌制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故祖昌可赠太子少傅制》<div id='poem_1229286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故祖昌可赠太子少傅制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229286")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229286'>敕：朕眷遇大臣，夐绝百僚之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229286_comment'></div>显扬先阀，并推三世之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229286_comment'></div>盖积善之源既深，肆流根之泽亦厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229286_comment'></div>具官某故祖某，生有懿行，没遗令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229286_comment'></div>夙传美于当年，初无缺行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229286_comment'></div>审贻谋于后叶，宜有显人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229286_comment'></div>钟此贤孙，为吾近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229286_comment'></div>方延登之伊始，稽典故之攸存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229286_comment'></div>宠追祖庙之光，超亚储闱之傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229286_comment'></div>英灵不泯，嘉命其承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229286_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故祖母制。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故祖母制》<div id='poem_1229287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故祖母制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229287")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229287'>敕：朕眷遇大臣，夐绝百僚之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229287_comment'></div>显扬先阀，并推三世之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229287_comment'></div>盖积善之源既深，肆流根之泽亦厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229287_comment'></div>具官某故祖母某氏，生有懿行，没遗令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229287_comment'></div>夙传闺阃之风，犹作乡闾之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229287_comment'></div>蓄其馀庆，钟此闻孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229287_comment'></div>方延置于岩廊，首褒崇于祖庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229287_comment'></div>追贲笄珈之赠，式增泉壤之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229287_comment'></div>魂而有知，服我嘉命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229287_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹父昱制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故父昱可赠太子少师制》<div id='poem_1229288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故父昱可赠太子少师制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229288")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229288'>敕：朕登用宝臣，参陪机政，岂独公朝之喜，亦惟私阀之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229288_comment'></div>宜有宠章，逮其考妣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229288_comment'></div>具官某故父某，抱能未试，藏器弗沽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229288_comment'></div>宗族称其慈仁，乡闾推其信谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229288_comment'></div>于公驷马，兹无愧于高门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229288_comment'></div>韦氏一经，终有传于遗子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229288_comment'></div>克生令器，为时显人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229288_comment'></div>养志何追，但美流根之泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229288_comment'></div>教忠有自，方收报国之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229288_comment'></div>欲慰孝心，式嘉褒典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229288_comment'></div>举密章之一命，亚储苑之三师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229288_comment'></div>英爽不忘，追崇未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229288_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229288_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故前母制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故前母李氏郝氏制》<div id='poem_1229289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故前母李氏郝氏制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1229289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229289'>敕：朕登用宝臣，参陪机政，岂独公朝之喜，亦惟私阀之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229289_comment'></div>宜有宠章，逮其考妣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229289_comment'></div>具官某故前母某氏，生禀淑质，来嫔庆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229289_comment'></div>惟妇职之无亏，惜天年之不永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229289_comment'></div>克相夫家之祉，钟兹嗣叶之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229289_comment'></div>均被子恩，何殊己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229289_comment'></div>锦囊犀轴，爰追贲于䌽纶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229289_comment'></div>翟茀鱼轩，用增光于泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229289_comment'></div>尚其冥漠，知克歆承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229289_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹故母制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹故母李氏制》<div id='poem_1229290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹故母李氏制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229290")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229290'>敕：朕登用宝臣，参陪机政，岂独公朝之喜，亦惟私阀之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229290_comment'></div>宜有宠光，逮其考妣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229290_comment'></div>具官某故母某氏，妇仪之善，母道之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229290_comment'></div>相其夫，则闺门之内无违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229290_comment'></div>训其子，则朝廷之间有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229290_comment'></div>发为贤业，服在近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229290_comment'></div>方收报上之忠，宜慰显亲之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229290_comment'></div>爰稽故事，式举彝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229290_comment'></div>特纡纶綍之华，追贲笄珈之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229290_comment'></div>尚其幽穸，歆此新恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229290_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　十一月，在越州，草范宗尹妻制词。作品：《参知政事范宗尹妻张氏可封和义郡夫人制》<div id='poem_1229291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事范宗尹妻张氏可封和义郡夫人制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229291")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229291'>敕：朕登用宝臣，参陪机政，岂独公朝之喜，亦惟私室之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229291_comment'></div>宜有宠光，逮其伉俪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229291_comment'></div>具官某妻张氏，赋资淑慎，禀质柔明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229291_comment'></div>既擢秀于闺房，宜作嫔于君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229291_comment'></div>献可以替否，曾弗夺于家谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229291_comment'></div>尽公不顾私，岂无资于内助？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229291_comment'></div>爰稽彝典，用侈新恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229291_comment'></div>甫从一命之初，遽锡小君之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229291_comment'></div>往祗休渥，嗣有褒封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229291_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229291_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2fbc3de0febc4e5cbb3f4500cc044aeb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2fbc3de0febc4e5cbb3f4500cc044aeb");'><span id='2fbc3de0febc4e5cbb3f4500cc044aeb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，48岁</div><div id='2fbc3de0febc4e5cbb3f4500cc044aeb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月8日</a>　四月八日，草朱胜非制词。作品：《宣奉大夫提举亳州明道宫朱胜非可除观文殿学士充江西荆湖南北路宣抚使制》<div id='poem_1229275' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣奉大夫提举亳州明道宫朱胜非可除观文殿学士充江西荆湖南北路宣抚使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229275")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229275_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229275'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229275'>敕：经体赞元，入则秉钧衡之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229275_comment'></div>折冲御侮，出则宣军旅之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229275_comment'></div>维兼资文武之臣，宜迭任安危之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229275_comment'></div>我图故弼，兹焕宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229275_comment'></div>具官某敦大而刚明，深沈而和裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229275_comment'></div>镇群情之疑畏，屹如鼎鼐之安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229275_comment'></div>裁庶事之纠纷，判若蓍龟之决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229275_comment'></div>顷罹变故，实赖弥纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229275_comment'></div>驯暴虎而卒无所伤，扶神器而终能返正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229275_comment'></div>逮从去位，旋坐黜官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229275_comment'></div>虽身远于朝廷，亮心存于王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229275_comment'></div>惟边尘之未靖，念国步之方艰，非时旧人，孰任吾事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229275_comment'></div>是用宠班秘殿，往总行师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229275_comment'></div>抚江湖三道之遥，临荆鄂上游之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229275_comment'></div>庶资宿望，式控中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229275_comment'></div>昔谢安起东山之游，以苍生之所系；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229275_comment'></div>而裴度委北门之寄，由朔寇之未宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229275_comment'></div>尚勤绥御之方，克副忧劳之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229275_comment'></div>维吾元老，岂烦训辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229275_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1229275_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月12日</a>　四月十二日，随高宗驻跸会稽。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月19日</a>　在会稽，四月十九日，草赵鼎制词。作品：《朝奉大夫试御史中丞赵鼎可除吏部尚书制》<div id='poem_1229297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉大夫试御史中丞赵鼎可除吏部尚书制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229297")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229297'>敕：《周官》冢宰，任首六卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229297_comment'></div>汉制尚书，位参八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229297_comment'></div>维职典铨衡之要，而班邻丞辅之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229297_comment'></div>在昔既然，于今斯重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229297_comment'></div>久虚厥次，兹得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229297_comment'></div>具官某和裕而靖庄，直方而敦大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229297_comment'></div>立朝正色，折冲允赖于精神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229297_comment'></div>遇事敢言，发愤每披其肝胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229297_comment'></div>赤墀频对，白简屡闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229297_comment'></div>载嘉乌府之劳，进陟銮坡之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229297_comment'></div>抗章引避，陈义甚高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229297_comment'></div>察其操守之坚，虽力辞于翰苑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229297_comment'></div>亮尔公忠之素，可轻去于朝廷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229297_comment'></div>其升常伯之联，往率天官之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229297_comment'></div>顾干戈扰攘，衣冠多失职之嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229297_comment'></div>而典籍散亡，胥吏有用权之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229297_comment'></div>实藉通明之鉴，克谐平允之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229297_comment'></div>往既乃心，无忝朕命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229297_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1229297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月</a>　四月，草李迨制词。作品：《起复中散大夫试户部侍郎李迨可除显谟阁待制江淮荆浙发运使制》<div id='poem_1229321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>起复中散大夫试户部侍郎李迨可除显谟阁待制江淮荆浙发运使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229321")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229321'>敕：朕惟狄难犹炽，方尝胆以思雠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229321_comment'></div>王师再行，政张颐而待哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229321_comment'></div>维时漕挽之寄，必资强济之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229321_comment'></div>式图近臣，以庀厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229321_comment'></div>具官某吏能敏捷，心计精明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229321_comment'></div>事朕军中，盖有潜藩之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229321_comment'></div>馈师海上，肆升从橐之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229321_comment'></div>既登贰于地官，实委成于邦计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229321_comment'></div>属敌兵之将退，顾粮道之尚艰，众且思琦，国方仰晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229321_comment'></div>宜易西清之职，往持大将之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229321_comment'></div>维江湖淮浙之间，困盗贼兵革之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229321_comment'></div>因功利而求宠，固尔不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229321_comment'></div>贪富强而劳民，岂朕所欲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229321_comment'></div>其善经于调度，以共济于艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229321_comment'></div>尚既乃心，毋忘斯训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229321_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月3日</a>　在会稽，五月三日，草范宗尹右相制。作品：《除范宗尹特授通议大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事进封髙平郡开国侯加食邑食实封制》<div id='poem_1229370' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229370' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229370?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除范宗尹特授通议大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事进封高平郡开国侯加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年五月甲辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229370")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229370_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229370'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229370'>门下：论一相而弼一人，斯举有邦之职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229370_comment'></div>典百寮以择百揆，必求名世之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229370_comment'></div>朕遭时险艰，注意贤隽，庶获中兴之佐，共图复古之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229370_comment'></div>我得其人，肆颁明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229370_comment'></div>中大夫、参知政事、高平县开国男、食邑四百户、赐紫金鱼袋范宗尹，端凝而和裕，沉厚而高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229370_comment'></div>学深造于本原，识该通于远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229370_comment'></div>布衣论事，马周若素官于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229370_comment'></div>白简持平，元衡负真宰之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229370_comment'></div>擢陪丞辅，备罄谋谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229370_comment'></div>勤小物而务振于颓纲，断大事而靡闻于遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229370_comment'></div>属虚魁柄，实总政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229370_comment'></div>询用群言，独取梓人之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229370_comment'></div>讲明故事，远追汉相之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229370_comment'></div>顾考慎之已详，察忠纯之可属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229370_comment'></div>其延登于揆路，俾寅亮于天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229370_comment'></div>仍陟文阶，进分侯社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229370_comment'></div>倍增采赋，昭示宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229370_comment'></div>慨念我家，夐高前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229370_comment'></div>久戢干戈之用，遽生疆埸之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229370_comment'></div>胡马长驱，但肆侵凌之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229370_comment'></div>乘舆远播，未知旋复之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229370_comment'></div>王师益媮，而无决胜之兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229370_comment'></div>军食寖艰，而乏相因之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229370_comment'></div>念兹国步，危若缀旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229370_comment'></div>非望可折冲，则何以镇服于四夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229370_comment'></div>非力能起废，则何以弥纶于百度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229370_comment'></div>繄汝秉钧之责，宽予当馈之嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229370_comment'></div>断以不疑，任之勿贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229370_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229370_comment'></div>兴衰拨乱，朕敢忘王业之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229370_comment'></div>持危扶倾，尔其任天下之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229370_comment'></div>尚赖同心之助，克伸尝胆之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229370_comment'></div>往究远图，奚劳多训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229370_comment'></div>可特授通议大夫、守尚书右仆射、同中书门下平章事，进封高平郡开国侯，食邑一千户，食实封四百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229370_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1229370_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，草范宗尹诏。作品：《赐新除通议大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事进封髙平郡开国侯范宗尹辞免恩命》<div id='poem_1229429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除通议大夫守尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事进封高平郡开国侯范宗尹辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229429")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229429'>敕宗尹：省所上劄子奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229429_comment'></div>自祸结远夷，岁甚一岁，长驱南牧，遂济于江，吴越荆湘，咸被其酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229429_comment'></div>迨今归寇，犹据淮壖，肆暴穷凶，窥我未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229429_comment'></div>朕虽痛心疾首，尝胆枕戈，盖未知其攸济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229429_comment'></div>重念舆图滋削，国步愈艰，顾瞻中原，孰与戮力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229429_comment'></div>则凡治军旅、制国用、抚百姓、攘四夷，一相之图，朕敢轻付？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229429_comment'></div>虚位逾月，实难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229429_comment'></div>维卿天畀瑰材，自负国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229429_comment'></div>由布衣策试之日，盖常陈爱君忧国之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229429_comment'></div>方壮年进用之时，固旧倚有德老成之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229429_comment'></div>擢陪大政，亦稔具瞻，求之在廷，无出其右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229429_comment'></div>制麻初布，欢然一词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229429_comment'></div>胡为逡巡，犹欲退避？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229429_comment'></div>卿而不可，尚谁可者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229429_comment'></div>亟安厥位，以副所期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229429_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229429_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1229429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月11日</a>　在会稽，五月十一日，草卢法原制词。作品：《徽猷阁学士通奉大夫卢法原可除户部尚书制》<div id='poem_1229319' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229319' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229319?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽猷阁学士通奉大夫卢法原可除户部尚书制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229319")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229319_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229319'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229319'>敕：朕躬乘艰运，志靖中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229319_comment'></div>永惟戎旅之繁，虑孰先于军食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229319_comment'></div>乃眷版曹之重，职实总于邦财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229319_comment'></div>敷求其人，俾共厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229319_comment'></div>历选列辟，得吾旧臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229319_comment'></div>具官某心计精明，器资宏博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229319_comment'></div>才济剧烦而不露，刃游盘错而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229319_comment'></div>典选天官，士克称于平允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229319_comment'></div>守藩坤服，人咸咏于中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229319_comment'></div>久叹滞淹，肆从收召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229319_comment'></div>其上三年之最，还居八座之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229319_comment'></div>慨念烟尘，远弥县县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229319_comment'></div>帑廪虚而干戈未戢，生灵困而征役不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229319_comment'></div>足食足兵，正方今之急务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229319_comment'></div>知取知予，思在昔之良规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229319_comment'></div>顾如汝能，无愧前比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229319_comment'></div>往钦朕命，尚懋尔庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229319_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1229319_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月11日</a>　在会稽，五月十一日，试尚书吏部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月15日</a>　在会稽，五月十五日，草高卫制。作品：《高卫可除显谟阁待制知虔州制》<div id='poem_1229345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高卫可除显谟阁待制知虔州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229345")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229345'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229345'>敕：大江之西，虔为剧郡，平时狱市，已称夥繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229345_comment'></div>矧胡马南侵，而豫章不守，宫闱官府，迁寓是邦，必资宿望之臣，俾任分忧之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229345_comment'></div>具官某蚤更器使，久著能声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229345_comment'></div>疏通之才，多所练达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229345_comment'></div>深厚之量，见谓老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229345_comment'></div>顷擢贰于天官，俾分曹于行省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229345_comment'></div>适兹择守，佥曰汝贤，爰更次对之班，就畀藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229345_comment'></div>军民未靖，其镇抚于营屯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229345_comment'></div>兵革甫宁，尚保安于宫掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229345_comment'></div>政成事定，朕不汝忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229345_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月17日</a>　在会稽，五月十七日，有叔厚除试尚书吏部侍郎制词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，有谢表。作品：《谢除吏部侍郎表》<div id='poem_1229606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除吏部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229606")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229606'>赞掖垣之名命，久尸六押之员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229606_comment'></div>典选部之铨衡，遽陟贰卿之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229606_comment'></div>出兼衣而在笥，束宝带以华身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229606_comment'></div>辞弗赐俞，宠徒增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229606_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣无庸之质，初乏寸长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229606_comment'></div>不学之资，但馀少戆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229606_comment'></div>偶在艰难之日，获陪侍从之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229606_comment'></div>朝夕论思，无画策吐奇之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229606_comment'></div>出入风议，异拾遗补过之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229606_comment'></div>徒谨职于丝纶，粗服勤于鞿靮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229606_comment'></div>未从汰免，更冒褒升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229606_comment'></div>维古天官，乃今吏选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229606_comment'></div>方干戈扰攘，衣冠多失职之嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229606_comment'></div>而文籍散亡，胥吏有用权之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229606_comment'></div>非值精明之鉴，难求平允之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229606_comment'></div>顾兹摄事之经时，惧以隳官而速谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229606_comment'></div>就加因任，岂所当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229606_comment'></div>忱辞虽切于循墙，温诏终难于反汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229606_comment'></div>周章就列，黾勉厚颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229606_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下神武兴衰，浚文图治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229606_comment'></div>犯五不韪，知大敌之将亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229606_comment'></div>奉三无私，悯天工之多旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229606_comment'></div>欲整齐于庶政，务甄叙于群材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229606_comment'></div>过俾愚臣，当斯剧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229606_comment'></div>而臣顷更多难，谨保馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229606_comment'></div>心折东潍，叹松楸之隔绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229606_comment'></div>梦游南海，惊鸿雁之飘零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229606_comment'></div>术先愧于空疏，志益凋于忧患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229606_comment'></div>进叨眷遇，曷副使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229606_comment'></div>世乱未夷，敢议保身之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229606_comment'></div>君恩当报，但坚许国之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229606_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1229606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，兼权直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月23日</a>　在会稽，五月二十三日，草《赐门下分镇诏》<div id='poem_1229404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐门下分镇诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年五月甲子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229404")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229404'>敕门下：周建侯邦，四国有藩垣之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229404_comment'></div>唐分节镇，北边无夷狄之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229404_comment'></div>永惟凉眇之资，履此艰难之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229404_comment'></div>为黎元之父母，未能除丧乱之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229404_comment'></div>保宗社之土疆，无以救侵凌之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229404_comment'></div>远巡南国，久隔中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229404_comment'></div>盍因豪杰之徒，各奠方隅之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229404_comment'></div>是用考古之制，权时之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229404_comment'></div>画野离疆，咸就瓜分之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229404_comment'></div>折冲御侮，俾无尾大之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229404_comment'></div>断自荆淮，接于畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229404_comment'></div>岂独植籓篱于江表，盖将崇屏翰于京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229404_comment'></div>欲隆镇抚之名，为辍按廉之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229404_comment'></div>有民有社，得节制于境中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229404_comment'></div>足食足兵，听专征于阃外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229404_comment'></div>若转移其财用，与废置其属僚，理或应闻，事无待报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229404_comment'></div>维宠光之所被，既并享于终身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229404_comment'></div>苟功烈之克彰，当永传于后裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229404_comment'></div>尚赖连衡之力，共输夹辅之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229404_comment'></div>期捍御于寇戎，用匡扶于王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229404_comment'></div>咨尔列辟，体予至怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229404_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1229404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，草汪藻诏。作品：《赐新除兵部侍郎兼权直学士院汪藻辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观差遣不允诏》<div id='poem_1229431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除兵部侍郎兼权直学士院汪藻辞免恩命乞除一在外宫观差遣不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229431")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229431'>敕汪藻：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229431_comment'></div>卿以隽望通才，独当琐闼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229431_comment'></div>以英词大笔，兼直銮坡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229431_comment'></div>从朕于艰，阅时最久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229431_comment'></div>眷言勤绩，姑俾序迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229431_comment'></div>乃因移疾以家居，遂欲投闲而远引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229431_comment'></div>载披来请，殊拂朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229431_comment'></div>矧进贰夏官，非有甚繁之务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229431_comment'></div>而留居翰苑，方资尔雅之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229431_comment'></div>其即钦承，毋劳逊避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229431_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229431_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229431_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，草张守诏。作品：《赐新除参知政事张守辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除参知政事张守辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229474")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229474'>敕张守：省所奏劄子，辞免新除参知政事恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229474_comment'></div>顷以胡骑长驱，直侵江表；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229474_comment'></div>乘舆远播，至涉溟波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229474_comment'></div>所赖二三之臣，左维右挈，迨兹旋跸，用克无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229474_comment'></div>惟卿以直道忠言，进联枢辅，谋谟协赞，为力居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229474_comment'></div>念国步之益艰，而舆图之滋削，政需贤哲，以救颠危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229474_comment'></div>卿有经济之才，而未克大施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229474_comment'></div>有忠嘉之略，而未克尽用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229474_comment'></div>肆辍本兵之务，俾陪机政之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229474_comment'></div>式资献可替否之忠，庶成兴衰拨乱之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229474_comment'></div>过形谦避，非朕所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229474_comment'></div>其殚夙夜之勤，以赴功名之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229474_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229474_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在会稽，五月，草赵鼎诏。作品：《赐新除签书枢密院事赵鼎辞免不允诏》<div id='poem_1229423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除签书枢密院事赵鼎辞免不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229423")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229423'>敕赵鼎：省所劄子奏，辞免新除签书枢密院事恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229423_comment'></div>卿操术端纯，性资忠鲠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229423_comment'></div>自居风宪，力振颓纲，纠弹罔避于权彊，慷慨直当于仇嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229423_comment'></div>忱诚无隐，刚毅不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229423_comment'></div>朕察其用心，既已计从而言听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229423_comment'></div>验之行事，庶克危持而颠扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229423_comment'></div>肆擢赞于中枢，俾参联于近辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229423_comment'></div>筹帷画策，方需留侯借箸之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229423_comment'></div>叛国寝谋，仰赖汲黯在朝之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229423_comment'></div>朕心虚伫，物论允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229423_comment'></div>遽览奏陈，犹形逊避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229423_comment'></div>其趣祗于位著，以共济于艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229423_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229423_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229423_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月1日</a>　在会稽，六月一日，有青词。作品：《越州天庆观谢雨道场青词》<div id='poem_1229801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>越州天庆观谢雨道场青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年6月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229801")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229801'>维建炎四年岁次庚戌，六月朔日，嗣天子臣谨遣某官，命道士三七人，于越州天庆观开启谢雨道场三昼夜，罢散日设醮一座，三百六十分位，谨上启太上开天执符御历含真体道昊天玉皇上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229801_comment'></div>伏以虏师深入，既妨务于三时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229801_comment'></div>农亩仅存，幸收功于一稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229801_comment'></div>乃兹闵雨，尝以呼天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229801_comment'></div>荷昭鉴之不违，岂精诚之能感？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229801_comment'></div>普洽为霖之泽，尽兴将槁之苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229801_comment'></div>人喜及私，国当足食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229801_comment'></div>载招羽客，恭启琼科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229801_comment'></div>庶陈醮谢之仪，终致丰穰之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229801_comment'></div>无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229801_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1229801'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北海集》卷一八，清乾隆翰林院钞本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1229801_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月4日</a>　在会稽，六月四日，草苏迟制词。作品：《朝散大夫直秘阁苏迟可除中书门下省检正诸房公事制》<div id='poem_1229336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229336' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229336'>敕具官某：朕于故家，积习名教，更练世务，见谓老成。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月5日</a>　在会稽，六月五日，高宗用叔厚所请，赐官员告身。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月11日</a>　在会稽，六月十一日，有祭文。作品：《金人残破江淛杀戮生灵募僧道作道场祭文》<div id='poem_1229799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229799' class='poemTitle </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229799")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229799_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1229799_comment'></div>朕以眇躬，托于士民之上，属兹艰运，播越靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229799_comment'></div>天未悔祸，强敌深入，延及江浙，莫御其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229799_comment'></div>坐视元元肝脑涂地，闾阎城郭，所过皆墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229799_comment'></div>陷汝无辜，由朕不德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229799_comment'></div>为民父母，深所痛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229799_comment'></div>已令州县之官，往集缁黄之侣，虔依圣教，俯荐幽魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229799_comment'></div>冥漠有知，歆此觞酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229799_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月22日</a>　在会稽，六月二十二日，草林之平制词。作品：《朝请郎监察御史林之平可除右司员外制》<div id='poem_1229318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请郎监察御史林之平可除右司员外制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年6月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229318")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229318'>敕具官某：文昌万微所会，而都司分纠六联，维时官曹，最为要重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229318_comment'></div>非学足以知治体，识足以达时变，不在兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229318_comment'></div>以尔奋繇儒术，列属宪台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229318_comment'></div>庀事远行，克中机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229318_comment'></div>载嘉才谞，宜有褒迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229318_comment'></div>进畴尔能，俾从宰士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229318_comment'></div>勉佐尔长，以举厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229318_comment'></div>尚有宠章，待尔成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229318_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229318_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月</a>　在会稽，六月，草吕颐浩诏。作品：《赐新除建康府路安抚大使兼知池州吕颐浩再辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除建康府路安抚大使兼知池州吕颐浩再辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1229494_comment'></div>君子处己，以用舍为行藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229494_comment'></div>大臣立朝，寄安危于进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229494_comment'></div>卿中辞政柄，出拥斋旄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229494_comment'></div>闵劳机务之繁，优假真祠之逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229494_comment'></div>惟乃心王室，能忘国步之艰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229494_comment'></div>顾无逾老臣，用倚帅藩之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229494_comment'></div>赐环趣召，弭节来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229494_comment'></div>苍生之望素高，元老之猷益壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229494_comment'></div>维吾旧德，宜体眷怀，勉图克复之功，毋徇好谦之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229494_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　在会稽，七月，草权邦彦诏。作品：《赐新除淮南江浙荆湖等路制置发运使权邦彦辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1229489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除淮南江浙荆湖等路制置发运使权邦彦辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229489")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229489_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229489'>敕邦彦：省所奏辞免恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229489_comment'></div>日者胡马南寇，所过为墟，荆湘江浙之间咸被其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229489_comment'></div>今防秋又偪，而军赋未充，实资才智之臣，克司漕挽之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229489_comment'></div>是用辍卿方面，付以六路之权，庶日千金，无乏大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229489_comment'></div>昔史称刘晏以民不加赋，而上用足，今民力竭矣，而调度方繁，非心计有馀，知所取予，其何以任此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229489_comment'></div>求之庶位，无以踰卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229489_comment'></div>往图足食之方，以徇移忠之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229489_comment'></div>逡巡退避，勿事小廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229489_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229489_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229489_comment'></div>秋热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229489_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　在会稽，七月，草谢克家诏。作品：《赐新除礼部尚书谢克家辞免恩命不允诏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（五月十一日，谢克家试工部尚书。 七月二十七日，已除礼部尚书。八月一日，除参知政事。克家除礼部尚书在五月十一日到八月一日之间，叔厚草不允其辞免诏书亦当在其间。）</span><div id='poem_1229448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除礼部尚书谢克家辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229448")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229448'>敕克家：省所奏，辞免礼部尚书恩命，事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229448_comment'></div>士大夫平居积学厉志，穷古今治乱之源，岂徒疲精思于陈言之末哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229448_comment'></div>盖将以有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229448_comment'></div>今中原沦没，国步阽危，政资其人，相与戮力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229448_comment'></div>如卿道德纯备，见闻殚洽，谋谟议论，维时所需。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229448_comment'></div>以疾去朝，滞于远郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229448_comment'></div>肆从收召，还长春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229448_comment'></div>庶几咨询，可闻至策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229448_comment'></div>夫干戈之际，固俎豆之未遑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229448_comment'></div>然揖逊之间，亦征诛之所寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229448_comment'></div>往祗乃职，毋事劳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229448_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229448_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229274?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝议大夫试中书舍人李公彦可转中奉大夫守中书舍人致仕制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年9月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229274")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229274'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229274'>敕：侍从之臣，朕所优遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229274_comment'></div>矧上还于官政，宜加厚于宠章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229274_comment'></div>具官某久以艺文，历居华要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229274_comment'></div>藉其素望，擢在近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229274_comment'></div>既观润色之能，方伫论思之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229274_comment'></div>属往从于行省，乃奔避于征尘，未即遄归，遽兹引疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229274_comment'></div>念艰难之际，虽切于用贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229274_comment'></div>矜确苦之辞，勉从于谢事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229274_comment'></div>其陟文阶之峻，以为故里之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229274_comment'></div>尚勤药石之功，永介寿康之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229274_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在会稽，秋，草吕颐浩诏。作品：《赐新除建康府抚大使兼知池州吕颐浩乞给假将治不允诏》<div id='poem_1229491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除建康府路安抚大使兼知池州吕颐浩乞给假将治不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229491")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229491'>敕颐浩：省所奏：「比因饮食不时，遂致胃弱，因伤寒变为疟疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229491_comment'></div>伏望俯念衰残，给假将治，才候稍安，即兼程起发前去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229491_comment'></div>事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229491_comment'></div>为臣之规固重于进退，许国之谊宜徇于安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229491_comment'></div>乃眷元臣，实勤多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229491_comment'></div>扁舟径去，身虽远于朝廷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229491_comment'></div>魏阙遐瞻，心谅存于王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229491_comment'></div>属此防秋之急，肆先作牧之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229491_comment'></div>素志克伸，何恙不已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229491_comment'></div>中兴江表，今复见于夷吾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229491_comment'></div>薄伐太原，尚有劳于吉甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229491_comment'></div>其趣介圭之觐，副兹仄席之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229491_comment'></div>所请宜不允，仍依累降指挥，疾速前来赴行在，奏事讫之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229491_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229491_comment'></div>秋热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229491_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1229491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年10月18日</a>　在会稽，十月十八日，充徽猷阁直学士、知漳州军府事、兼管内劝农使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年10月19日</a>　在会稽，十月十九日，有祈晴文。作品：《越州圆通寺祈晴文》<div id='poem_1229844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>越州圆通寺祈晴文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年10月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229844")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229844'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229844'>维建炎四年岁次庚戌十月庚午朔，十九日戊子，皇帝遣某官，使僧四十七人，于越州圆通寺开启祈晴道场者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229844_comment'></div>伏以愁霖不止，惧伤高廪之藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229844_comment'></div>妙应无方，敢叩普门之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229844_comment'></div>维兹霖雨，乃涉严冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229844_comment'></div>云气益繁，久妨明于日月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229844_comment'></div>场工未毕，将阙奉于粢盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229844_comment'></div>愿回慧照之光，尽扫积阴之沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229844_comment'></div>鞭烛龙而衔耀，茅檐惬献曝之忱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229844_comment'></div>驱石燕之飞翔，编户免祁寒之怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229844_comment'></div>庶终穑事，以慰人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229844_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229844_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='18bf36ce72c94320acaf195a0032eda1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("18bf36ce72c94320acaf195a0032eda1");'><span id='18bf36ce72c94320acaf195a0032eda1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1135')">1134-1135年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='18bf36ce72c94320acaf195a0032eda1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月3日</a>　八月三日，绍兴府到任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月3日</a>　在会稽，八月三日，有谢启。作品：《绍兴府到任谢两府启》<div id='poem_1229733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍兴府到任谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229733")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229733_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229733'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229733'>伏奉告命，特授宝文阁学士、知绍兴府事、充两浙东路安抚使、马步军都总管，已于今月三日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229733_comment'></div>视草北门，许辞近职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229733_comment'></div>承流东道，叨莅名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229733_comment'></div>更延阁以宠行，即使朝而临遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229733_comment'></div>全进退雍容之礼，免仓皇迫逐之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229733_comment'></div>去国有名，省躬无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229733_comment'></div>伏念某憨而多忤，拙以寡徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229733_comment'></div>早直禁林，久掌丝纶之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229733_comment'></div>坐妨要地，曾无研练之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229733_comment'></div>过被上恩，曲怜孤进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229733_comment'></div>既与经帷之侍，复参使观之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229733_comment'></div>惟兼居于高华，致丛生于谤咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229733_comment'></div>中其要害，谓本由文字而受知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229733_comment'></div>托以嫌疑，乃颛指语言而为咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229733_comment'></div>纵皇明之赐察，岂臣迹之敢安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229733_comment'></div>宜丐閒身，庶全晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229733_comment'></div>青冥倦鹤，固绝意于骞飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229733_comment'></div>皂枥疲驽，未忘情于株朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229733_comment'></div>姑徇妻孥之计，愿分民社之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229733_comment'></div>仰叩天慈，果从人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229733_comment'></div>既窃剖符之寄，仍联鸣玉之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229733_comment'></div>矧此越邦，中分浙水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229733_comment'></div>甫违禁闼，即涉治封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229733_comment'></div>行无信次之淹，居有登临之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229733_comment'></div>虽米盐期会，未容坐啸之閒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229733_comment'></div>而弹射排根，稍缓必争之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229733_comment'></div>恩私甚厚，侪偶是希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229733_comment'></div>退省所蒙，谁知其自？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229733_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官品量多士，汇进群才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229733_comment'></div>蝇俯燕依，曾未戚疏之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229733_comment'></div>雕搏鹢退，各因势分之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229733_comment'></div>俯怜衰命之姿，特假便安之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229733_comment'></div>凡兹优幸，尽出保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229733_comment'></div>东道已遥，空忆召贤之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229733_comment'></div>修门自远，未知奉最之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229733_comment'></div>感幸兼怀，名言曷既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1229733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在绍兴，冬，刘豫诱金人拥兵南侵，窥伺江浙，叔厚缮甲治兵，犒王师，扼海道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月9日</a>　在会稽，闰二月九日，转承议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月</a>　在会稽，闰二月，有谢表。作品：《谢转官并加恩表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　在会稽，仲春，有文。作品：《题金坡遗事后》<div id='poem_1229765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题金坡遗事后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229765")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229765'>乙卯仲春，孙太冲自西蜀见寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229765_comment'></div>时去翰苑，守礼会稽已半岁云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229765_comment'></div>綦某叔厚志。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1229765_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　在会稽，春，因臂疾，再乞宫观。作品：《再乞宫观奏状》<div id='poem_1229671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞宫观奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229671")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229671'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229671'>臣近曾具奏，以抱疾寖久，恐妨职事，乞除一在外宫观差遣，伏奉诏书不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229671_comment'></div>臣仰体睿训，不敢继有渎闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229671_comment'></div>今者勉治所职，又历五旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229671_comment'></div>而臣比因久雨，冒阴湿之气，臂疾屡作，艰于书字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229671_comment'></div>又以体尝伏暑，遇热增甚，心思昏愦，动多健忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229671_comment'></div>若尚冒居剧郡，深恐自取颠沛，上孤陛下天地父母始终保全之大德，夙夜愧惧，不敢遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229671_comment'></div>臣契勘本府近日催科应办等事，如和买本钱、借拨军粮及和籴米，皆已数足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229671_comment'></div>收趣箭镞翎毛，按月无违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229671_comment'></div>分造十三车战船熟材，亦已起发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229671_comment'></div>其馀逐一次第推行，别无规避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229671_comment'></div>直缘衰残，力不任事，须至再有陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229671_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣悃愊，特降睿旨，检会前奏，除臣一在外宫观差遣，任便居住，庶就休閒，以便医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229671_comment'></div>冒犯天威，不胜俟命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229671_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1229671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　在会稽，春，有谢表。作品：《谢乞宫观不允诏表》<div id='poem_1229614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢乞宫观不允诏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229614")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229614'>准奏院递到诏书一道，以臣陈乞在外宫观差遣不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229614_comment'></div>需章有请，冒陈恳悃之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229614_comment'></div>纶旨弗俞，优假宠绥之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229614_comment'></div>感深以泣，荣甚而惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229614_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣昨补外官，适当会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229614_comment'></div>提封八县，丛米盐期会之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229614_comment'></div>领牧七州，兼城郭封疆之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229614_comment'></div>属有边书之警，大为海道之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229614_comment'></div>缮甲治兵，力盖忘其不足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229614_comment'></div>矫情镇物，众则谓之无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229614_comment'></div>虽黾勉以疚心，率拘挛而束手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229614_comment'></div>伟矣亲征之策，大哉播告之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229614_comment'></div>师当有功，人以无恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229614_comment'></div>洎奉解严之令，遂宽失职之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229614_comment'></div>而臣悸魄未宁，沉疴愈惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229614_comment'></div>勤奚补于拙政，老益凋于壮心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229614_comment'></div>辄叩帝阍，愿收郡印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229614_comment'></div>丐宫祠之闲禄，以养馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229614_comment'></div>酬君父之至恩，或容异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229614_comment'></div>宜即大河之域，忽颁一札之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229614_comment'></div>褒劝弥加，犹迟久成之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229614_comment'></div>拊循备至，方惩数易之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229614_comment'></div>体睿训之甚明，岂愚诚之敢执？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229614_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁于接物，恕以临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229614_comment'></div>驾驭群材，曲轸轩墀之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229614_comment'></div>规恢大业，均图郡邑之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229614_comment'></div>捧温诏之如春，觉懦衷之增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229614_comment'></div>然臣迂疏有素，固陋不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229614_comment'></div>当官而行，惧难胜于怨咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229614_comment'></div>奉身而退，况真迫于衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229614_comment'></div>勉希尘露之劳，终冀乾坤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229614_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1229614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　在会稽，六月，荐举凌景夏任秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　在会稽，七月，落职奉祠，提举江州太平观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　在会稽，七月，有谢表。作品：《谢宫祠表》<div id='poem_1229614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢乞宫观不允诏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229614")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229614'>准奏院递到诏书一道，以臣陈乞在外宫观差遣不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229614_comment'></div>需章有请，冒陈恳悃之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229614_comment'></div>纶旨弗俞，优假宠绥之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229614_comment'></div>感深以泣，荣甚而惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229614_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣昨补外官，适当会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229614_comment'></div>提封八县，丛米盐期会之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229614_comment'></div>领牧七州，兼城郭封疆之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229614_comment'></div>属有边书之警，大为海道之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229614_comment'></div>缮甲治兵，力盖忘其不足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229614_comment'></div>矫情镇物，众则谓之无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229614_comment'></div>虽黾勉以疚心，率拘挛而束手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229614_comment'></div>伟矣亲征之策，大哉播告之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229614_comment'></div>师当有功，人以无恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229614_comment'></div>洎奉解严之令，遂宽失职之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229614_comment'></div>而臣悸魄未宁，沉疴愈惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229614_comment'></div>勤奚补于拙政，老益凋于壮心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229614_comment'></div>辄叩帝阍，愿收郡印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229614_comment'></div>丐宫祠之闲禄，以养馀年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229614_comment'></div>酬君父之至恩，或容异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229614_comment'></div>宜即大河之域，忽颁一札之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229614_comment'></div>褒劝弥加，犹迟久成之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229614_comment'></div>拊循备至，方惩数易之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229614_comment'></div>体睿训之甚明，岂愚诚之敢执？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229614_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁于接物，恕以临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229614_comment'></div>驾驭群材，曲轸轩墀之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229614_comment'></div>规恢大业，均图郡邑之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229614_comment'></div>捧温诏之如春，觉懦衷之增气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229614_comment'></div>然臣迂疏有素，固陋不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229614_comment'></div>当官而行，惧难胜于怨咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229614_comment'></div>奉身而退，况真迫于衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229614_comment'></div>勉希尘露之劳，终冀乾坤之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229614_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1229614_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年3月29日</a>　三月二十九日，随高宗次定海县。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6360c516bd254982aa69f314882a2a09_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，48岁</div><div id='6360c516bd254982aa69f314882a2a09' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月2日</a>　四月二日，草王仲薿制词。作品：《降授通议大夫充显谟阁待制知袁州王仲薿可先次落职放罢制》<div id='poem_1229353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>降授通议大夫充显谟阁待制知袁州王仲薿可先次落职放罢制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229353")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229353'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229353'>敕：昔天宝之乱，河北诸郡悉陷，独常山、平原能为国守，则以杲卿、真卿二颜在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229353_comment'></div>功虽不遂，而堂堂忠烈之姿相望一时，可谓不辱其门，而无负于国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229353_comment'></div>以尔具官某出自相阀，宜知义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229353_comment'></div>久尘侍从之班，未闻报效，尚缘家世，每与使令，为郡江西，与其弟并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229353_comment'></div>属秋师之南寇，顾城守之弗图，力诚不支，死犹有说，乃敢显亏臣节，颓其家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229353_comment'></div>临川既降，宜春继屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229353_comment'></div>鲁卫之政，若循一途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229353_comment'></div>偷生之计则然，教忠之训安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229353_comment'></div>汝虽不惭于颜氏兄弟，亦何施面目见汝先人于地下乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229353_comment'></div>其解郡章，并收从橐，往需后命，以省前非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229353_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229353_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月3日</a>　四月三日，随高宗至明州城外。<br /></div>
-----end
