-----title
临海
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='740139a486b244979cf8e7ea0bd55363_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("740139a486b244979cf8e7ea0bd55363");'><span id='740139a486b244979cf8e7ea0bd55363_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，48岁</div><div id='740139a486b244979cf8e7ea0bd55363' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月2日</a>　一月二日，随高宗泊台州港口。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月3日</a>　一月三日，随高宗次章安镇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月4日</a>　在章安镇，一月四日，与赵鼎、李正民、富直柔等同对于舟中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月10日</a>　在章安镇，一月十日，草郭仲荀制词。作品：《殿前都指挥使昭化军节度使郭仲荀可责授汝州团练副使广州安置制郭仲荀责授汝州团练副使》<div id='poem_1229350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殿前都指挥使昭化军节度使郭仲荀可责授汝州团练副使广州安置制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年1月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229350")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229350'>敕：自干戈外侮，寇攘日深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229350_comment'></div>皆缘将帅之臣，莫适任患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229350_comment'></div>虽有国家之法，曾不加诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229350_comment'></div>至因循成姑息之风，肆偃蹇蓄自安之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229350_comment'></div>欲严师律，宜正邦刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229350_comment'></div>具官某蚤践戎行，尝更边寄，久典周庐之卫，遂分斋钺之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229350_comment'></div>谓其被宠以知恩，庶克临危而效死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229350_comment'></div>属江津之失守，当浙部之戒严，考彼师言，汝为宿将，俾副宣威之任，冀收御敌之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229350_comment'></div>贼已侵杭，兵宜备越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229350_comment'></div>怀私顾望，智岂迷于利昏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229350_comment'></div>闻敌仓黄，胆真惭于身大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229350_comment'></div>规作奔逃之计，漫陈分戍之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229350_comment'></div>未闻朝命而遽行，多取军须而妄费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229350_comment'></div>既移师而远遁，乃委众以先驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229350_comment'></div>居民惊扰于闾阎，部曲散离于山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229350_comment'></div>逮还经于行在，辄潜过于轻舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229350_comment'></div>隳军而长寇雠，既负畔官之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229350_comment'></div>委质而为臣子，敢乖事上之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229350_comment'></div>览近臣之抗言，用中司而即讯，靡知引咎，犹欲饰非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229350_comment'></div>此而弗惩，孰不可忍！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229350_comment'></div>尚念勤劳之旧，时宽典宪之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229350_comment'></div>黜以散员，投之远服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229350_comment'></div>往体涵容之德，毋忘惕励之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229350_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1229350_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9ff54b5417a74563b0e844ef0f2cf850_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ff54b5417a74563b0e844ef0f2cf850");'><span id='9ff54b5417a74563b0e844ef0f2cf850_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，48岁</div><div id='9ff54b5417a74563b0e844ef0f2cf850' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年3月20日</a>　三月二十日，随高宗次章安镇。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='460823a369e543cbb5f5bbc684eda23a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("460823a369e543cbb5f5bbc684eda23a");'><span id='460823a369e543cbb5f5bbc684eda23a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1142')">1135-1142年</a>，53-60岁</div><div id='460823a369e543cbb5f5bbc684eda23a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　七月，退居临海。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月17日</a>　在临海闲居，九月十七日，有祭文。作品：《祭范丞相文》<div id='poem_1229796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭范丞相文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229796")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229796'>维绍兴六年岁次丙辰，九月丙寅朔，十七日壬午，检校少傅、庆远军节度使、提举江州太平观郭仲荀，检校少傅、泸州军节度使、充中太一宫使钱忱，宝文阁学士、左承议郎、提举江州太平观綦某，右中大夫、充徽猷阁待制、提举江州太平观卢知源，随州观察使、前提举江州太平观张思正等，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于丞相观文殿学士高平范公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229796_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229796_comment'></div>天生异人，意其甚艰，待用于世，决非偶然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229796_comment'></div>既钟杰材，而俾相国，盍假之年，以究多绩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229796_comment'></div>寒乡下里，乃克生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229796_comment'></div>器度不凡，自其儿童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229796_comment'></div>妙龄射策，名震四海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229796_comment'></div>壮岁登庸，仪形一代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229796_comment'></div>亦既用矣，若有以为，天乎难谌，而止于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229796_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229796_comment'></div>靖康之元，公任谏诤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229796_comment'></div>犯颜无讳，冀回上听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229796_comment'></div>今皇识之，曰此爱君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229796_comment'></div>求于艰难，延秉国钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229796_comment'></div>面命词臣，玉色怡豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229796_comment'></div>汝善制草，予得贤辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229796_comment'></div>公怀感激，自尽不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229796_comment'></div>佥谋是用，旧典是稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229796_comment'></div>运物无心，无偏无党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229796_comment'></div>合其异同，一此刑赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229796_comment'></div>遇才则进，见可则行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229796_comment'></div>百工任职，万事得平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229796_comment'></div>敌侵淮濆，谓我避敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229796_comment'></div>公伐其谋，不战自北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229796_comment'></div>寇犯江浙，豺狼纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229796_comment'></div>指授大将，妖氛载清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229796_comment'></div>祸乱稍夷，人心小定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229796_comment'></div>镇安中外，邦基克正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229796_comment'></div>逮公去位，以迄于今，皇纲不坠，前功可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229796_comment'></div>盛年壮烈，一跌未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229796_comment'></div>庶几公归，胡夺之速！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229796_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229796_comment'></div>天台赤城，公所留居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229796_comment'></div>寄情丘壑，争席樵渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229796_comment'></div>间守永嘉，及期去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229796_comment'></div>如还故乡，对客欢适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229796_comment'></div>岂期小疾，奄至膏肓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229796_comment'></div>中台遽折，一鉴遂亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229796_comment'></div>龙华兰若，山水奇秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229796_comment'></div>公所甚爱，蓝舆时扣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229796_comment'></div>公性超悟，临终不迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229796_comment'></div>谁谓窀穸，乃此其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229796_comment'></div>挹公雅量，怀公厚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229796_comment'></div>迩惊远疑，孰不嗟戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229796_comment'></div>矧百姻族，庇荫其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229796_comment'></div>伤感途巷，执绋累累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229796_comment'></div>凡我文武，夙被钧播。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229796_comment'></div>列奠过车，涕泗交堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229796_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1229796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月</a>　在临海闲居，九月，有挽诗。作品：《故丞相高平范公挽歌辭三首》<div id='poem_535502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/535502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故丞相高平范公挽歌辞三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_535502")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535502'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535502'>遇主方英妙，当朝独老成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535502'>小车何耄耋，前席起公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535502'>感会真千载，哀荣止半生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535502'>伤心埋玉处，愁雾锁佳城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535502'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535502_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_535503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/535503?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535503'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535503'>帷幄言犹在，山林迹已迁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535503'>登庸疑早贵，福艾欠长年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535503'>浑厚风神粹，恢宏德度全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535503'>直应天夺速，何物恨鸢肩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535503_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535503'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535503_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_535504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/535504?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535504'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535504'>忆昔金銮直，天颜喜色新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535504'>草麻惭大手，命相得良臣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535504'>内赐充怀袖，廷扬耸搢绅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535504'>秪今馀典册，那复见斯人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535504'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　在临海闲居，三月，代吕颐浩撰谢表。作品：《代吕颐浩谢赐御书<兰亭>表》<div id='poem_1229620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代吕颐浩谢赐御书《兰亭》表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229620")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229620'>臣某近赴行在奏事，朝辞出门，行至建康府东门十里，伏蒙圣慈赐臣御书《兰亭》一轴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229620_comment'></div>绛阙清都，甫违帝所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229620_comment'></div>云章奎画，忽到人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229620_comment'></div>被宠锡之非常，觉衰残之有耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229620_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以隶文变古，书法争新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229620_comment'></div>魏氏已还，东晋擅摇毫之妙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229620_comment'></div>钟繇而降，右军驰独步之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229620_comment'></div>矧兰亭修禊之游，非金谷望尘之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229620_comment'></div>骋怀寄傲，存逸想于胸中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229620_comment'></div>感事临文，发奇资于笔下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229620_comment'></div>斯极当年之美，遂成历世之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229620_comment'></div>珍藏既出于云门，传刻仅留于朔塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229620_comment'></div>疲精莫近，绝轨谁攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229620_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下好学性成，多能天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229620_comment'></div>稍属干戈之暇，不遗翰墨之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229620_comment'></div>心慕手追，何劳取法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229620_comment'></div>龙盘凤翥，直与抗行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229620_comment'></div>实为今古之无双，岂止帝王之第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229620_comment'></div>臣少勤笔砚，晚际风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229620_comment'></div>忧常在于邦家，老已捐于文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229620_comment'></div>误膺上赐，还愧夙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229620_comment'></div>怀宝言归，未免登床之诮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229620_comment'></div>据鞍自失，但惊照乘之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229620_comment'></div>期传秘于私门，庶输忠于永世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1229620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年12月</a>　在临海闲居，十二月，江州太平观秩满，乞再任，有奏状。作品：《乞再任宫观奏状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年4月3日</a>　在临海闲居，四月三日，转朝奉郎，进封开国伯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年4月26日</a>　在临海闲居，四月二十六日，有谢表。作品：《谢转官并加恩表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　在临海闲居，是年，次女嫁于营丘仇车。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年4月</a>　在临海闲居，四月，吕颐浩卒，叔厚有挽诗。作品：《故丞相吕成公挽歌詩辭》<div id='poem_535505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/535505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故丞相吕成公挽歌诗辞五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_535505")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535505'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535505'>翊戴兴炎祚，权宜仿晋都。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535505'>关中萧相国，江左管夷吾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535505'>感会逢英主，拘挛鄙腐儒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535505'>人间留不得，去与列星俱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535505_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535505'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535505_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_535506' id='poem_sentence_3_535506'>还师期克敌，遗恨失斯时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535506'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535507'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535507'>仗钺除君侧，披荆立本朝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535507'>伤心桃李径，霜霰日萧条。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/535508?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535508'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535508'>名与功高大，身为世重轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535508'>初传都督令，已慑敌人情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535508'>门谢三千客，胸包十万兵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535508'>圣王分陜意，叹息失长城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535508'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535508_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_535509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_535509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/535509?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_535509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_535509'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_535509'>龊龊诚何算，堂堂亦已休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_535509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_535509'>嗟闻闭东阁，忍复过西州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_535509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_535509'>会送宜千乘，归藏但一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_535509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_535509'>往来埋玉恨，清泪涨溪流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_535509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_535509'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_535509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月</a>　在临海闲居，六月，再提举江州太平观秩满，乞三任，有奏状。作品：《乞再任宫观奏状二道》<div id='poem_1229673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞再任宫观奏状<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229673")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229673'>臣昨知绍兴府、充两浙东路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229673_comment'></div>缘臣多病自陈，蒙恩差提举江州太平观，任便居住，合至今年十二月满三十个月罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229673_comment'></div>伏念臣顷繇遭际，过窃高华，名在禁严，任更方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229673_comment'></div>虽不能而当止，顾大德之未酬，坐视时艰，敢图自逸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229673_comment'></div>但犬马寖衰之齿，疾疹屡侵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229673_comment'></div>况妻孥不给之资，姻嫁仍迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229673_comment'></div>既无壮事，犹利閒官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229673_comment'></div>辄忍愧于心颜，重投诚于君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229673_comment'></div>尚抚旧物，曲轸至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229673_comment'></div>傥迟暮之秋复堪于烦使，则糜捐之节终效于初期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229673_comment'></div>臣欲候今任满日再乞宫观一次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229673_comment'></div>干冒宸旒，臣无任跼蹐俟命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月22日</a>　在临海闲居，次女归宁，闰六月二十二日，暴疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月25日</a>　在临海闲居，闰六月二十五日，次女卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月28日</a>　在临海闲居，闰六月二十八日，殡次女于台州城东普济院之西。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年6月28日</a>　在临海闲居，闰六月二十八日，有埋铭记。作品：《亡第二女埋铭记》<div id='poem_1229795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亡第二女埋铭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年6月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229795")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229795'>北海綦氏，宝文阁学士某之次女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229795_comment'></div>生十有八年，嫁于营丘仇车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229795_comment'></div>又二年，来宁父母，因暴疾，三日而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229795_comment'></div>后三日，权殡于台州城东普济院之西，实绍兴十年闰六月二十八日也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1229795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年12月</a>　在临海闲居，十二月，撰潘特竦墓志铭。作品：《故左朝请郎守尚书右司员外郎致仕潘公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1229792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故左朝请郎守尚书右司员外郎致仕潘公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229792")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229792_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229792'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229792'>潘氏世为处州青田右姓，其先本武林人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229792_comment'></div>青田有沐溪乡，旧传东晋时尝有鹤沐于其溪，因以得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229792_comment'></div>山林幽邃，形势深阻，而中多美田，殆为异境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229792_comment'></div>公之六世祖避五季乱至此，爱之，遂家焉，子孙寖以蕃庶，居是乡者今数十百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229792_comment'></div>曾祖讳惟德，祖讳惟，素儒业，咸以长者称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229792_comment'></div>考赠朝奉郎讳麃，学优不仕，而笃于行义，乡人爱慕之，有争讼者不之官府，而来取决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229792_comment'></div>尝举八行，不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229792_comment'></div>宣和中，妖贼方腊之党陷处州，境内多被其害，独以谋帅里社之人卫其乡，贼不能犯，远近赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229792_comment'></div>公其长子也，讳特竦，字廷立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229792_comment'></div>性颖悟嗜学，幼所习诵，终身不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229792_comment'></div>年十九，学成，游太学，与英俊并处，凡十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229792_comment'></div>校试升选，每居前列，名称籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229792_comment'></div>大观四年，遂以上舍及第，释褐调长洲主簿，选为吉州州学教授，改高邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229792_comment'></div>秩满，除太学正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229792_comment'></div>丁妣安人叶氏忧，服除，授辟廱正，未赴而辟廱罢，为邓州司仪曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229792_comment'></div>公以经术入官，而吏能精明，若所夙习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229792_comment'></div>郡太守初见公，与语，奇之，试以疑事委公处决，无不得宜，乃叹曰：「君通才，当为朝廷用，而淹留州县，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229792_comment'></div>因荐于时宰，复除太学正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229792_comment'></div>考满，改宣教郎，俄迁博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229792_comment'></div>公久历学官，滞于进，而守职惟谨，不改常度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229792_comment'></div>贵游子来肄业，罕循理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229792_comment'></div>有两生犯规禁，自以挟势，必见优容，公判其罚如规，而一生当斥去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229792_comment'></div>同寮失色，司业亦以为言，公执不夺，识者多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229792_comment'></div>丁外艰去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229792_comment'></div>既终，哭谓其二弟曰：「吾于时寡合，向屈志仕宦，本以为亲荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229792_comment'></div>今抱永慕之戚，此兴衰矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229792_comment'></div>乃于旧庐之侧植嘉橘，筑堂，日游息其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229792_comment'></div>取楚辞《橘颂》之语名堂，曰「与友为文」，以见其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229792_comment'></div>居久之，不为赴调计，亲族共相敦勉，乃出造朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229792_comment'></div>时行在扬州士大夫稍集，公甫至，会更定宫观官令，欣然请于有司，不俟报，谒告径归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229792_comment'></div>政府间有招之者，不往见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229792_comment'></div>已而，资格未应，不得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229792_comment'></div>閒居再踰岁，值车驾幸永嘉，将旋跸会稽，而临海居间为要郡，朝廷择才贰郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229792_comment'></div>政府有荐公者，遂除通判台州，且趣之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229792_comment'></div>公至，谓太守曰：「今朝廷艰虞，仰给州县，宜留意财赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229792_comment'></div>丰财之术，非它求也，课其入而勒其出，则用度自充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229792_comment'></div>若循蹈旧习，任情慢令，徒慕宽厚之名，缓急何以塞责」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229792_comment'></div>太守悟曰：「君言是矣，自今请悉听君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229792_comment'></div>于是公得究心经理，凡利应入公上者，不复有耗蠹隐滞之弊，郡中财计为之羡溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229792_comment'></div>迨六师回驭，若行朝所供亿，转输相继，未尝告乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229792_comment'></div>明年，讨建寇范汝为，宣抚使以兵十万出其境，费给悉具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229792_comment'></div>时方多事，州郡趣办不时，往往以军期取具编户，吏缘为奸，民受其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229792_comment'></div>独临海一郡，终公之去，无毫发横敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229792_comment'></div>以奉行籴事不扰，先期而足，被赏，朝廷益知公才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229792_comment'></div>及受代，召赴都堂审察，未至，擢尚书金部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229792_comment'></div>自兵兴以来，当官为政者率务姑息、称人情，而公在临海，专以奉公惜费、杜请托、抑侥倖为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229792_comment'></div>人或不乐，乃因疑似，以事谤公，达于言路，到省才月馀，遂坐谏官章疏罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229792_comment'></div>以请，连主管建州之冲佑、台之崇道观，优游里闬凡六年，以自适其素愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229792_comment'></div>读书赋诗，以自娱乐，亲旧相过，辄置酒尽欢，退黜虽久，未尝见其几微于辞气间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229792_comment'></div>绍兴七年秋，起为广南东路转运判官，命复中寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229792_comment'></div>明年，再除江南西路，未赴，擢为度支员外郎，进大理少卿、右司员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229792_comment'></div>不半岁三迁，而人犹恨其晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1229792_comment'></div>于是朝廷方用公而未止也，公亦感激自尽，思效其才，至忘饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1229792_comment'></div>会大暑，暴中暍，居三日，疾革，以请得致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1229792_comment'></div>卒年五十有八，时九年秋七月辛巳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1229792_comment'></div>累阶至左朝请郎，佩服六品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1229792_comment'></div>公事亲孝，与二弟相友睦，待人诚信，必践言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1229792_comment'></div>才智有馀，而临事不苟，历仕中外，所至称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1229792_comment'></div>居乡好义，有先君子风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1229792_comment'></div>遇姻族有无告者，赒其贫乏，恤其孤寡，孜孜不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1229792_comment'></div>建炎初，建卒叶侬作乱，掠龙泉之松源乡，而沐溪接壤，乡人震恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1229792_comment'></div>公方服丧在家，喟然曰：「吾先君尝保此乡，小子其敢忘之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1229792_comment'></div>乃设方略，率乡人之壮健，栅于险要，坚壁以御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1229792_comment'></div>贼至，不得入，遁去，州郡赖之以无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1229792_comment'></div>上其事于朝，特加赏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1229792_comment'></div>后数岁，松溪贼危李窃发，其锋直抵沐溪境上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1229792_comment'></div>公如前拒守，闾井获全，乡人德公不忘，及其没也，少长皆为之流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1229792_comment'></div>呜呼，使天假公年，获尽其用，则所施设岂止一乡之惠而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1229792_comment'></div>公耽玩书史，始终不厌，为文温丽，自成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1229792_comment'></div>有集三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1229792_comment'></div>学既该览，尝作类书，补前人所遗者，又采近世文士词语以附益之，成五十卷，曰《课儿集》，传其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1229792_comment'></div>娶同郡叶氏，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1229792_comment'></div>子男二人，长曰曾，将仕郎，次曰肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1229792_comment'></div>孙男一人、女二人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1229792_comment'></div>曾卜以十年冬十有二月丁酉，葬公于其乡油田之原，盖公平日所属目之地，追遗志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1229792_comment'></div>先期，得其舅西安宰叶君绶状公行事，已，见属曰：「先人晚乃遇合，用矣，不幸奄忽，赍志而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1229792_comment'></div>今葬，当有铭以诏后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1229792_comment'></div>私念生平先友可托兹事莫如公宜，是以来请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1229792_comment'></div>余感其言，顾不得辞，遂以寄哀于此文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1229792_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1229792'>沐溪之水，窈而清兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1229792_comment'></div>群山合沓，环如城兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1229792_comment'></div>仙人沐鹤，曾此经兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1229792_comment'></div>韬奇韫秀，閟厥灵兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1229792_comment'></div>钟美于人，公其英兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1229792_comment'></div>受才孔多，学蚤成兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1229792_comment'></div>贤关典教，士服膺兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1229792_comment'></div>通守一邦，其政平兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1229792_comment'></div>首公不挠，孰谤憎兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1229792_comment'></div>含香入侍，迹靡停兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1229792_comment'></div>襆被去曹，中甚轻兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1229792_comment'></div>归与橘友，同芳馨兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1229792_comment'></div>偾而复起，道将行兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1229792_comment'></div>卿联宰属，官亟升兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1229792_comment'></div>嗟天与时，不遐龄兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1229792_comment'></div>三日卧家，疾莫兴兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1229792_comment'></div>还丧里社，皆失声兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1229792_comment'></div>公乎保我，今谁凭兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1229792_comment'></div>怀德不忘，传令名兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1229792_comment'></div>视其后人，宜有庆兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1229792_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年5月23日</a>　在临海闲居，五月二十三日，转朝散郎，进封高密郡开国侯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年6月9日</a>　在临海闲居，六月九日，有谢表。作品：《谢转官并加恩表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年1月1日</a>　在临海闲居，一月一日，有祭文。作品：《祭知台州胡端明文》<div id='poem_1229797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭知台州胡端明文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229797")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229797'>维绍兴十有二年岁次壬戌，正月朔日，宝文阁学士、左朝散郎、提举江州太平观綦某，徽猷阁直学士，左朝请大夫、提举江州太平观李擢，随州观察使、提举江州太平观张思正等，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故知府、尚书、端明己懋兄之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229797_comment'></div>惟公抱负纯诚，蹈履吉德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229797_comment'></div>宽裕有容，柔惠且直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229797_comment'></div>太傅中庸，征东清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229797_comment'></div>禀乎天资，匪由外饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229797_comment'></div>晋陵门阀，实冠南国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229797_comment'></div>名卿巨儒，相望赫奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229797_comment'></div>公又继之，为世矜式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229797_comment'></div>荐取词科，飞腾俊域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229797_comment'></div>乃登侍从，周旋帝侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229797_comment'></div>代言西台，给事左掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229797_comment'></div>三入禁林，再位常伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229797_comment'></div>羽仪朝廷，光华典册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229797_comment'></div>露门劝讲，从容启迪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229797_comment'></div>陈善纳忠，岂专䌷绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229797_comment'></div>崔琳仲舒，事该今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229797_comment'></div>怀素无量，时推博硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229797_comment'></div>济时戡难，繄公之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229797_comment'></div>帝亦知之，靡施不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229797_comment'></div>顾瞻钧衡，将有显陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229797_comment'></div>公厌承明，恳求閒适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229797_comment'></div>屈临海邦，于焉偃息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229797_comment'></div>版舆就养，公志则怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229797_comment'></div>静治期年，民安盗息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229797_comment'></div>外淹一州，人望未斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1229797_comment'></div>谓当遄归，奋庸熙绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1229797_comment'></div>暴疾乘之，朝不及夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1229797_comment'></div>老成云亡，有识所惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1229797_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1229797_comment'></div>某等顷接清班，联行并植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1229797_comment'></div>道同志合，淡然莫逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1229797_comment'></div>间阔几时，再见颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1229797_comment'></div>车骑临存，迎门倒舄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1229797_comment'></div>抵掌笑谈，洞见肝膈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1229797_comment'></div>更唱迭和，盈于翰墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1229797_comment'></div>俯仰之间，遂成陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1229797_comment'></div>思正迟暮退居，视公匪敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1229797_comment'></div>猥承泛爱，欢如旧识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1229797_comment'></div>杯酒流行，屡陪燕席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1229797_comment'></div>謦欬如在，音容遽隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1229797_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1229797_comment'></div>昔公之来，朱幡画戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1229797_comment'></div>稚耋欢呼，光动阡陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1229797_comment'></div>今公之归，丹旐素羃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1229797_comment'></div>徒御凄凉，奄就窀穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1229797_comment'></div>祸福无常，变故叵测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1229797_comment'></div>谓仁者寿，天理何啬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1229797_comment'></div>公薄世荣，晚耽禅寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1229797_comment'></div>死生之理，固已自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1229797_comment'></div>我辈怀贤，宁免伤恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1229797_comment'></div>寓辞奠觞，寄哀何极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1229797_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1229797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年1月</a>　在临海闲居，一月，追荐胡交修，有文。作品：《追荐文》<div id='poem_1229798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>追荐文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229798")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229798'>伏以禁门入侍，尝膺持橐以同朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229798_comment'></div>祠馆便居，获际剖符而出守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229798_comment'></div>喜依仁之有托，每叙旧以交欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229798_comment'></div>岂期旦暮之间，遽叹幽明之隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229798_comment'></div>人之不淑，天果何知！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229798_comment'></div>曷纾写于悲情，苐庄严于梵福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229798_comment'></div>伏愿知府尚书，端明不昧，尘障皆空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229798_comment'></div>以平生悟佛之因，證今日超凡之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229798_comment'></div>高名贵位，绝馀累于他生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229798_comment'></div>正念真观，永归依于此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229798_comment'></div>谨疏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年3月</a>　在临海闲居，三月，陈敏为叔厚写真。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　在临海闲居，春，转左朝请郎致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年4月8日</a>　在临海闲居，四月八日，书杜庭圭父墓志铭。作品：《书杜瓘父墓志铭》<div id='poem_1229766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229766' class='poemTitle href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229766")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229766_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229766'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229766'>余寓临海，与杜君庭圭居相近，往还甚熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229766_comment'></div>一日，出其先德之铭，俾得与观，而亡友虞仲容跋语在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229766_comment'></div>反覆展读，余是以益信其父子之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229766_comment'></div>绍兴十二年四月八日北海綦某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1229766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月4日</a>　在临海，八月四日，卒。<br /></div>

-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a2a2da0b11646e7a431260333ce1d8e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a2a2da0b11646e7a431260333ce1d8e");'><span id='4a2a2da0b11646e7a431260333ce1d8e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月21日</a>　一月二十一日，随高宗泊温州港口。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月21日</a>　一月二十一日，在温州港口，草吴表臣制词。作品：《朝奉郎吴表臣可除监察御史制》<div id='poem_1229292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎吴表臣可除监察御史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年1月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229292'>敕具官某：文昌万微所会，而御史六察，分纠列曹，非学足以知今古，识足以明治体，不在兹选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229292_comment'></div>以尔智术疏通，更练世务，才猷之美，趣操之端，见推士论，达于朕听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229292_comment'></div>耳目之任，尔实宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229292_comment'></div>自兵兴以来，事多从权，取便一切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229292_comment'></div>典章堕紊，荡无纲纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229292_comment'></div>绳治振肃，要如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229292_comment'></div>庶几艰难之中，犹有朝廷之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229292_comment'></div>往践厥次，毋违朕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229292_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月25日</a>　一月二十五日，草滕康、刘珏制词。作品：《资政殿学士朝请大夫权知三省枢密院事滕康可落职提举亳州明道宫资政殿学士朝散大夫权同知三省枢密院事刘珏可落职提举江州太平观制》<div id='poem_1229348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>资政殿学士朝请大夫权知三省枢密院事滕康可落职提举亳州明道宫资政殿学士朝散大夫权同知三省枢密院事刘珏可落职提举江州太平观制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年1月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229348")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229348'>敕：朕以边尘未靖，江戍方严，式图近辅之臣，往总行台之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229348_comment'></div>即豫章之便郡，奉长乐之安居，分釐政事之常，期固邦家之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229348_comment'></div>苟辜委遇，曷逭谴诃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229348_comment'></div>具官某等各以时名，扬于禁路，偶承人乏，进视柄司，俾陪侍从之行，冀副艰难之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229348_comment'></div>既同责任，罔克寅恭，或狠愎而无远谋，或烦碎而失大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229348_comment'></div>两执所短，交诋其非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229348_comment'></div>弗思备御之图，旋致奔逃之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229348_comment'></div>敌兵既逼，军伍皆离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229348_comment'></div>慈闱宁免于惊惶，宫掖半遭于劫辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229348_comment'></div>衣冠顿仆，黎庶伤残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229348_comment'></div>谋实尔乖，咎将谁执？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229348_comment'></div>览彼台臣之奏，劳予旰食之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229348_comment'></div>其镌秘殿之华资，尚假真祠之优禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229348_comment'></div>往加循省，毋重悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229348_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229348_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cdeacdf8b21742749342855bbbb6992d_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月2日</a>　二月二日，随高宗驻跸温州江心亭，草曾楙制词。作品：《朝议大夫试礼部尚书曾楙可除显谟阁学士知洪州制》<div id='poem_1229298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229298' id='poem_sentence_2_1229298_comment'></div>具官某，儒学有闻，行谊无玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229298_comment'></div>更践三朝之久，越跻八座之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229298_comment'></div>尝历藩宣，每著声绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229298_comment'></div>眷济阴之郡政，朕所深知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229298_comment'></div>郡邑新残，务致安民之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229298_comment'></div>政成事定，不汝久劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229298_comment'></div>维吾迩臣，当体兹意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229298_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229355")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229355'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229355'>敕具官某：尔顷尝条上防秋之策，若可施行，论者固以尔为疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229355_comment'></div>朕不欲以人废言，故置群议，而付之以其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229355_comment'></div>乃自去冬以来，寂无奏报，而寇得济江而南者，则尔所部也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229355_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229355_comment'></div>使经画几察，有以先之，如尔之言，能至是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229355_comment'></div>用人之失，果败吾事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229355_comment'></div>其镌禁职，乃罢厥官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229355_comment'></div>往省尔愆，以俟后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229355_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月2日</a>　二月二日，随高宗驻跸温州江心亭，草卢知原制词。作品：《奉直大夫充集英殿修撰知洪州王子献可先次落职放罢制》<div id='poem_1229354' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229354' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229354?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉直大夫充集英殿修撰知洪州王子猷可先次落职放罢制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229354")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229354_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229354'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229354'>敕具官某：朝廷置守以典一州，命帅以临一路，固欲任民社之托，遏寇攘之侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229354_comment'></div>傥乖所期，奚逭明宪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229354_comment'></div>尔顷由宿望，分牧江西，庶资御敌之方，可冀折冲之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229354_comment'></div>而有城弗守，闻寇遽奔，捐井邑于豺狼，陷生灵于涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229354_comment'></div>力虽不足，责欲谁归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229354_comment'></div>乃引咎于抗章，方原情而议罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229354_comment'></div>其上帅藩之符节，仍镌禁殿之班资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229354_comment'></div>往讼前愆，以需后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229354_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1229354_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月2日</a>　二月二日，随高宗驻跸温州江心亭，草王子献制词。作品：《中奉大夫直龙图阁知温州卢知原治状有闻可特除右文殿修撰制》<div id='poem_1229323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中奉大夫直龙图阁知温州卢知原治状有闻可特除右文殿脩撰制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229323")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229323'>敕具官某：昔汉宣中兴，以为太守吏民之本，数变易则下不安，故二千石有治理效，辄以玺书勉厉，增秩赐爵，用表章之，人以竞劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229323_comment'></div>汉世良吏，于斯为盛，朕甚慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229323_comment'></div>以尔剸剧有馀，临民不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229323_comment'></div>永嘉假守，阅时即多，蔼然治声，达于予听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229323_comment'></div>俾升华于书殿，式增重于守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229323_comment'></div>朕方久郡将之权，以图厥绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229323_comment'></div>尔其先国家之急，勿恤乃私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229323_comment'></div>益观政事之修，庸副吏民之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229323_comment'></div>罔俾前美，独尊昔人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229323_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月17日</a>　二月十七日，随高宗驻跸永嘉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月17日</a>　二月十七日，在永嘉，草王衣制词。作品：《中散大夫行大理少卿王衣可除大理正卿制》<div id='poem_1229326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中散大夫行大理少卿王衣可除大理正卿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229326")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229326'>敕具官某：廷尉天下之平，职当守正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229326_comment'></div>大理人命所系，戒在深文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229326_comment'></div>苟非其人，可与兹选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229326_comment'></div>以尔处心忠恕，用法详明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229326_comment'></div>久更践于刑官，屡决平于疑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229326_comment'></div>体钦恤哀矜之意，得重轻宽急之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229326_comment'></div>进列正卿，是为因任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229326_comment'></div>昔释之居职，时无冤民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229326_comment'></div>日知理囚，议无死法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229326_comment'></div>予欲胜残而止杀，尔其据正以持平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229326_comment'></div>往率乃僚，期继前轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229326_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1229326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月21日</a>　在永嘉，二月二十一日，上《举仇悆充监司奏状》<div id='poem_1229675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举仇悆充监司奏状<span class='inlineComment2'>（建炎四年二月二十一日中书舍人上）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229675")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229675'>准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，行在从官各举可充监司者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229675_comment'></div>右，臣伏睹起复朝散郎、新差知建昌军仇悆，性资忠厚，趣操端方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229675_comment'></div>进士登科，富于学术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229675_comment'></div>历任县道，皆有治迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229675_comment'></div>律身无过，疾恶如雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229675_comment'></div>其为政以举法循理为务，抑豪右，伸寒弱，不挠于彊御，不诎于势利，所至而人思爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229675_comment'></div>使其当一道之寄，必能激浊扬清，除民疾苦，如言者之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229675_comment'></div>今保堪充监司任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229675_comment'></div>如蒙朝廷擢用后，有不如所举，臣甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229675_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1229675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月22日</a>　在永嘉，二月二十二日，草邵薄制词。作品：《朝奉郎提举亳州明道宫邵薄可责授汝州团练副使峡州安置制》<div id='poem_1229351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎提举亳州明道宫邵薄可责授汝州团练副使峡州安置制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229351")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229351'>敕具官某：仲尼上圣也，君命召则不俟而行：圬者贱工也，而其为言曰「食焉不怠其事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229351_comment'></div>夫圣与庸亦远矣，然义之所在，不相为谋而有合焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229351_comment'></div>尔儒服衣冠，世有名节，久习朝廷之事，尝为侍从之臣，稔行治之有闻，宜险夷之不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229351_comment'></div>而乃避匿君命，务从便安，耗蠹公钱，坐縻供馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229351_comment'></div>忘圣人之大训，为贱工之所羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229351_comment'></div>岂尔之贤，而安处此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229351_comment'></div>至于干挠府政，妄腾事端，则又非所望于尔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229351_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229351_comment'></div>靖康、建炎之际，尔则未免于累矣，乃惮从朕于艰难，是诚何心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229351_comment'></div>度尔之私，其以亲故，览近臣之劾状，益有恻于朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229351_comment'></div>姑易散员，迁之远郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229351_comment'></div>体兹宽宪，毋重悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229351_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1229351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月23日</a>　在永嘉，二月二十三日，草王似制词。作品：《徽猷阁直学士通议大夫知庆阳府王似可差知成都府制》<div id='poem_1229312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽猷阁直学士通议大夫知庆阳府王似可差知成都府制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229312")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229312'>敕：自顷中州云扰，外寇日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229312_comment'></div>眷惟井络之区，独保剑门之险，肆求良牧，以惠远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229312_comment'></div>具官某赡智通方，周才济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229312_comment'></div>垂绅鸣玉，久联侍从之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229312_comment'></div>分阃析符，屡典藩宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229312_comment'></div>顷更方面，实莅庆阳，羌戎绥服其风声，吏士畏安其教令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229312_comment'></div>念威边乘塞，虽资方叔之壮猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229312_comment'></div>而化俗使民，更藉文翁之善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229312_comment'></div>其易梦刀之任，勿辞叱驭之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229312_comment'></div>勉尔令图，宽予忧顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229312_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月</a>　在温州，二月，草傅崧卿制词。作品：《朝奉郎中书门下省检正诸房公事傅崧卿可除直龙图阁知越州制》<div id='poem_1229343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎中书门下省检正诸房公事傅崧卿可除直龙图阁知越州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229343")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229343'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229343'>敕具官某：乃者长江失守，敌骑南侵，爰及会稽，并陷烽火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229343_comment'></div>念戎车之退，徒委空城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229343_comment'></div>而兵火之馀，尚多失业，肆求良牧，往抚疲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229343_comment'></div>以尔富有艺文，通知世务，辍自机衡之地，往从金革之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229343_comment'></div>捍牧圉以临戎，既心存于王室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229343_comment'></div>即乡邦而为政，庶身习于民情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229343_comment'></div>其升延阁之华，以侈绣衣之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229343_comment'></div>烟尘甫熄，益脩御敌之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229343_comment'></div>郡邑新残，务致安民之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229343_comment'></div>勉赴功名之会，永为闾里之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229343_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1229343_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
漳州（龙溪）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='63d5b811431844e7b807c7cb7b9a45ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("63d5b811431844e7b807c7cb7b9a45ee");'><span id='63d5b811431844e7b807c7cb7b9a45ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1132')">1130-1132年</a>，48-50岁</div><div id='63d5b811431844e7b807c7cb7b9a45ee' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年12月</a>　十二月，到漳州任，有谢启。作品：《漳州到任谢两府启》《漳州到任谢本路监司启》<div id='poem_1229706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漳州到任谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229706")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229706'>通籍禁门，莫效腹心之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229706_comment'></div>部符支郡，乃缘管内之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229706_comment'></div>既得请以之官，遂怀惭而莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229706_comment'></div>伏念某顷从羁旅，仅脱险艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229706_comment'></div>幸逢圣运之中兴，骤玷从班之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229706_comment'></div>恩深报重，未伸狗马之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229706_comment'></div>福过灾生，遽有弟兄之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229706_comment'></div>闵雄狐之狼狈，困岭峤之流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229706_comment'></div>九族畴依，一身是责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229706_comment'></div>抗章北阙，辄蒙从欲之慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229706_comment'></div>授印南州，曲徇便私之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229706_comment'></div>念兹漳浦，僻在海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229706_comment'></div>百粤之人好争，民今少讼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229706_comment'></div>七闽之俗逐末，境独多田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229706_comment'></div>使无横歛之虞，即有安生之佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229706_comment'></div>优游卒岁，或宽更代之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229706_comment'></div>饱暖全家，端恨外迁之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229706_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官均调元化，斟酌众宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229706_comment'></div>播物无私，自轸纳沟之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229706_comment'></div>回天有力，俾谐为郡之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229706_comment'></div>某敢不绥抚军民，理平庶狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229706_comment'></div>顾欲一门之生养，必思四境之安宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229706_comment'></div>报政山城，傥许奉三年之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229706_comment'></div>程能全郡，冀终收一日之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229706_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1229706_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1229707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漳州到任谢本路监司启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229707")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229707'>比者中辞省户，出绾郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229707_comment'></div>即驰驿以之官，已涓辰而莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229707_comment'></div>眷兹漳浦，僻在海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229707_comment'></div>百越之人好争，民今少讼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229707_comment'></div>七闽之俗逐末，境独多田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229707_comment'></div>苟无横歛之忧，真有安生之佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229707_comment'></div>抚存骨肉，既宽狱讼之虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229707_comment'></div>宣布诏条，更获优閒之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229707_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官推诚无间，为政有先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229707_comment'></div>肆谐补外之行，克遂便私之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229707_comment'></div>本于惠养，敢忘仲郢之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229707_comment'></div>拙在催科，难奏阳城之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229707_comment'></div>愿仰依于大庇，庶少憩于孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229707_comment'></div>感幸兼怀，敷宣曷既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229707_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1229707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年12月</a>　十二月，到漳州任，有启。作品：《赴漳州与帅守监司到启》<div id='poem_1229708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴漳州与帅守监司到启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229708")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229708'>比者得请便私，蒙恩补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229708_comment'></div>优假守符之寄，来依使节之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229708_comment'></div>既临遣于行朝，即奔驰而就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229708_comment'></div>出鲸池之骇浪，已次部封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229708_comment'></div>挹麈柄之清谈，将承矩范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229708_comment'></div>其为欣幸，难罄敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229708_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1229708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月28日</a>　在龙溪，适改元还故秩，一月二十八日，复授通直郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月</a>　在龙溪，一月，有谢表。作品：《谢复官表》<div id='poem_1229608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢复官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229608")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229608'>涣命诞敷，肇锡纪年之庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229608_comment'></div>解恩旁浃，普沾宥罪之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229608_comment'></div>尽涤往愆，复还故秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229608_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣顷承人乏，误被圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229608_comment'></div>尘从橐之清班，委铨曹之剧务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229608_comment'></div>奉有司之法，常自戒于阔疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229608_comment'></div>牵同列之求，卒轻贻于悔吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229608_comment'></div>词既连于白简，名遂挂于丹书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229608_comment'></div>降黜犹新，方深循省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229608_comment'></div>矜怜未整，遽俾蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229608_comment'></div>祗服训言，但增感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229608_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下绍隆宝祚，兴起丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229608_comment'></div>推尧舜之好生，与民更始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229608_comment'></div>复文武之旧业，其命维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229608_comment'></div>特宽一眚之辜，以尽群材之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229608_comment'></div>虽如愚赣，亦在涵容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229608_comment'></div>臣敢不金石持心，冰霜励操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229608_comment'></div>体皇家之忠厚，去民政之烦苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229608_comment'></div>瘴海身遥，更蒙私于雨露；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229608_comment'></div>阊阖籍在，尚接武于鸳鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229608_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1229608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月</a>　在龙溪，九月，上言漳州不可再有科敛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月</a>　在龙溪，九月，有贺启。作品：《贺吕忠穆公着左相启》<div id='poem_1229702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1229702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1229702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吕忠穆公著左相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30943, "宋", "綦崇礼", "poem_title_1229702")'>綦崇礼</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1229702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1229702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1229702'>播告大廷，还登上宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1229702_comment'></div>峻班仪于左棘，首揆路于中台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1229702_comment'></div>四夷耸闻，九鼎增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1229702_comment'></div>伏惟某官贤推名世，道富经邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1229702_comment'></div>岳降神而生申，实维周翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1229702_comment'></div>帝赉弼而得说，用作商霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1229702_comment'></div>变故屡更，精忠弥著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1229702_comment'></div>扫除内难，高五龙夹日之勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1229702_comment'></div>攘却外虞，成一马渡江之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1229702_comment'></div>方辅宁于法驾，将经济于神州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1229702_comment'></div>贝锦遽兴，扁舟径去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1229702_comment'></div>属分江而谋帅，乃仗钺以临戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1229702_comment'></div>羽扇纶巾，已坐清于妖祲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1229702_comment'></div>命圭相印，盖叠赏于元功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1229702_comment'></div>矧独兼文武之资，宜并注安危之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1229702_comment'></div>逮闻虚位，果趣赐环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1229702_comment'></div>非衣之谤何伤，有衮之思咸属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1229702_comment'></div>顾乃心王室，喜魁柄之重归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1229702_comment'></div>而戮力中原，伫皇家之再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1229702_comment'></div>天时有待，物望攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1229702_comment'></div>某迹滞一涯，神驰数仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1229702_comment'></div>聆制麻而相庆，曾无瘴海之殊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1229702_comment'></div>引宾履以交趋，独叹翘材之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1229702_comment'></div>其如瞻颂，可尽名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1229702_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1229702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年10月28日</a>　在龙溪，十月十八日，转奉议郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月13日</a>　在龙溪，十一月十三日，有谢表。作品：《谢转官并加恩表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在龙溪，是年，举荐陈汝楫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　在龙溪，一月，请建州权罢鼓铸二年，以监兵避乱散逸。<br /></div>
